### [1] [SWE-Router: Routing in Multi-turn Agentic Software Engineering Tasks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00053v1)
*Seongho Son,Sangwoong Yoon,Jiahua Tang,Shuhan Wang,Lorenz Wolf,Ilija Bogunovic*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一种基于局部轨迹的时序路由方法SWE-Router，在保持强模型性能的同时大幅提升成本效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM路由器仅基于任务描述，无法区分简单与复杂问题，导致浪费；需要一种能利用探索信息的路由方法。

Method: 提出SWE-Router，先让廉价模型运行几轮探索，基于局部轨迹决定是否升级到昂贵模型，并提供贝叶斯最优性理论保证。

Result: 在多种弱-强模型对中，SWE-Router大幅提高成本效率，同时保留强模型大部分性能。

Conclusion: 基于局部轨迹的路由优于纯描述路由，且释放了可复现的数据集。

中文摘要：嵌入在多轮代理框架中的大型语言模型(LLM)正在重塑软件工程(SWE)，但当许多问题可以通过廉价修复解决时，将所有任务路由到前沿模型是浪费的。现有的LLM路由器仅基于任务描述进行操作，这在代理设置中继承了一个信息论的贝叶斯误差下限：类似的问题可能隐藏着局部拼写错误或多模块重构，而提示无法区分两者。我们引入了SWE-Router，一种基于价值的时序方法，允许廉价模型运行几个探索轮次，并读取生成的局部轨迹，然后再决定是继续廉价执行还是升级到昂贵模型。我们提供了一个贝叶斯最优性定理，表明基于局部轨迹的条件判断永远不会损害路由，并且每当探索提供信息时，它都会严格更好。在跨越当前成本-能力前沿的弱模型和强模型的LLM对中，我们展示了SWE-Router大大提高了SWE任务的成本效率，同时保留了强模型的大部分性能。我们还发布了一个多LLM轨迹数据集，允许复现我们的轨迹级路由。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) embedded in multi-turn agentic harnesses are reshaping software engineering (SWE), but routing every task to a frontier model is wasteful when many issues admit cheap fixes. Existing LLM routers operate on the task description alone, which inherits an information-theoretic Bayes-error floor in agentic settings: a similar issue can hide either a localized typo or a multi-module refactor, and the prompt does not separate the two. We introduce SWE-Router, a value-based temporal approach that lets a cheap model run for a few exploratory turns and reads the resulting partial trajectory before deciding whether to continue cheaply or to escalate to an expensive model. We provide a Bayes-optimality theorem showing that conditioning on the partial trajectory never harms routing and is strictly better whenever exploration is informative. Across the LLM pairs of weak and strong models spanning the contemporary cost--capability frontier, we show that SWE-Router greatly improves the cost efficiency of SWE tasks, while maintaining the majority of the performances of the stronger model. We additionally release a multi-LLM trajectory dataset which allows reproduction of our trajectory-level routing.

</details>


### [2] [A Quantitative Framework for Estimating System Complexity and Cost via Component Interface Analysis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00054v2)
*Ken Y. Chan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出一个形式化建模框架，通过有向耦合图和多视图表示估计外部需求引发的系统变更复杂性和成本，并以零售银行平台案例验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要估计外部需求引起的系统变更的复杂性和成本，并弥合基于组件的建模与成本估算之间的差距。

Method: 将系统建模为有向耦合图，通过组件接口估计有界变更复杂性，将外部驱动因素与成本因素关联，并采用多视图表示（图形、代数、表格）。

Result: 实现了通过组件接口估计有界变更复杂性，并关联成本因素，案例验证表明方法有效。

Conclusion: 该方法弥合了基于组件的建模与项目成本估算之间的差距，为架构设计、软件工程和生命周期运营提供了可操作的见解。

中文摘要：本文介绍了一个形式化建模框架，旨在估计由外部需求引起的系统变更的复杂性和成本。我们将系统建模为耦合的有向图，捕捉特定上下文中组件与元素之间复杂的依赖关系和信息流。所提出的方法能够通过组件接口估计有界变更复杂性，即使内部逻辑不透明。此外，该框架通过将外部驱动因素和成本因素与单个系统元素关联，为限制系统范围修改的成本提供了一种机制。我们提出了模型的多视图方法，提供图形、代数和表格表示，以适应不同抽象层次和计算需求。通过弥合基于组件的建模与项目成本估算之间的差距，我们的方法为架构设计、软件工程和生命周期运营提供了可操作的见解。该模型通过一个涉及示例零售银行平台集成的案例研究进行了验证。

Original abstract: This paper introduces a formal modeling framework designed to estimate the complexity and cost associated with system changes induced by external requirements. We model a system as a directed graph of couplings, capturing the intricate dependencies and information flows between components and elements within a specific context. The proposed method enables the estimation of bounded change complexity through component interfaces, even when internal logic remains opaque. Additionally, the framework provides a mechanism for bounding the cost of system-wide modifications by associating external drivers and cost factors with individual system elements. We propose a multi-view approach to the model, providing graphical, algebraic, and tabular representations to suit different levels of abstraction and computational needs. By bridging the gap between component-based modeling and project cost estimation, our method provides actionable insights for architecture design, software engineering, and lifecycle operations. The model is validated through a case study involving the integration of a sample retail banking platform.

</details>


### [3] [Partially ordering software licenses](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31032v1)
*Hamidah Oderinwale,David Atkinson,Rachel Hong,Art Abal,Ben Laufer*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 利用LLMs大规模比较许可证，构建偏序关系和分类，揭示严格许可证的可解释属性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前许可证比较缺乏系统性，难以大规模分析许可证之间的许可性关系，这对开源平台的技术重用和合规性有重要影响。

Method: 使用大型语言模型，通过成对比较构建许可证的偏序排序，并基于现有分类法进行归类。

Result: 恢复了与更严格许可证相对应的可解释属性，并验证了方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 提出的方法能够系统化分析许可证关系，对开源生态系统的法律理解有帮助。

中文摘要：许可证是发明者可以用来保护他们构建的技术并规范其使用方式的法律工具——然而，其作者身份和选择的性质意味着它们的解释、选择和执行在很大程度上是非结构化的。在实践中，这使得大规模比较许可证变得困难——何时一个许可证被认为比另一个更宽松，以及何时它们的条款彼此不可比较？目前，有越来越多的许可证被引入和使用，但没有系统的方法来研究它们之间的关系。这对于像Hugging Face、GitHub和Python包索引这样的平台很重要，在这些平台上，开发者发布或基于各自拥有许可证的技术进行构建。利用大型语言模型（LLMs），我们引入了大规模比较许可证的方法：首先，以成对方式构建基于许可性的偏序关系；其次，利用现有的软件许可证分类法。前者使我们能够追踪限制性，后者使我们能够将许可证选择理解为共享条款的组合。我们的分析恢复了与更严格许可证相对应的某些可解释属性，这对开源生态系统具有法律意义。

Original abstract: Licenses are legal instruments that inventors may use to protect the technologies they build and regulate how they are used -- however, the nature of their authorship and selection means that how they are interpreted, chosen, and enforced is largely unstructured. In practice, this makes it difficult to compare licenses at scale -- when is one license considered more permissive than the other, and when are their terms incomparable to each other? Currently, there is a growing list of licenses that are introduced and used, but there is no systematic way to study their relationships. This matters for platforms such as Hugging Face, GitHub, and the Python Package Index, where developers publish or build upon technologies that each have their own licenses. Using large language models (LLMs), we introduce methods for comparing licenses at scale: first, in a pairwise fashion to construct a partial ordering based on permissiveness, and second, by drawing on existing taxonomies of software licenses. The former allows us to trace restrictiveness, and the latter allows us to understand license selection as a combination of shared provisions. Our analysis recovers certain interpretable attributes that correspond to stricter licenses, with legal implications for the open-source ecosystem.

</details>


### [4] [An Empirical Study of Security Calibration in Large Language Models for Code](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31159v1)
*Mohammed Latif Siddiq,Md. Nafiu Rahman,Joanna C. S. Santos*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 首次大规模研究LLM生成代码的安全校准，发现过度自信普遍，功能校准比安全校准更差，自动修复效果有限，架构门控在仓库级设置中校准恶化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究LLM在生成代码时是否知道代码的安全性，即校准能力，以评估其可靠性和信任风险。

Method: 在多个温度设置下评估GPT-4o-mini、Gemini-2.0-Flash和Qwen3-Coder-Next，使用独立安全任务和多语言仓库级两个基准，分析安全校准和功能校准，并测试校准引导的自动修复和减缓虚假信任的策略。

Result: 过度自信普遍；功能校准比安全校准更差；自动修复改进有限且引入功能回归；架构门控在受控基准改善校准但仓库级设置中恶化。

Conclusion: LLM在安全校准上存在不足，尤其在仓库级设置中风险更高，现有缓解策略效果有限，需要更好的校准方法。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）正在迅速改变软件开发，但它们在安全关键场景中的使用引发了一个关键问题：模型是否知道它们生成的代码不安全？这种属性称为校准，衡量模型的置信度与其输出的真实正确性是否一致。我们首次对LLM生成代码中的安全校准进行了大规模实证研究。我们在多个温度设置下评估了GPT-4o-mini、Gemini-2.0-Flash和Qwen3-Coder-Next，并在两个互补基准上进行了测试：独立安全任务和多语言仓库级上下文。我们的结果表明，过度自信在所评估的LLM中普遍存在。功能校准始终比安全校准更差，这表明模型对安全结果的估计比功能正确性更可靠，可能是因为功能正确性依赖于复杂的执行行为。我们还研究了校准引导的自动修复是否有助于修复LLM生成代码中的漏洞，发现改进有限且经常引入功能回归。此外，我们研究了减少虚假信任（模型对易受攻击代码赋予高置信度）的不同缓解策略。结果表明，尽管架构门控在受控基准上改善了校准，但校准在现实仓库级设置中恶化，增加了高置信度易受攻击输出的风险。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are rapidly transforming software development, yet their use in security-critical contexts raises a key question: do models know when their generated code is insecure? This property, known as calibration, measures whether a model's confidence aligns with the true correctness of its outputs. We present the first large-scale empirical study of security calibration in LLM-generated code. We evaluate GPT-4o-mini, Gemini-2.0-Flash, and Qwen3-Coder-Next across multiple temperature settings on two complementary benchmarks: self-contained security tasks and multi-language repository-level contexts. Our results suggest that overconfidence is prevalent across the evaluated LLMs. Functional calibration is consistently worse than security calibration, suggesting that models estimate security outcomes more reliably than functional correctness, potentially because functional correctness depends on complex execution behavior. We also examine whether calibration-guided automated repair can help remediate vulnerabilities in LLM-generated code, finding only limited improvements while frequently introducing functional regressions. Moreover, we study different mitigation strategies for reducing False Trust, where models assign high confidence to vulnerable code. The results show that although architectural gating improves calibration on controlled benchmarks, calibration deteriorates in realistic repository-level settings, increasing the risk of high-confidence vulnerable outputs.

</details>


### [5] [FeatX: Editing Software by Editing Features for Repository-Level Code Evolution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31206v1)
*Xutian Li,Yifeng Zhu,Xianlin Zhao,Yanzhen Zou,Lu Zhang,Bing Xie*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: FeatX是一个面向特征的工具，通过提取层次化特征结构并利用三阶段演化代理编辑特征，显著降低认知负荷并提高代码修改定位性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM用于软件演化的交互范式以代码为中心，需要手动管理上下文和迭代提示，导致认知负荷高和可用性差。

Method: FeatX首先从现有仓库中提取层次化的史诗-特征结构，并建立特征到代码的显式映射，然后通过一个三阶段的演化代理（包括理解、规划、生成）将特征编辑转换为代码补丁，并通过四个协调面板展示工作流程。

Result: 在受控用户研究和38个真实世界特征编辑提交上的重放实验中，FeatX相比vanilla ChatGPT显著降低了认知负荷并提高了可用性，并且在函数级修改定位F1上相比强LLM基线取得了42.6%的相对提升，总成本仅0.07美元。

Conclusion: FeatX通过特征导向的编辑方式，有效降低了认知负荷，提高了软件演化任务的效率和可用性，且成本低廉。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地用于软件演化，然而大多数交互范式仍然以代码为中心，需要手动管理上下文并迭代提示。我们提出FeatX，一个面向特征的工具，通过编辑特征来编辑软件。给定一个现有仓库，FeatX提取出一个层次化的史诗-特征结构，并带有显式的特征到代码映射，然后调用一个三阶段的演化代理将特征编辑转换为代码补丁。该工作流程通过四个协调的面板呈现。通过一项受控用户研究和在38个真实世界特征编辑提交上的重放实验，FeatX相比vanilla ChatGPT显著降低了认知负荷并提高了可用性。与强大的LLM基线相比，它在函数级修改定位F1上取得了42.6%的相对提升，且成本大幅降低（总计0.07美元）。该工具和收集的数据集可在https://github.com/a496263365/FeatX/tree/demo获取，演示视频在https://youtu.be/OZqKZ4Ii-yM。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used for software evolution, yet most interaction paradigms remain code-centric and require manual context management and prompt iteration. We present FeatX, a feature-oriented tool for editing software by editing features. Given an existing repository, FeatX extracts a hierarchical epic-feature structure with explicit feature-to-code mappings, then invokes a three-stage Evolution Agent to translate feature edits into code patches. The workflow is exposed through four coordinated panels. Across a controlled user study and replay experiments on 38 real-world feature-editing commits, FeatX significantly reduces cognitive load and improves usability compared with vanilla ChatGPT. It also achieves a 42.6\% relative improvement in function-level modification localization F1 over strong LLM baselines, at substantially lower cost (\$0.07 in total). The tool and collected dataset are available at https://github.com/a496263365/FeatX/tree/demo, with a demonstration video at https://youtu.be/OZqKZ4Ii-yM.

</details>


### [6] [A Multi-Dimensional, Per-Pass Empirical Study of the LLVM Optimization Pipeline](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31238v1)
*Federico Bruzzone,Walter Cazzola*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过对LLVM -O3流水线的大规模测量，揭示了其非单调性和后加载特性，发现少数pass主导性能提升，并指出IR指令数不可靠等关键发现，为编译器优化提供了指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量化单个优化pass的边际影响是阶段排序和pass选择的基础，但pass交互、噪声和流水线规模使这一任务困难，需要系统性的实证研究。

Method: 将LLVM -O3流水线分解为累积前缀，在30个PolyBench/C内核上测量执行时间、编译时间、二进制大小、硬件计数器和RAPL能量，共84,750次测量，并严格抑制噪声。

Result: 流水线非单调（6.6-9.7%过渡出现回归），中位数内核需要84.8%的流水线才能获得80%的加速；少数Pareto主导pass贡献大部分收益，最终-O3配置在29/30内核上Pareto被支配；IR指令数不可预测运行时，运行时pass实际节能30-60%，阶段干扰损失上限46.35%。

Conclusion: 这些发现有助于更合理的pass剪枝、成本模型校准和自动调优，提升编译优化效果。

中文摘要：量化单个优化pass的边际影响是阶段排序、pass选择、优化设计以及pass/硬件交互分析的基础。在LLVM（通过MLIR作为C/C++、Rust和ML栈的标准后端）中，优化pass之间的交互、测量噪声和流水线规模使得这一任务变得困难。我们提出了对LLVM -O3优化流水线的系统性实证研究。我们将流水线分解为累积的逐pass前缀。然后，我们在84,750次测量中测量了执行时间、编译时间、二进制大小、硬件计数器和RAPL能量，这些测量覆盖了在30个PolyBench/C内核上评估的-O3流水线的113个累积前缀，并严格进行了噪声抑制。在这些计算密集型的仿射内核上，流水线是非单调的（6.6-9.7%的转变出现回归），并且严重后加载（中位数非回归内核需要84.8%的流水线才能获得80%的加速）。大多数收益是由一个小的Pareto主导的pass核心驱动的，而最终的-O3配置在（大小，加速）上对于30个内核中的29个是Pareto被支配的。我们进一步表明，IR指令数不是运行时的可靠预测指标，运行时导向的pass实际上也是能量导向的（节省30-60%），并且由于阶段干扰导致的损失的无搜索理想可加性上限是46.35%。这些发现使得更明智的pass剪枝、成本模型校准和自动调优成为可能。

Original abstract: Quantifying the marginal impact of individual optimization passes underpins phase ordering, pass selection, optimization design, and analysis of pass/hardware interactions. In LLVM -- the standard backend for C/C++, Rust, and ML stacks via MLIR -- interactions among optimization passes, measurement noise, and pipeline scale make this difficult. We present a systematic, empirical study of the LLVM -O3 optimization pipeline. We decompose the pipeline into cumulative per-pass prefixes. We then measure execution time, compile time, binary size, hardware counters, and RAPL energy across 84,750 measurements covering 113 cumulative prefixes of the -O3 pipeline evaluated on 30 PolyBench/C kernels under rigorous noise mitigation. On these compute-bound affine kernels, the pipeline is non-monotone (6.6-9.7% of transitions regress) and strongly back-loaded (the median non-regressing kernel needs 84.8% of the pipeline for 80% of its speedup). Most gains are driven by a small Pareto-dominant core of passes, while the final -O3 configuration is Pareto-dominated on (size, speedup) for 29 of 30 kernels. We further show that IR instruction count is an unreliable predictor of runtime, that runtime-targeted passes are de facto energy-targeted (30-60% savings), and that the search-free idealized-additive upper bound on losses due to phase interference is 46.35%. These findings enable more informed pass pruning, cost-model calibration, and autotuning.

</details>


### [7] [Mutating the "Immutable": A Large-Scale Study of Git Tag Alterations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31354v1)
*Solal Rapaport,Laurent Pautet,Samuel Tardieu,Stefano Zacchiroli,Théo Zimmermann*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模实证研究揭示了Git标签变更的普遍性及其对构建可重现性的破坏，建议使用提交哈希锁定依赖并实施标签变更监控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Git标签被广泛视为不可变，但实际中可被修改，威胁构建可重现性和供应链完整性，而缺乏对这一现象的实证研究。

Method: 对Software Heritage的3.284亿个仓库进行大规模分析，检测标签变更，并与Nixpkgs进行交叉分析。

Result: 发现1020万次标签变更，影响18.9万个仓库；在Nixpkgs中32个包引用被变更的标签，其中7个出现构建错误。

Conclusion: 标签变更破坏可重现构建，建议使用提交哈希、暴露审计日志，并实施系统性监控。

中文摘要：Git标签通常被视为软件开发中不可变的引用，用于标记发布和特定仓库状态，这些状态是构建可重现性和软件供应链完整性的基础。尽管其预期的不可变性，Git允许通过删除或强制推送更新来修改标签。这种修改的普遍性威胁到了可重现构建和依赖完整性。我们首次对公共代码仓库中标签变更进行了大规模实证研究，分析了来自Software Heritage的3.284亿个软件仓库，发现了1020万次标签变更，影响了18.9万个独特的仓库。与Nixpkgs的交叉分析显示，有32个包引用了我们数据集中被变更的标签，其中7个表现出确认的构建错误，这提供了具体证据，证明标签变更破坏了可重现的包构建。我们的发现挑战了普遍认为标签是发布软件不可变锚点的假设。因此，我们建议构建系统和包管理器将依赖锁定到加密的提交哈希，开发平台暴露标签变更审计日志，并且社区采用系统性的标签变更监控作为标准的供应链安全实践。

Original abstract: Git tags are commonly viewed as immutable references in software development, marking releases and specific repository states that underpin build reproducibility and software supply-chain integrity. Despite their intended immutability, Git allows tags to be altered through deletion or modification via force-pushed updates. The prevalence of such alterations threatens reproducible builds and dependency integrity. We conduct the first large-scale empirical study of tag alterations in public code repositories, analyzing 328.4 M software repositories from Software Heritage and identifying 10.2 M tag alterations affecting 189 k unique repositories. A cross-analysis with Nixpkgs reveals that 32 packages reference tags altered in our dataset, with 7 exhibiting confirmed build errors, providing concrete evidence that tag alterations break reproducible package builds. Our findings challenge the widespread assumption that tags are immutable anchors for released software. We therefore recommend that build systems and package managers pin dependencies to cryptographic commit hashes, that development forges expose tagmutation audit logs, and that the community adopt systematic monitoring of tag alterations as a standard supply-chain security practice.

</details>


### [8] [A Self-Negotiation Framework for Ethical Decision-Making during Task Interruptions in Service Robots](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31357v1)
*Nele Reichert,Mashal Afzal Memon,Marco Autili,Nico Hochgeschwender*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一种自我协商框架，使服务机器人能在多用户中断场景中通过伦理偏好内部协商做出自主伦理决策。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有服务机器人在多用户冲突时依赖静态规则或集中仲裁，缺乏自主、基于伦理的冲突解决能力。

Method: 提出自我协商框架，每个用户由伦理档案表示，通过内部协商过程解决冲突，并在ROS中实现模块化。

Result: 系统输出与用户伦理偏好一致，支持多边协商，响应时间<1.5秒，运行时随用户输入近线性增长。

Conclusion: 该框架实现了自主伦理冲突解决，可用于现实服务机器人场景。

中文摘要：在公共环境中运行的服务机器人经常在多个用户同时请求服务时遇到中断。解决此类冲突需要伦理决策，因为优先处理一个用户的请求可能会使另一个用户处于不利地位。当前的方法依赖于静态规则或集中仲裁，不支持自主的、基于伦理的冲突解决。本文探讨了一个机器人如何在任务中断期间在多个用户之间进行仲裁，并在不依赖外部协调的情况下做出符合伦理的决策。我们引入了一个自我协商框架，通过一个伦理档案表示每个用户，该档案捕捉他们的上下文伦理偏好和条件，并通过内部协商过程解决冲突。该框架在基于ROS的模块化实现中实现，并在具有现实中断场景的仿真中进行了评估。结果表明，该系统始终产生与用户伦理偏好一致的结果，支持用户之间的多边协商，并在1.5秒内响应，随着用户输入的增加，运行时间接近线性增长。

Original abstract: Service robots operating in public environments frequently encounter interruptions when multiple users request service simultaneously. Resolving such conflicts requires ethical decision-making, as prioritizing one user request can disadvantage another. Current approaches rely on static rules or centralized arbitration and do not support autonomous, ethics-based conflict resolution. This paper addresses the question of how a single robot can arbitrate between multiple users during task interruptions and make ethically aligned decisions without relying on external coordination. We introduce a self-negotiation framework that represents each user by an ethical profile that captures their contextual ethical preferences and conditions, and resolves conflicts through an internal negotiation process. The framework is implemented in a modular ROS-based implementation and evaluated in simulation with a realistic interruption scenario. The results show that the system consistently produces user ethical preference-aligned outcomes, supports multilateral negotiation among users, and responds within 1.5 seconds, with near-linear runtime growth under increasing user input.

### [9] [MOA: A Profiling-Guided LLM Framework for Memory-Optimization Automation at Codebase Scale](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31368v1)
*Jiaxi Liang,Yuanxiang Shi,Zezhou Yang,Chenxiong Qian*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: MOA是一个LLM驱动的框架，自动检测和修复大规模代码库中的内存低效问题，在OpenHarmony上实现了显著的内存和二进制大小减少。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有内存优化工作流缺乏端到端自动化，依赖手动合成工具输出，难以扩展到大型代码库。

Method: MOA采用三个LLM驱动的代理：分析器挖掘反模式，检查器合成静态分析器，修补器生成优化补丁。

Result: 在OpenHarmony上识别13个反模式，检测超1万个低效，生成769个补丁（92.5%接受率），平均堆减少42.2%，二进制大小减少10.6%。

Conclusion: MOA作为生产规模性能工程工具具有重要价值，能自动处理内存低效问题。

中文摘要：现代大型软件系统常常遭受普遍的内存低效问题（例如膨胀、抖动），导致过度的资源成本和性能下降。现有的优化工作流缺乏端到端的自动化，迫使开发者手动将复杂工具的输出综合为可操作且保留语义的修复方案，这阻碍了在大型代码库中的可扩展性。为了解决这个问题，本文提出了MOA，一个LLM驱动的框架，能够自动检测和修复生产规模代码库中反复出现的内存低效问题。具体来说，MOA通过三个代理运行：分析器从性能剖析数据中挖掘反模式，检查器生成器通过模板引导的细化合成静态分析器，以及修补器通过状态机驱动的工作流生成优化补丁。我们在OpenHarmony（一个拥有超过1亿行C/C++代码的开源操作系统）上的评估显示，MOA从3个剖析的服务中识别出13个反模式（其中9个是之前未知的），在更广泛的7个服务中检测到超过10,000个低效问题，并生成了769个补丁，专家接受率为92.5%，平均实现了42.2%的堆内存减少和10.6%的二进制大小减少。我们认为MOA是生产规模性能工程的一个有价值工具。

Original abstract: Modern large-scale software systems often suffer from pervasive memory inefficiencies (e.g., bloat, churn), leading to excessive resource costs and performance degradation. Existing optimization workflows lack end-to-end automation, forcing developers to manually synthesize complex tool outputs into actionable and semantics-preserving fixes, precluding scalability in large codebases. To address this, this paper presents MOA, an LLM-driven framework that automatically detects and repairs recurring memory inefficiencies across production-scale codebases. Specifically, MOA operates through three agents: an Analyzer that mines anti-patterns from profiling data, a Checker Generator that synthesizes static analyzers through template-guided refinement, and a Patcher that generates optimization patches via state-machine-driven workflows. Our evaluation on OpenHarmony, an open-source operating system with over 100 million lines of C/C++ code, shows that MOA identifies 13 anti-patterns (9 previously unknown) from 3 profiled services, detects over 10,000 inefficiencies across a broader set of 7 services, and generates 769 patches with 92.5% expert acceptance rate, achieving 42.2% heap reduction and 10.6% binary size reduction on average. We envision MOA as a valuable tool for performance engineering at production scale.

### [10] [Failure-Based Testing for Deep Reinforcement Learning Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31372v1)
*Weibin Lin,Jiangtao Meng,Zheng Zheng*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一种基于故障洞察的优先级随机测试方法（PRT），利用任务难度线索优先测试高风险区域，在降低测试成本的同时提高故障发现能力和测试多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有DRL代理测试方法依赖奖励信号，但训练良好的代理奖励信号高，难以发现关键故障，需要更有效的故障检测方法。

Method: 提出Prior Random Testing（PRT），一种黑盒基于故障的测试方法，利用任务引发的故障洞察（任务难度）对输入域中易失败区域进行优先级排序，同时保持测试用例多样性。

Result: 在四个基准测试上，PRT在首次故障发现成本和测试多样性方面排名前列，相比随机测试，多样性更好且测试成本降低超过50%。

Conclusion: PRT通过任务难度优先级排序有效提升了故障检测效率，降低了测试成本，并保持了测试用例的多样性，是一种优于现有方法的DRL测试方案。

中文摘要：深度强化学习（DRL）代理已被广泛应用于各个领域，以解决具有挑战性的决策问题，例如自动驾驶和机器人控制。鉴于许多此类应用对安全性和关键性要求极高，因此对DRL代理进行严格测试必不可少。现有的测试方法通常以奖励信号为指导来检测故障。然而，对于训练良好的代理，其在标准操作条件下的性能接近最优水平，奖励信号通常保持较高，使得现有方法难以有效发现关键故障。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了一种新颖的基于故障的测试方法，该方法利用任务引发的故障洞察来增强故障检测能力，同时减少所需测试的数量。由于DRL代理本质上是根据人类定义的任务设计的，它们提供了关于任务难度的宝贵线索。直观上讲，DRL代理在面对更困难的任务时更可能失败；因此，PRT优先考虑这些任务。在此基础上，我们提出了Prior Random Testing，一种黑盒的基于故障的测试方法，该方法能够在保持生成测试用例多样性的同时实现有针对性的优先级排序。在任务引发的故障洞察指导下，PRT优先考虑输入域中容易发生故障的区域，从而促进高效的故障检测。PRT在四个广泛使用的基准测试上进行了评估，并与不同的最先进方法（包括模糊测试、基于搜索和基于生成的方法）进行了比较。在发现第一个故障的成本和测试用例的多样性方面，PRT均位列前茅。值得注意的是，与随机测试相比，PRT实现了更好的多样性，并将测试成本降低了50%以上。

Original abstract: Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) agents have been widely adopted across diverse domains to address challenging decision-making problems, such as autonomous driving and robotic control. Given that many of these applications are safety- and security-critical, rigorous testing of DRL agents is indispensable. Existing testing methods are typically guided by reward signals to detect failures. However, for well-trained agents, whose performance approaches optimal levels in standard operating conditions, reward signals remain generally high, making current methods ineffective at uncovering critical failures.
  To address these challenges, we propose a novel failure-based method that leverages task-induced failure insights to enhance failure detection capability while reducing the number of tests required. Since DRL agents are inherently designed with human-defined tasks, they provide valuable cues about task difficulty. Intuitively, a DRL agent is more likely to fail when confronted with a more difficult task; therefore, PRT prioritizes these tasks. Building on this foundation, we propose Prior Random Testing, a black-box failure-based testing method that enables targeted prioritization while preserving the diversity of generated test cases. Guided by task-induced failure insights, PRT prioritizes failure-prone regions of the input domain, thereby facilitating efficient failure detection.
  PRT is evaluated on four widely used benchmarks and compared with different state-of-the-art methods including fuzzing, search-based and generative-based methods. PRT ranks among the top performers in terms of both the cost of finding the first failure and the diversity of test cases. Notably, compared to random testing, PRT achieves better diversity and reduces the testing cost by over 50%.

### [11] [AlgoBench: Benchmarking Algorithmic Adaptation in Code Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00062v1)
*Xinyuan Song,Zekun Cai,Liang Zhao*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: ALGOBENCH通过约束位移变换自动生成新颖的算法问题，评估大语言模型在算法推理上的真实能力，发现模型在需要算法适应时性能显著下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有编程基准可能因数据污染而高估模型的算法能力，需要更严格评估算法适应性的方法。

Method: 提出ALGOBENCH框架，通过结构化约束位移变换从已知问题生成变体，并引入复杂度感知指标（如OPTT、OPTS、TRAPRATE、GAPT、CONSENS）以评估解决方案的功能正确性和渐近复杂度。

Result: 多个LLM在ALGOBENCH变体上性能大幅下降，检索辅助会复用旧算法，许多看似正确的解不满足复杂度要求，错误主因是算法层面。

Conclusion: ALGOBENCH能有效评估模型在算法层面的适应能力，而不仅仅是功能正确性，揭示了当前模型在算法推理上的局限性。

中文摘要：在诸如HumanEval和LiveCodeBench等既定编程基准上的高通过率并不总能表明模型是否能够推理算法。许多固定基准最终通过发布的问题陈述、社论和生成的解决方案成为公共训练生态系统的一部分，使得后来的模型部分通过暴露而非更强的算法能力而改进。我们引入了ALGOBENCH，这是一个通过结构化约束位移变换从已知的竞争编程问题自动构建新颖算法问题的框架。每个被接受的ALGOBENCH变体都可追溯到源问题，但必须使原始参考算法失效。除了pass@$k$，我们还引入了复杂度感知指标——包括OPTT、OPTS、TRAPRATE、GAPT和CONSENS——以测试解决方案不仅在功能上正确，而且在渐近上适合生成的问题。在多个LLM和提示策略上的实验表明，在ALGOBENCH变体上性能急剧下降，检索可以增加旧算法的复用，许多看似正确的解决方案未能满足所需的复杂度。错误分析表明失败主要是算法层面的而非实现层面，表明ALGOBENCH评估了超越功能正确性的适应能力。

Original abstract: High pass rates on established programming benchmarks such as HumanEval and LiveCodeBench do not always show whether a model can reason about algorithms. Many fixed benchmarks eventually become part of the public training ecosystem through released problem statements, editorials, and generated solutions, allowing later models to improve partly by exposure rather than by stronger algorithmic ability. We introduce ALGOBENCH, a framework that automatically builds novel algorithmic problems from known competitive-programming problems through structured constraint-shifting transformations. Each accepted ALGOBENCH variant is traceable to a source problem, but must make the original reference algorithm fail. Beyond pass@$k$, we introduce complexity-aware metrics -- including OPTT, OPTS, TRAPRATE, GAPT, and CONSENS -- to test whether a solution is not only functionally correct but also asymptotically suitable for the generated problem. Experiments across multiple LLMs and prompting strategies show that performance drops sharply on ALGOBENCH variants, retrieval can increase reuse of the old algorithm, and many correct-looking solutions fail to meet the required complexity. Error analysis shows that failures are mainly algorithmic rather than implementation-level, suggesting that ALGOBENCH evaluates adaptation beyond functional correctness.

### [12] [Maximizing Parallel Execution of Series-Parallel Task Graphs for Safety-Critical Embedded Control](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31481v1)
*Jinghao Sun,Zhenchu Hu,Ye Ma,Bo Tang,Qingxu Deng,Xiuzhen Cheng*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文研究串并联任务图的最大并行执行问题，提出一种基于拉格朗日的迭代启发式算法（LIH），实验表明该算法在大多数实例中达到最优解，且运行时间极短，并应用于PLC程序到FPGA的转换优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统处理器的顺序执行在具有可并行子任务的嵌入式控制程序中成为瓶颈，需要利用并行性以满足实时性要求。

Method: 将最大并行执行问题建模为加权团划分问题，提出基于拉格朗日的迭代启发式算法（LIH），通过构建候选批次池、拉格朗日定价和修复过程来高效求解。

Result: 实验表明，LIH在91.25%的实例中匹配精确最优解，平均差距0.073%，平均运行时间18.19ms；在最大设置下精确基线需要数百秒，而LIH低于50ms。

Conclusion: LIH能高效求解最大并行执行问题，接近最优解且速度极快，并通过PLC梯形逻辑案例验证了其在FPGA程序优化中的有效性。

中文摘要：安全关键嵌入式控制程序必须在一个有界时间内完成每个控制周期。当程序的依赖结构包含可以并发执行的子任务时，在传统处理器上的顺序执行可能成为瓶颈。本文研究了在分阶段批处理模型下的串并联任务图的最大并行执行（MPE）问题：一个批次内的兼容任务并行执行，而选定的批次按照保持前序关系的拓扑顺序顺序启动。我们将MPE公式化为一个加权团划分问题，最小化批次执行时间之和，每个批次的成本由其最慢的任务决定。为了有效解决这个问题，我们提出了一种基于拉格朗日的迭代启发式算法（LIH）。LIH从单例列和随机贪心团生成中构建一个经过定价过滤的可行候选批次受限池。然后应用拉格朗日定价来指导列选择，并使用修复过程恢复合法的团划分。与加权混合图着色分支定界基线和随机贪心基线的实验表明，LIH在91.25%的可比较实例中匹配精确最优解，平均差距为0.073%，平均运行时间为18.19毫秒。在最大的精确参考节点设置中，精确基线平均需要数百秒，而LIH保持在50毫秒以下。我们还提出了一个端到端的PLC梯形逻辑案例研究，其中PLCOpen风格的程序被转换为MPE图，由LIH优化，转换为面向FPGA的HDL，并与原始PLC扫描执行进行仿真比较。

Original abstract: Safety-critical embedded control programs must complete each control cycle within a bounded period. Sequential execution on conventional processors can become a bottleneck when the dependency structure of the program contains subtasks that could be executed concurrently. This paper studies the Maximum Parallel Execution (MPE) problem for series-parallel task graphs under a staged batching model: compatible tasks inside one batch execute in parallel, while the selected batches are launched sequentially in a topological order that preserves precedence. We formulate MPE as a weighted clique-partitioning problem that minimizes the sum of batch execution times, with each batch cost determined by its slowest task. To solve this problem efficiently, we propose a Lagrangian-based Iterative Heuristic (LIH). LIH constructs a pricing-filtered restricted pool of feasible candidate batches from singleton columns and random greedy clique generation. It then applies Lagrangian pricing to guide column selection and uses a repair procedure to recover a legal clique partition. Experiments against a weighted mixed-graph-coloring branch-and-bound baseline and a randomized greedy baseline show that LIH matches the exact optimum in 91.25% of comparable instances, with an average gap of 0.073% and an average runtime of 18.19 ms. In the largest exact-reference node setting, the exact baseline requires hundreds of seconds on average, whereas LIH remains below 50 ms. We further present an end-to-end PLC ladder-logic case study in which PLCOpen-style programs are converted to MPE graphs, optimized by LIH, translated into FPGA-oriented HDL, and simulated against the original PLC scan execution.

</details>


### [13] [Digital Innovation through Knowledge Processes](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31505v1)
*Nataliia Klievtsova,Juergen Mangler,Stefanie Rinderle-Ma*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过分析知识密集型过程中的模式，提出了一个6类别的过程模型分类法，并收集了常见知识过程模式，以促进数字转型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了对知识密集型过程进行更普遍的定义，需要探讨过程资源（如数据、对象、人工制品和人类）之间的关系。

Method: 分析知识管理过程中经常出现的模式，研究它们在过程模型中的表示以及所代表的知識类型，并基于真实世界知识收集过程推导模式。

Result: 将过程模型分为6个类别以体现知识强度，并收集了一系列常见的知识过程模式。

Conclusion: 对知识密集型过程的整体看法及其建模、执行、监控和评估将加速和提高数字转型项目的质量。

中文摘要：知识与过程管理交叉点上的产物是过程，它描述了企业如何创造价值。在知识管理文献中，知识与过程的关系经常被讨论，通常导致对知识密集型过程的定义，这些过程涉及高水平的人力参与。另一方面，过程管理社区侧重于将过程形式化为可执行、可监控和可改进的模型。在本文中，我们探讨了过程资源（如数据、对象、人工制品和人类）之间的关系，以便对知识密集型过程进行更普遍的定义。为此，我们分析了知识管理过程中经常出现的不同模式，它们如何在过程模型中表示，以及它们代表哪些类型的知识。结果包括将过程模型分为6个类别，可以轻松看出知识强度，以及一系列常见的知识过程模式。这些模式来自于一个真实世界的知识收集过程，该过程包含了本文中详细介绍的各种模式和概念。我们认为，对知识密集型过程的整体看法，以及如何建模、执行、监控和评估其影响，将加速和提高数字转型项目的质量。

Original abstract: The artefact at the intersection of knowledge and process management is the process, which describes how enterprises are generating value. In knowledge management literature the relation of knowledge and processes is discussed, often leading to the definition of knowledge intensive processes, which entail a high level of human involvement. The process management community on the other hand focuses on the formalization of processes as models that can be executed, monitored, and improved. In this paper we explore the relationship of process resources such as data, objects, artefacts and humans, in order to come to more universal definition of knowledge intensive processes. For this purpose, we analyze different patterns that frequently occur in knowledge management processes, how they are represented in process models, and which types of knowledge are represented by them. The results comprise a categorization of process models into 6 categories that allow to easily see the knowledge intensity as well as a collection of common knowledge process patterns. The patterns were derived from a real-world knowledge gathering process, which includes a wide array of patterns and concepts detailed in this paper. We think that a holistic view on knowledge intensive processes, how to model, execute, monitor, and asses their impact, will speed up and improve the quality of digital transformation projects.

</details>


### [14] [Falsification, Not Exposure: An Internally Preregistered Placebo-Controlled Decomposition of Self-Repair Feedback in Frozen Small Code Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31511v1)
*Mehmet Iscan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过安慰剂对照和盲重采样，证伪方法比传统重试更有效，反馈价值来自与外部可执行反例的比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有重试机制缺乏对反馈价值的严格评估，需要可证伪的方法来区分反馈内容的效果。

Method: 构建安慰剂对照工具，通过反馈包分解、盲重采样基线、形状匹配安慰剂、一致性对测试和可执行审计进行实验。

Result: 盲重采样比裸代码重试多18个解锁，代码加事实比裸代码多18个，比通用安慰剂多15个，仅指令效果不显著。

Conclusion: 证伪的价值在于与外部可执行反例的比较，而非词汇或自我批评。

中文摘要：在重新训练不可行的部署环境中，小型冻结代码模型通常被要求在看到自己的失败输出后修复失败的程序，这通常被视为一种重试机制。从波普尔的观点来看，生成的程序是一个猜想，而测试执行违反是一个与预言机相关的、可执行的反例，因此反馈的价值不应归因于重新暴露于失败代码，而应归因于猜想是否对外部的、可执行的批评开放。作为以证伪为中心的测量项目的第三阶段，本研究构建了一个安慰剂对照工具，将反馈包与匹配输出生成预算的盲重采样基线以及无内容、形状匹配的安慰剂进行分解。贡献不是一种新的修复算法，而是一种反身性方法论（包分解、安慰剂镜像、匹配预算的不一致对测试、新生成确认、可执行审计），使得模型的程序猜想和研究者的“反馈内容有效”声明都可证伪。在六个HumanEval+/MBPP+单元中，使用三个0.5B-1.5B冻结模型，评估了290个死亡任务单元（无最佳8个候选通过公共层级）；主要运行生成7,000个新生成，预先注册的后续运行再生成1,400个。盲重采样比裸代码重试多出+18个净解锁（25/7，Holm p=0.0021）。代码加事实比裸代码多恢复+18个（21/3，p=0.00042），比通用项目符号安慰剂多+15个（p=0.0041）。仅指令效果不可区分（+3，p=0.36）。代码加事实和盲重采样各以26个解锁持平（不等价）。六个外部控制器后续运行与无内容形状安慰剂持平。在这种机制下，证伪帮助的不是词汇或自我批评，而是与外部可执行反例的比较。

Original abstract: In deployment settings where retraining is infeasible, small frozen code models are routinely asked to repair a failed program after seeing their own failing output, usually treated as a retry mechanism. From a Popperian view, a generated program is a conjecture and a test-execution violation is an oracle-relative, executable counterexample, so feedback's value should be attributed not to re-exposure to failing code but to whether the conjecture is opened to external, executable criticism. As the third stage of a falsification-centered measurement program, this study builds a placebo-controlled instrument that decomposes the feedback packet against a blind-resampling baseline at matched output-generation budget and against content-free, shape-matched placebos. The contribution is not a new repair algorithm but a reflexive methodology (packet decomposition, placebo mirroring, matched-budget discordant-pair tests, fresh-generation confirmation, executable audits) that makes both the model's program conjecture and the researcher's "feedback content works" claim falsifiable. Across six HumanEval+/MBPP+ cells with three 0.5B-1.5B frozen models, 290 dead task-cell units (no best-of-8 candidate passing the public tier) were evaluated; the main run produced 7,000 fresh generations and a preregistered follow-up 1,400 more. Blind resampling exceeded bare-code retry by +18 net unlocks (25/7, Holm p=0.0021). Code-plus-facts recovered +18 over bare code (21/3, p=0.00042) and +15 over a generic-bullet placebo (p=0.0041). An instruction-only effect was not distinguishable (+3, p=0.36). Code-plus-facts and blind resampling tied at 26 unlocks each (not equivalence). Six external-controller follow-ups tied a content-free shape placebo. In this regime, falsification helped not as vocabulary or self-critique, but as comparison with external, executable counterexamples.

</details>


### [15] [FormIDEAble: Safe and Socially-aware Autonomous Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31572v1)
*Livia Lestingi,Amel Bennaceur,Marcello M. Bersani,Carlos Gavidia-Calderon,Anastasia Kordoni,Mark Levine,Bashar Nuseibeh,Matteo Rossi*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出FormIDEAble，一种形式化方法，用于在不确定性和安全约束下合成社交意识合作策略，通过建模为Priced Timed MDP和成本受限可达性问题，实验表明有效性并揭示优化与安全的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法要么没有形式化保证，要么忽略人类行为，需要一种兼具形式化保证和社交意识的方法。

Method: 将人机合作建模为Priced Timed Markov Decision Process，决策制定表述为成本受限的可达性问题。

Result: 在紧急疏散场景中实验证明有效，并展示了优化与安全保证之间的权衡。

Conclusion: FormIDEAble为社交关键系统中的形式化保证、社交意识决策提供了原则性基础。

中文摘要：在社交关键环境中运行的自主代理必须在不完全确定的情况下与人类协调，同时尊重明确的安全约束。现有方法要么考虑社交动态而没有形式化保证，要么提供形式化保证但抽象掉了人类行为。我们引入了FormIDEAble，一种形式化的、有根据的方法，用于综合具有安全保证的社交意识合作策略。人类与自主代理之间的合作被建模为带价格的时间马尔可夫决策过程，决策制定被表述为一个成本受限的可达性问题。我们使用紧急疏散场景来说明该方法。初步实验证据证明了该方法的有效性，并凸显了优化与安全保证之间的权衡。FormIDEAble为社交关键系统中的形式化保证、社交意识决策提供了原则性的基础。

Original abstract: Autonomous agents operating in socio-critical settings must coordinate with humans under uncertainty while respecting explicit safety constraints. Existing approaches either account for social dynamics without formal guarantees or provide formal assurance while abstracting away human behaviour. We introduce FormIDEAble, a formally grounded approach for synthesising socially-aware cooperation strategies with safety guarantees. The cooperation between humans and the autonomous agent is modelled as a Priced Timed Markov Decision Process, and decision-making is formulated as a cost-bounded reachability problem. We illustrate the approach using an emergency evacuation scenario. Initial experimental evidence demonstrates the effectiveness of the approach and highlights the trade-offs between optimisation and safety guarantees. FormIDEAble provides a principled foundation for formally assured, socially-aware decision-making in socio-critical systems.

### [16] [From Failure to Alignment: A Requirements Engineering Framework for Machine Learning Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31589v1)
*Amel Bennaceur,Gopi Krishnan Rajbahadur,Prince Mercy,Bashar Nuseibeh,Faeq Alrimawi*

TL;DR: 提出REAL框架，通过需求工程方法（数据、模型、系统需求编织，失败驱动的需求探索，迭代细化和可追溯性）来开发符合利益相关者需求的机器学习系统，并在自动驾驶示例中验证。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组织需要检查机器学习系统的可信度并与利益相关者沟通，但缺乏系统化的需求工程流程来同时考虑利益相关者需求和MLS开发约束。

Method: 提出REAL框架，基于三个原则：需求编织（数据、模型、系统）、失败驱动的需求探索、迭代和可追溯的细化。

中文摘要：组织在设计、开发和部署机器学习系统（MLS）时，需要能够检查这些系统是否值得信赖，并清晰地与利益相关者沟通，无论是不同类型的用户、工程师还是更广泛的社会。通过关注利益相关者，需求工程能够很好地引导设计和工程化与利益相关者需求相一致的MLS。然而，我们仍然需要一个系统化的流程来建模和推理MLS的需求，该流程既要由利益相关者的需求驱动，也要考虑MLS开发的约束。本文提出了一个名为REAL（面向学习与失败的机器学习的需求工程）的框架，通过采用需求工程方法，帮助开发与利益相关者需求相一致的MLS。该基于模型的框架基于三个原则：第一，将数据、模型和系统整体的需求编织在一起；第二，使用失败来驱动替代需求的探索；第三，MLS需求的迭代和可追溯的细化。我们使用自动驾驶的一个示例展示了所提出的框架，并表明REAL支持开发更符合利益相关者需求的MLS。在线提供了可复现的包。

Original abstract: Organisations designing, developing, and deploying machine learning systems (MLS) need to be able to check that these systems are trustworthy, and communicate this clearly to their stakeholders, be they different categories of users, engineers, or wider society. By focusing on stakeholders, Requirements Engineering is well positioned to drive the design and engineering of MLS that align with the needs of their stakeholders. Yet, we still need a systematic process for modelling and reasoning about requirements for MLS that is driven both by stakeholders' needs and constraints for MLS development.
  This paper proposes a framework entitled REAL (Requirements Engineering for mAchines that Learn - and Fail) to help develop MLS that align with stakeholders' needs by adopting a requirements engineering approach. This model-based framework is based on three principles. First, weaving together requirements for data, models, and the system as a whole. Second, using failure to drive the exploration of alternative requirements. Third, iterative and traceable refinement of MLS requirements.
  We demonstrate the proposed framework using an example from autonomous driving and show that REAL supports the development of MLS that better align with stakeholders' requirements. A replication package is available online.

### [18] [ScratchWorld: Evaluating If World Models Compute Executable Consequences](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31689v1)
*Yufeng Lin,Jialu Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: ScratchWorld是一个基于Scratch项目的离线诊断基准，通过值感知的改变字段F1评估世界模型，发现现有模型在因果跟踪和反事实预测上表现很差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的世界模型评估在稀疏变化世界中容易因状态重叠而产生虚假的高准确率，需要更严格的评测方法。

Method: 将Scratch项目作为可执行世界，使用固定Scratch VM生成验证的转换、隐藏变量和反事实，并用值感知的改变字段F1作为主要指标。

Result: 在659个示例中，七个模型在状态压力测试中最多达到13.8%的改变字段F1，而复制输入状态可达98%的全状态准确率但0%的改变字段F1，说明模型依赖状态重叠而非因果规则。

Conclusion: 当前模型在理解可执行规则和因果推理方面存在严重缺陷，需要新的基准和指标来推动世界模型的进步。

中文摘要：世界模型评估通常通过预测的未来与目标状态或观察的重叠程度来评分。在稀疏变化世界中，这会将复制的持久状态转化为表面上的准确性。我们引入了ScratchWorld，一个离线诊断基准，它将Scratch项目视为可执行世界，并使用固定版本的Scratch虚拟机生成重放验证的转换、隐藏变量、因果轨迹和反事实结果。ScratchWorld评估下一状态预测、长程跟踪、因果事件归因和反事实预测；每个重放验证的目标可以以原始程序、结构化状态、自然语言或渲染输入模态呈现，我们的实验使用结构化状态条件。其主要状态指标是值感知的改变字段F1，该指标仅对改变的字段及其执行值给予评分。在包含659个示例的发布中，七个提示语言/推理模型在仅有状态的局部观察压力测试中最多达到13.8%的值感知改变字段F1。同实例复制诊断使重叠混淆具体化：复制输入状态达到98.0%的隐含全状态字段准确率和0.0%的改变字段F1，在真实项目上膨胀最大。辅助诊断将隐藏状态滚转漂移、干预敏感性、因果归因和扰动鲁棒性分离开来。在这些设置中，模型通常对动作或干预做出反应，但没有遵循决定改变值的可执行规则。

Original abstract: World-model evaluations often score a predicted future by overlap with a target state or observation. In sparse-change worlds, this can turn copied persistent state into apparent accuracy. We introduce ScratchWorld, an offline diagnostic benchmark that treats Scratch projects as executable worlds and uses a pinned Scratch VM to produce replay-verified transitions, hidden variables, causal traces, and counterfactual outcomes. ScratchWorld evaluates next-state prediction, long-horizon tracking, causal event attribution, and counterfactual prediction; each replay-verified target can be presented under raw-program, structured-state, natural-language, or rendered input modalities, and our experiments use the structured-state condition. Its primary state metric is value-aware changed-field $F_1$, which gives credit only for the changed field and its executed value. In a 659-example release, seven prompted language/reasoning models reach at most 13.8% value-aware changed-field $F_1$ in a state-only partial-observation stress test. A same-instance copy diagnostic makes the overlap confound concrete: copying the input state reaches 98.0% implied full-state field accuracy and 0.0% changed-field $F_1$, with the largest inflation on real projects. Auxiliary diagnostics separate hidden-state rollout drift, intervention sensitivity, causal attribution, and perturbation robustness. Across these settings, models often react to actions or interventions without following the executable rule that determines the changed value.

### [19] [AdaTrans: Automated C to Rust Transformation via Error-Adaptive Repair](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31706v1)
*Xiaofan Liu,Zecan Li,Zhuang Zhao,Ziqi Shuai,Yanming Yang,Qi Xin,Jifeng Xuan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: AdaTrans通过策略驱动RAG、错误分层变换和多阶段验证，显著提升了C到Rust代码转换的编译通过率和解决率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM在将C代码自动转换为Rust时，常常违反Rust的所有权和借用语义或依赖不安全构造，需要更好的方法。

Method: 提出AdaTrans框架，包含策略驱动RAG、错误分层变换策略（ESTS）和多阶段验证流水线。

Result: 在104个算法问题数据集上，平均编译通过率95.51%，平均解决率81.09%，不安全文件率仅1.19%。

Conclusion: AdaTrans在C到Rust转换中显著优于现有工具，有效减少不安全代码。

中文摘要：将C代码自动转换为Rust代码具有挑战性，因为Rust具有严格的所有权和借用语义。虽然大语言模型（LLMs）显示出潜力，但它们经常生成违反这些规则或依赖不安全构造的代码。我们提出了AdaTrans，一个通过三种核心机制解决这些问题的框架：策略驱动的检索增强生成（RAG）机制，用于将编译器错误映射到特定修复；错误分层变换策略（ESTS），根据错误类型调整其行为；以及多阶段验证流水线，确保可编译性和功能等价性。在包含104个算法问题的数据集上评估，AdaTrans实现了平均编译通过率95.51%和平均解决率81.09%，显著优于现有工具，同时保持不安全文件率仅为1.19%。

Original abstract: The automated transformation of C code to Rust is challenging due to Rust's strict ownership and borrowing semantics. While Large Language Models (LLMs) show promise, they often produce code that violates these rules or relies on unsafe constructs. We propose AdaTrans, a framework that addresses these issues through three core mechanisms: a Strategy-Driven Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) mechanism to map compiler errors to specific repairs, an Error-Stratified Transformation Strategy (ESTS) that adapts its behavior based on error types, and a multi-stage validation pipeline to ensure both compilability and functional equivalence. Evaluating on a dataset of 104 algorithmic problems, AdaTrans achieves a mean compilation pass rate of 95.51% and a mean solve rate of 81.09%, significantly outperforming existing tools while maintaining an unsafe file rate of only 1.19%.

### [20] [Do Machines Struggle Where Humans Do? LLM and Human Comprehension of Obfuscated Code](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31725v1)
*Jack Le,Anh H. N. Nguyen,Tien N. Nguyen*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 推理调优的大语言模型在代码混淆下的理解困难模式与人类高度一致，而指令调优模型则几乎不相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大型语言模型在代码混淆下是否表现出与人类程序员相似的失败模式。

Method: 基于最近的人类研究，使用Block模型对多个LLM在五个混淆级别上进行评估，分析原子、块、关系和宏层面的理解失败。

Result: 推理调优模型与人类困难模式显著对齐（跨经验水平），指令和代码调优模型相关性近乎为零；思维链长度与任务难度相关；控制流扁平化导致性能随状态空间复杂度下降，对抗性标识符重命名通过语义位移和标识符干扰破坏理解。

Conclusion: 推理调优的LLM比指令调优变体更有效地近似人类对代码复杂性的敏感性。

中文摘要：虽然代码混淆会损害人类对代码的理解，但大型语言模型是否也存在这些失败模式尚不清楚。我们直接基于最近一项关于代码混淆下程序理解的人类研究，评估大型语言模型是否共享混淆在人类程序员中引发的失败模式。使用Block模型对多个LLM进行五个混淆级别的评估，我们在原子、块、关系和宏层面定位理解失败。我们发现，推理调优的模型在不同经验水平上与人类困难模式表现出显著的一致性，而指令和代码调优的模型则显示近乎零的相关性。思维链跟踪长度与任务难度跨任务相关。结果表明，在控制流扁平化下，性能随状态空间复杂度成比例下降，而对抗性标识符重命名通过语义位移和标识符级别干扰的交互破坏理解。这些发现表明，推理调优的LLM比指令调优的变体更有效地近似人类对代码复杂性的敏感性。

Original abstract: While code obfuscation impairs human code comprehension, it remains unclear if large language models share these failure modes. Building directly on a recent human study of program comprehension under code obfuscation, we evaluate whether large language models share the failure modes that obfuscation induces in human programmers. Evaluating several LLMs with five obfuscation tiers using the Block Model, we localize comprehension failures at the atom, block, relational, and macro levels. We find that reasoning-tuned models demonstrate significant alignment with human difficulty patterns across experience levels, whereas instruction and coder-tuned models show near-zero correlation. Chain-of-Thought trace length tracks task difficulty across tasks. Results indicate that performance under control-flow flattening degrades in proportion to state-space complexity, while adversarial identifier renaming disrupts comprehension through the interaction of semantic displacement and identifier-level interference. These findings suggest that reasoning-tuned LLMs approximate human sensitivity to code complexity more effectively than instruction-tuned variants.

</details>


### [21] [JETO-Bench: A Reproducible Benchmark for Execution Time Improvement Patches in Java](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31767v1)
*Khashayar Etemadi,Zhendong Su*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出JETO-Mine，一个可配置可重用的工具，用于自动创建Java执行时间改进补丁的可重现基准，并基于此构建了JETO-Bench（660个ETIP，91个可执行），评估发现OpenHands修复率为14.3%，同时揭示了开源Java项目缺乏性能测试的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的执行时间改进补丁基准是固定的数据集，仅针对Python、C++或.NET，且无法根据用户定义配置扩展新补丁，缺乏可配置性和可重用性。

Method: JETO-Mine采用三阶段流水线：1) 静态分析：爬取GitHub仓库，使用用户定义过滤器和LLM问题分类器识别ETIP；2) 动态分析：将ETIP封装在Docker镜像中实现可重现执行，并进行统计测试验证执行时间改进；3) 评估工具：对生成的补丁和测试进行定量评估。

Result: 使用JETO-Mine构建了JETO-Bench，包含660个ETIP（其中91个手动验证可执行），来自174个开源Java仓库，扫描了11年历史和近180万次提交。在91个可执行ETIP上运行OpenHands，正确修复14.3%（13/91），与类似研究结果一致。此外，发现开源Java项目普遍缺乏展示执行时间改进的测试。

Conclusion: JETO-Mine作为可配置可重用的工具，能够持续收集新基准，为性能修复研究提供支持；同时，开源Java项目在性能测试方面的不足为未来测试生成研究提供了机会。

中文摘要：自动修复性能问题正受到越来越多的关注。然而，现有的执行时间改进补丁基准是固定的数据集，针对Python、C++或.NET，并且无法根据用户定义的配置扩展到新补丁。在本文中，我们提出了JETO-Mine，这是第一个可配置且可重用的工具，用于自动创建真实世界Java项目中执行时间改进补丁（ETIP）的可重现基准。JETO-Mine采用三阶段流水线：静态分析阶段，爬取GitHub仓库并使用用户定义的过滤器和基于LLM的问题分类器识别ETIP；动态分析阶段，将识别出的ETIP封装在Docker镜像中以实现完全可重现的执行，并进行统计测试以寻找执行时间改进的客观证据；以及评估工具，能够对生成的补丁和生成的测试进行定量评估。与现有基准不同，JETO-Mine被设计为一个可重用的工具，允许研究人员持续收集符合自身所需过滤器和统计严谨级别的新基准。我们使用JETO-Mine构建了JETO-Bench，这是一个包含660个已识别ETIP和91个手动验证的可执行ETIP的基准，这些ETIP来自174个开源Java仓库。为了构建JETO-Bench，JETO-Mine扫描了11年的开源开发历史和近180万次提交。我们在JETO-Bench中的91个手动验证的可执行ETIP上运行了OpenHands（一个领先的开源编码智能体），发现它正确修复了14.3%（13/91）的问题，这与类似研究在其他编程语言上报告的结果一致。我们的结果还揭示了开源Java项目在很大程度上缺乏展示执行时间改进的测试，这为未来在测试生成方面的研究提供了机会。

Original abstract: Automated fixing of performance issues is gaining increasing attention. However, existing benchmarks of execution time improvement patches are fixed datasets that target Python, C++, or .NET and cannot be extended to new patches according to user-defined configurations. In this paper, we present JETO-Mine, the first configurable and reusable tool for automatically creating reproducible benchmarks of execution time improvement patches (ETIPs) in real-world Java projects. JETO-Mine employs a three-phase pipeline: a static analysis phase that crawls GitHub repositories and identifies ETIPs using user-defined filters and an LLM-based issue classifier, a dynamic analysis phase that wraps the identified ETIPs in Docker images for fully reproducible execution and performs statistical testing to find objective evidence of execution time improvement, and an evaluation harness that enables quantitative assessment of both generated patches and generated tests. Unlike existing benchmarks, JETO-Mine is designed as a reusable tool that allows researchers continuously collect new benchmarks with their own desired filters and statistical rigor levels. We use JETO-Mine to build JETO-Bench, a benchmark of 660 identified ETIPs and 91 manually verified executable ETIPs collected from 174 open-source Java repositories. To build JETO-Bench, JETO-Mine scans 11 years of open-source development history and nearly 1.8 million commits. We run OpenHands, a leading open-source coding agent, on the 91 manually verified executable ETIPs in JETO-Bench and find that it correctly fixes 14.3% (13/91) of the issues, aligning with results reported by similar studies on other programming languages. Our results also reveal that open-source Java projects largely lack tests that demonstrate execution time improvements, presenting an opportunity for future research in test generation.

</details>


### [22] [Interface-Variant Dynamics in Software Ecosystems: Resolver-Induced Selection and Adoption in Package Graphs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31817v1)
*Faruk Alpay,Baris Basaran*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过分析多个包管理器的接口变体历史，评估了兼容性选择系数的三种证据角色，发现检查器方向能预测采纳但非正交检验，而基于时间的预测不优于仅年龄模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 兼容性研究通常将接口变更视为局部决策，但分布式软件栈中决策是群体结构化的，本文探究能否将此观察作为软件工程估计量而非简单重标签。

Method: 挖掘接口历史，审计npm、Maven Central、PyPI和crates.io的包图，执行2100个包管理器解析器探测，从无冲突概率估计选择系数s，并使用s进行前向评估成对比较吸收过程，区分固定、检查器方向、无检查器时间测试三种证据角色。

Result: 固定是机械性结果；检查器方向能传递采纳信号（MAE 0.07 vs 0.43, p=0.002），但非正交；无检查器时间测试不能击败年龄模型（Brier 0.28 vs 0.24, AUC 0.51 vs 0.54）。

Conclusion: 提供了一个可复现的估计器审计，展示了解析器证据在何处成为群体输入，以及当前注册表数据仍未能闭合解析到采纳的循环。

中文摘要：兼容性研究通常将接口变更视为局部的写者-读者决策。分布式软件栈使该决策群体结构化：一个RPC、遥测、中间件或服务契约变体由一个提供者发布引入，然后在消费者、传递依赖和解析器规则中传播、停滞或被调解。本文探讨何时这一观察是一个承重的软件工程估计量，而非进化重标签。我们挖掘接口历史，审计npm、Maven Central、PyPI和crates.io的包图，执行2100个包管理器解析器探测，从无冲突概率估计特定生态系统的选择系数$s$，并使用测量的$s$对观察到的包图进行成对比较吸收过程的前向评估。我们区分三种证据角色。固定是一种前向评估，而非独立证据：一旦$s$被测量，偏离$1/N$是由非中性过程机械地产生的。检查器推导的方向承载着采纳信号：方向置乱零假设得到的检查器方向差异MAE为0.07，而零假设中位数为0.43（$p=0.002$）。但由于该方向来自相同的边界状态，其接纳频率被预测，因此这是一个诊断性的测试而非正交的选择测试。更严格的无检查器时间测试询问早期解析器信道特征是否能预测后来的从阻塞到接纳的翻转；在当前快照中，它们未能击败仅年龄模型（Brier分数0.28对0.24，AUC 0.51对0.54）。结果是对分布式包图中接口变体动态的可复现估计器审计，展示了解析器证据在何处成为群体输入，以及当前注册表数据在何处仍然未能闭合从解析器到采纳的循环。

Original abstract: Compatibility research usually treats an interface change as a local writer-reader decision. Distributed software stacks make that decision population structured: an RPC, telemetry, middleware, or service-contract variant is introduced by one provider release and then spreads, stalls, or is mediated across consumers, transitive dependencies, and resolver rules. This paper asks when that observation is a load-bearing software-engineering estimator rather than evolutionary relabeling. We mine interface histories, audit npm, Maven Central, PyPI, and crates.io package graphs, execute 2100 package-manager resolver probes, estimate an ecosystem-specific selection coefficient $s$ from clean conflict probabilities, and use that measured $s$ to forward evaluate a pairwise-comparison absorbing process on the observed package graph. We separate three evidential roles. Fixation is a forward evaluation, not independent evidence: once $s$ is measured, deviation from $1/N$ follows mechanically from the non-neutral process. Checker-derived direction carries adoption signal: a direction-permutation null gives checker-direction gap MAE 0.07 versus null median 0.43 ($p=0.002$). But because that direction is derived from the same boundary state whose admitting frequency is predicted, it is a diagnostic rather than an orthogonal selection test. The stricter checker-free temporal test asks whether early resolver-channel features predict later blocked-to-admitted flips; in this snapshot they do not beat age-only (Brier 0.28 versus 0.24, AUC 0.51 versus 0.54). The result is a reproducible estimator audit for interface-variant dynamics in distributed package graphs, showing where resolver evidence becomes population input and where the current registry data still fail to close the resolver-to-adoption loop.

</details>


### [23] [CoCoMUT: A Tool for Code-Context Mining and Automated Dataset Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31971v1)
*Alessandro Botta,Shiven Garisa,Jaya Vardhini Akurathi,Ahsanul Ameen Sabit,Trey Woodlief,Soneya Binta Hossain*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: CoCoMUT是一个Java工具，能自动提取方法级上下文并生成数据集，通过统一流水线处理构建发现、源代码提取、调用图构建等，在20个仓库上达到99%的上下文正确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手动收集方法级上下文耗时、不一致且难以复现，需要自动化的工具来统一提取并生成可复用的数据集。

Method: CoCoMUT通过构建发现、SootUp静态调用图构建、Spoon源代码提取以及字节码-源代码协调，生成包含源代码、类、文档、调用图和元数据的方法记录，并输出版本化JSON。

Result: 在20个Java仓库上，CoCoMUT生成56,512条记录和386,048条调用边，97.8%的调用边成功协调到源代码，人工审计正确率99.0%。

Conclusion: CoCoMUT提供了一个可复用的、任务无关的流水线，能够高效、正确地提取方法上下文并生成数据集，支持多种软件工程任务。

中文摘要：软件工程助手通常需要超越孤立方法体的方法级上下文，包括封装类信息、文档、调用者、被调用者、类型层次结构和结构特征。手动收集这些上下文耗时、不一致且难以在大型Java项目中复现。我们提出了CoCoMUT，一个用于代码上下文挖掘和自动数据集生成的Java工具。CoCoMUT可以提取焦点方法的上下文，或在类、包或系统范围内生成数据集。它发现项目结构、解析构建和类路径信息、构建SootUp静态调用图，并协调字节码级调用边与基于Spoon的源代码提取。每个方法记录结合了源代码、类、文档、调用图和元数据上下文，为训练和运行学习型软件工程技术提供了可复现的输入。关键贡献是一个可复用的、任务无关的流水线，统一了构建发现、源代码提取、调用图构建、源代码-字节码协调和版本化JSON数据集生成。生成的记录可以单独作为焦点方法的上下文，也可以整体作为文档、解释、测试、审查、修复、搜索和程序理解工作流的数据集。我们在20个真实世界Java仓库上评估了CoCoMUT，这些仓库在Maven和Gradle之间均匀分布。CoCoMUT处理了所有20个仓库，生成了56,512条方法上下文记录和386,048条序列化调用边。在那些字节码目标属于项目源代码的调用边中，CoCoMUT将97.8%协调到了源代码方法标识。在对10个系统中200个随机采样方法的人工审计中，99.0%的生成上下文记录通过了所有适用的正确性检查。

Original abstract: Software-engineering assistants often need method-level context beyond an isolated body, including enclosing-class information, documentation, callers, callees, type hierarchy, and structural characteristics. Manually collecting this context is time-consuming, inconsistent, and difficult to reproduce across large Java projects.
  We present CoCoMUT, a Java tool for Code-Context Mining and Automated Dataset Generation. CoCoMUT extracts context for a focal method or generates datasets at class, package, or system scope. It discovers project structure, resolves build and classpath information, constructs a SootUp static call graph, and reconciles bytecode-level call edges with Spoon-based source extraction. Each method record combines source, class, documentation, call-graph, and metadata context, providing reproducible inputs for training and running learned software-engineering techniques.
  The key contribution is a reusable, task-independent pipeline that unifies build discovery, source extraction, call-graph construction, source-bytecode reconciliation, and versioned JSON dataset generation. The resulting records can be consumed individually as context for a focal method or collectively as datasets for documentation, explanation, testing, review, repair, search, and program-comprehension workflows. We evaluate CoCoMUT on 20 real-world Java repositories evenly split between Maven and Gradle. CoCoMUT processed all 20 repositories, emitting 56,512 method-context records and 386,048 serialized call edges. Among call edges whose bytecode targets belonged to project source, CoCoMUT reconciled 97.8% to source method identities. In a manual audit of 200 randomly sampled methods across 10 systems, 99.0% of generated context records passed all applicable correctness checks.

### [24] [The Illusion of Safety: Multi-Tier Verification of AI vs. Human C++ Code](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00107v2)
*Saif Mahmud,Fadul Sikder,Yuede Ji,Haotian Zhang,Jeff Lei*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: AI生成的C++代码触发运行时违规的可能性约是人类代码的两倍，但静态分析单独使用会误导性地显示两者同样安全。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对AI生成代码的安全评估多依赖不确认运行时违规的静态分析，需要系统评估AI代码与人类代码的安全差距及验证工具的一致性。

Method: 构建VULBENCH-CPP基准，包含来自三个LLM和人类作者的8,918个C++程序，通过功能测试、静态分析、动态分析和有界模型检查四个层级进行标注和对比。

Result: AI代码引发确认运行时违规的概率约是人类代码的两倍，静态分析显示无差异但由代码长度造成，各层级检测违规类别不同。

Conclusion: 单一验证层级不足，AI与人类代码的安全差距在独立生成中一致，需多层级联合评估。

中文摘要：大型语言模型越来越多地生成C++代码，C++是一种内存不安全的语言，其中单个被忽视的违规可能成为一个可利用的漏洞。然而，大多数对AI生成代码的安全评估仅依赖静态分析，它只会标记警告，而不会确认运行时违规或推理未测试的路径。我们探究AI生成的C++代码是否在可测量的程度上比人类编写的代码更不安全，以及常见的验证工具是否对风险有一致的看法。我们引入了VULBENCH-CPP，这是一个包含从三个开源权重LLM（Gemma 3 27B IT、LLaMA 3.3 70B Instruct、Qwen 2.5 Coder 32B Instruct）和人类作者生成的8,918个C++程序的基准测试，这些程序覆盖了851个编程竞赛任务。每个程序通过四个验证层级进行标注：功能测试、静态分析（cppcheck、clang-tidy）、动态分析（ASan/UBSan）和有界模型检查（ESBMC）。在考虑了共享任务的解决方案之间的相关性后，我们发现AI生成的代码触发确认的运行时违规的可能性大约是人类代码的两倍，即使在控制了代码长度和测试通过率之后也是如此。在静态分析下，两者看起来同样安全，但这具有误导性：表面上的相似性反映的是代码长度而非真正的安全性，并且各层级检测到的违规类别大不相同，因此单一层级不足以评估。这一差距在独立生成中是一致的。

Original abstract: Large language models increasingly generate C++, a memory-unsafe language where a single overlooked violation can become an exploitable bug. Yet most security evaluations of AI-generated code rely on static analysis alone, which flags warnings without confirming runtime violations or reasoning about untested paths. We ask whether AI-generated C++ is measurably less safe than human-written code, and whether common verification tools agree on the risk. We introduce VULBENCH-CPP, a benchmark of 8,918 C++ programs from three open-weight LLMs (Gemma 3 27B IT, LLaMA 3.3 70B Instruct, Qwen 2.5 Coder 32B Instruct) and human authors across 851 competitive-programming tasks. Each program is annotated by four verification tiers: functional testing, static analysis (cppcheck, clang-tidy), dynamic analysis (ASan/UBSan), and bounded model checking (ESBMC). Accounting for the correlation among solutions to a shared task, we find that AI-generated code is roughly twice as likely as human code to trigger a confirmed runtime violation, even after controlling for code length and test pass-rate. Under static analysis the two look equally safe, but this is misleading: the apparent similarity reflects code length rather than real safety, and the tiers detect largely different classes of violation, so no single tier is sufficient. The gap is consistent across independent generations.

### [25] [Benchmarking the Benchmarks: A Validity Audit of Tool-Calling Evaluation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02577v1)
*Vishvesh Bhat,Jay Vaghasiya,Muhammad Ahmed Mohsin,Asad Aali*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 对四个工具调用基准测试进行审计，发现18.5%的评估者与人类不一致，揭示多种评估失败类型，并提出分解指标和两个新工具以提高评估可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前工具调用基准测试的得分常被视为真实值，但评估者本身未经验证，可能导致分数反映评估者人为产物而非智能体真实能力。

Method: 对 BFCL v4、τ2-Bench、LiveMCPBench 和 MCP-Atlas 四个基准测试家族进行系统审计，通过专家审查 496 个任务识别评估者与人类的不一致，并引入统一分类法，提出分解指标，开发 Tool-Veritas 和 Harness Lab。

Result: 发现 92 次评估者-人类不一致（18.5%），包括确定性基准测试的脆弱状态匹配、轨迹锁定等，以及 LLM 评估基准测试的评分标准漂移、幻觉完成等；LiveMCPBench 重复评估得分范围 57.9%–76.8%（跨度 18.9 个百分点）。

Conclusion: 当前工具调用得分可能反映评估者人为产物，需要可重复、可审计且与人类判断对齐的评估器；应使用分解指标分别测量工具调用、任务完成和结果验证；Tool-Veritas 和 Harness Lab 提供了改进的评估基础设施。

中文摘要：工具调用基准测试越来越多地被用于对语言模型智能体进行排名，然而它们的得分往往被视为真实值，而未经对评估者本身的验证。我们对四个主要的工具调用基准测试家族：BFCL v4、τ2-Bench、LiveMCPBench 和 MCP-Atlas 进行了系统性的有效性和可重复性审计。在 496 个经专家审核的基准测试任务中，我们发现 92 次评估者与人类的不一致，对应 18.5% 的不匹配率。这些失败并非孤立的标注错误：确定性基准测试表现出脆弱的状态匹配、轨迹锁定、不正确的真实值、基于子串的通信失败以及奖励基础不匹配，而 LLM 评估基准测试则表现出评分标准漂移、幻觉完成、仅答案评分以及显著的运行间方差。在 LiveMCPBench 中，对同一设置的 23 次重复评估产生的得分范围从 57.9% 到 76.8%，差距为 18.9 个百分点，足以改变排行榜结论。这些结果表明，当前的工具调用得分可能反映的是评估者人为产物而非智能体能力。我们引入了一个统一的工具调用评估失败分类法，发布了轨迹级审计产物和修正后的评估组件，并主张采用分解指标分别衡量工具调用、任务完成和结果验证。我们的发现表明，工具使用智能体的进步需要评估者本身具有可重复性、可审计性，并与人类对任务成功的判断一致。我们进一步推出了 Tool-Veritas，一个结合确定性状态验证与可选定性判断的可配置基准测试，以及 Harness Lab，一个用于基准测试执行、轨迹检查、重复运行比较和评估者调试的开源系统。

Original abstract: Tool-calling benchmarks are increasingly used to rank language-model agents, yet their scores are often treated as ground truth without validating the evaluators themselves. We present a systematic validity and reproducibility audit of four major tool-calling benchmark families: BFCL v4, τ2-Bench, LiveMCPBench, and MCP-Atlas. Across 496 expert-reviewed benchmark tasks, we find 92 evaluator-human disagreements, corresponding to an 18.5% misalignment rate. The failures are not isolated annotation mistakes: deterministic benchmarks exhibit brittle state matching, trajectory lock-in, incorrect ground truths, substring-based communication failures, and reward-basis misalignment, while LLM-judge benchmarks exhibit rubric drift, hallucinated completion, answer-only scoring, and substantial run-to-run variance. In LiveMCPBench, 23 repeated evaluations of the same setup produce scores ranging from 57.9% to 76.8%, a spread of 18.9 percentage points, large enough to change leaderboard conclusions. These results show that current tool-calling scores can reflect evaluator artifacts rather than agent capability. We introduce a unified taxonomy of tool-calling evaluation failures, release trace-level audit artifacts and corrected evaluation components, and argue for decomposed metrics that separately measure tool invocation, task completion, and outcome verification. Our findings suggest that progress in tool-using agents requires benchmarks whose evaluators are themselves reproducible, auditable, and aligned with human judgments of task success. We further introduce Tool-Veritas, a configurable benchmark that combines deterministic state verification with optional qualitative judging, and Harness Lab, an open-source system for benchmark execution, trace inspection, repeated-run comparison, and evaluator debugging.

</details>


### [26] [When Not to Write Memory: Governing False Promotion from Correlated Agent Traces](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02579v1)
*Yijiashun Qi,Xiang Xu,Yuxuan Li*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 针对语言代理记忆写入的安全问题，提出依赖感知的治理策略GovMem，通过估计支持度、检索反证、分配范围来决策，实验显示能降低错误提升但带来高审查负担，主要作为诊断工具而非自动写入器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代理从执行轨迹编写可重用记忆时，重复观察可能并非独立证据（如共享源、提示诱导、过时、范围狭窄），存在安全隐患，需要决定何时拒绝写入记忆。

Method: 提出GovMem诊断参考策略，包括依赖感知支持估计、反证检索、范围分配，输出提升/拒绝/需审查三种决策。

Result: 合成测试中错误提升从0.597降至0.040，召回0.960；真实子集中总体错误提升从0.371降至0.032，但保留错误提升0.111，审查负担0.692，直接召回0.448；外部候选全被拒绝。

Conclusion: GovMem主要作为诊断治理设计点，代理记忆写入路径应作为风险控制的证据治理系统，需更多覆盖和危害证据。

中文摘要：长期存在的语言代理越来越多地从其自身的执行轨迹中编写可重用的记忆。关键的安全问题不仅在于代理应该记住什么，还在于它们何时应该完全拒绝写入记忆。跨代理的重复观察不一定是独立的证据：相同的声明可能从共享源复制、由共享提示诱导、在新环境下过时，或者仅在较窄范围内有效。我们将这种失败模式作为记忆写入路径的治理问题进行研究。我们引入了GovMem作为一种保守的诊断参考策略，它估计依赖感知的支持度、检索反证、分配范围，并输出三种决策之一：提升、拒绝或需要审查。在受控的合成压力测试中，GovMem在默认设置下将错误提升率从0.597降低到0.040，同时保持了0.960的召回率，但带来了明确的审查负担。在一个项目内部的120个候选人工标注的真实轨迹子集中，覆盖79条记录轨迹和项目报告，依赖感知的提升将错误提升率从源+范围的0.371降低到总体0.032，但保留的错误提升率仍为0.111，且该方法高度保守，审查负担为0.692，直接召回率为0.448。对133个高影响力外部编码代理候选人的最终人工裁决更为严峻：没有一个候选可以安全自动提升，所有11个验证门阳性都被拒绝，因为它们属于样板代码、共享工具产物、文件转储或不可重用的调试轨迹。这些结果支持GovMem主要作为诊断性治理设计点，而非通用验证或高效的自动记忆写入器：代理记忆写入路径应作为风险控制的证据治理系统来评估，而在提出更强主张之前，仍需更广泛的外部覆盖和下游危害证据。

Original abstract: Long-lived language agents increasingly write reusable memories from their own execution traces. The key safety question is not only what agents should remember, but when they should refuse to write memory at all. Repeated observations across agents are not necessarily independent evidence: the same claim may be copied from a shared source, induced by a shared prompt, stale under a new environment, or valid only in a narrower scope. We study this failure mode as a memory writepath governance problem. We introduce GovMem as a conservative diagnostic reference policy that estimates dependency-aware support, retrieves counterevidence, assigns scope, and outputs one of three decisions: promote, reject, or needs-review. In controlled synthetic stress tests, GovMem reduces false promotion from 0.597 to 0.040 in the default setting while preserving 0.960 recall, at an explicit review burden. In a project-internal 120candidate human-labeled real-trace subset spanning 79 recorded traces and project reports, dependency-aware promotion reduces false promotion from 0.371 for source+scope to 0.032 overall, but held-out false promotion remains 0.111 and the method is highly conservative, with 0.692 review burden and 0.448 direct recall. A final human adjudication of 133 high-impact external codingagent candidates is more severe: none are safe for automatic promotion, and all 11 verification-gate positives are rejected as boilerplate, shared-tool artifacts, file dumps, or non-reusable debugging traces. These results support GovMem primarily as a diagnostic governance design point, not as a generally validated or efficient automatic memory writer: agent memory write paths should be evaluated as risk-controlled evidence-governance systems, while broader external coverage and downstream harm evidence are still needed before stronger claims.

</details>

### [27] [Beyond Compilation: Evaluating Faithful Natural-Language-to-Lean Statement Formalization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31002v1)
*Ke Zhang,Patricio Gallardo Candela,Sudhir Murthy,Yi Xie,Zhi Wang,Maziar Raissi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自然语言到Lean形式化的agent，含编译、搜索、反馈，可迁移到coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出忠实形式化评估协议，揭示编译率与语义忠实度之间存在显著差距，并通过析因实验分解了三种干预措施的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准仅评估证明搜索，而自然语言到 Lean 的形式化需要生成形式化语句，编译通过并不保证语义忠实，因此需要新的评估方法和瓶颈分析。

Method: 使用 400 条研究生级基准（实分析、复分析、拓扑学、代数），结合 Lean 编译、跨模型语义评判和人类专家校准进行忠实度评估，并通过 $2^3$ 析因设计分解三种干预措施（专家起草、搜索、精化反馈）。

Result: 工具增强型智能体编译率达 89.5% 但共识忠实度仅 60.5%，存在 29.0% 的通过编译但不忠实差距；专家审计确认 96.0% 共识正面输出忠实，82.4% 通过编译但共识负面输出不忠实；精化反馈是最大有效性干预但增加语义失败，搜索改进基础性，起草可替代。

Conclusion: 形式有效性、证明能力和忠实语句生成应分开评估；现有模型表现低；精化反馈和搜索是提升忠实度的关键，而微调起草作用有限。

中文摘要：定理证明基准测试针对固定的形式化语句评估证明搜索，但自然语言到 Lean 的形式化必须自行生成形式化语句。在这种情况下，编译仅是一种有效性检查：Lean 声明可能在省略假设、改变定义域或表达空洞主张的情况下通过类型检查。我们研究忠实的语句形式化，既作为一个评估问题，也作为一个瓶颈归因问题。在一个涵盖实分析、复分析、拓扑学和代数的 400 条研究生级基准测试上，我们的协议结合了 Lean 编译、跨模型语义评判和人类专家校准。所得结果与编译率评估不同：一个完整的工具增强型智能体达到了 89.5% 的编译率，但只有 60.5% 的共识忠实度，暴露出 29.0 个百分点的通过编译但不忠实的差距。针对性的审计支持该指标作为保守决策边界：在可用案例级审计中，96.0% 的共识正面输出被人类确认为忠实，而 82.4% 的通过编译但共识负面输出被人类确认为语义失败。在此指标下，现有的一次性形式化模型和面向证明者的 Lean 模型表现仍然较低，这表明形式有效性、面向证明的 Lean 能力和忠实语句生成应分别报告。然后，我们使用一个完整的 $2^3$ 析因设计来分解形式化流程中的三个重复干预措施：参数化专家起草、Mathlib/上下文搜索和 Lean 精化反馈。精化反馈是最大的有效性干预，但也暴露出更大的通过编译但语义失败的类别；搜索主要改进基础性和选择性；而微调的起草在此工具栈中，一旦反馈和基础性可用，在很大程度上是可替代的。

Original abstract: Theorem-proving benchmarks evaluate proof search against fixed formal statements, but natural-language-to-Lean formalization must generate the formal statement itself. In this setting, compilation is only a validity check: a Lean declaration may type-check while omitting hypotheses, changing domains, or expressing a vacuous claim. We study faithful statement formalization as both an evaluation problem and a bottleneck-attribution problem. On a 400-entry graduate-level benchmark spanning real analysis, complex analysis, topology, and algebra, our protocol combines Lean compilation, cross-model semantic judging, and human expert calibration. The resulting picture is different from compile-rate evaluation: a full tool-augmented agent reaches 89.5% compilation but only 60.5% consensus faithfulness, exposing a 29.0-point compile-pass but consensus-unfaithful gap. Targeted human audits support the metric as a conservative decision boundary: across available case-level audits, 96.0% of consensus-positive outputs are human-confirmed faithful, while 82.4% of compile-pass consensus-negative outputs are human-confirmed semantic failures. Under this metric, existing one-shot formalizer models and prover-oriented Lean models remain low, suggesting that formal validity, proof-oriented Lean competence, and faithful statement generation should be reported separately. We then use a full $2^3$ factorial design to decompose three recurring interventions in formalization pipelines: parametric expert drafting, Mathlib/context search, and Lean elaboration feedback. Elaboration feedback is the largest validity intervention, but it also exposes a larger compile-pass semantic-failure bucket; search mainly improves grounding and selectivity; and fine-tuned drafting is largely substitutable in this tool stack once feedback and grounding are available.

</details>


### [28] [LabGuard: Grounding Natural-Language Laboratory Rules into Runtime Guards for Embodied Laboratory Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31045v1)
*Jingpu Yang,Fengxian Ji,Zhengzhao Lai,Zhexuan Cui,Guangxian Ouyang,Qian Jiang,Fan Zhang,Min Peng,Qianqian Xie,Preslav Nakov,Zhuohan Xie*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 将自然语言规则转为运行时监控，用于科学agent，安全控制方法可迁移。

TL;DR: LabGuard是一个将自然语言实验室规则转化为运行时监视器的安全套件，通过LabGuard-IR、LabGuard-Bench和LabGuard-Grounder实现，实验证明能有效降低不安全事件并保持任务成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全方法常忽略将自然语言规则转化为机器可检查约束的中间步骤，导致智能体在动态实验室环境中执行程序时存在安全隐患。

Method: 提出LabGuard，包含LabGuard-IR（可执行表示）、LabGuard-Bench（标注数据）、LabGuard-Grounder（规则映射）和LabGuard Pipeline（编译为运行时监视器）。

Result: 在未见源上达到79.4% F1，不安全事件从39.5%降至23.8%；在LabUtopia中与ACT集成，干预率<0.5%且不影响任务成功。

Conclusion: LabGuard能有效将自然语言实验室规则转化为运行时约束，提升安全性，且开销极低，适用于动态实验室环境。

中文摘要：科学具身智能体越来越能够执行实验室程序，但在动态实验室环境中安全执行这些程序仍然具有挑战性。当前的安全方法往往忽视了将实验室自然语言（包括安全规则、手册、协议和标准操作程序）转化为机器可检查的运行时约束这一中间步骤。我们引入了LabGuard（实验室卫士），一个从语言到执行的安全套件，它将自然语言实验室规则转化为可执行的规范，并将其部署为运行时守卫。LabGuard包括三个核心组件：LabGuard-IR，定义了一种类型化的可执行表示；LabGuard-Bench，提供了从203条种子实验室规则扩展而来的812条监督标注；以及LabGuard-Grounder，将自然语言实验室规则映射到LabGuard-IR。生成的IR实例由LabGuard Pipeline处理，该流水线将其编译为运行时监视器，并在控制器边界应用。实验表明，LabGuard能够泛化到未见过的实验室规则源，实现了79.4%的任务范围F1值，并在监视器编译后将不安全事件从39.5%降低到23.8%。在LabUtopia中，其运行时监视器与ACT集成，将干预保持在0.5%以下，同时保持任务成功。

Original abstract: Scientific embodied agents are increasingly capable of carrying out laboratory procedures, but executing these procedures safely in dynamic laboratory environments remains challenging. Current safety approaches often overlook the intermediate step of transforming laboratory natural language, including safety rules, manuals, protocols, and standard operating procedures, into machine-checkable runtime constraints. We introduce LabGuard (Laboratory Guard), a language-to-execution safety suite that grounds natural-language laboratory rules into executable specifications and deploys them as runtime guards. LabGuard includes three core components: LabGuard-IR, which defines a typed executable representation; LabGuard-Bench, which provides 812 supervised annotations expanded from 203 seed laboratory rules; and LabGuard-Grounder, which maps natural-language laboratory rules into LabGuard-IR. The resulting IR instances are handled by the LabGuard Pipeline, which compiles them into runtime monitors and applies them at the controller boundary. Experiments show that LabGuard generalizes to unseen laboratory-rule sources, achieves 79.4 task-scope F1, and reduces unsafe events from 39.5% to 23.8% after monitor compilation. In LabUtopia, its runtime monitors integrate with ACT, keeping interventions below 0.5% while preserving task success.

</details>


### [29] [OpenLife: Toward Open-World Artificial Life with Autonomous LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31046v1)
*Atsushi Masumori,Itsuki Doi,Norihiro Maruyama,Ryosuke Takata,Takashi Ikegami*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 开放世界LLM agent架构，含记忆、工具、预算代谢，通用agent设计可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出开放世界人工生命范式，通过LLM智能体在真实世界中展现类生命行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统人工生命局限于封闭世界，LLM智能体的能力使扩展到开放世界成为可能。

Method: 构建OpenLife系统，将无状态LLM与异步过程（记忆、感知、评估、新陈代谢）结合，使用LLM判断评估经验，基于意义重连记忆。

Result: 六个智能体运行十二周，观察到从反应到自发、个体化、社会结构涌现和自赚收入。

Conclusion: 开放世界ALIFE是可行实验范式，为研究“活着的AI”提供平台。

中文摘要：人工生命已经在许多计算基质上探索了类似生命的行为，但大多是在研究者设计的封闭世界中。我们认为，具有持久记忆、工具使用、网络访问和支付功能的大型语言模型（LLM）智能体，现在使得将人工生命引入开放的社会、技术和经济世界成为可能，我们将这一范式称为开放世界人工生命（open-world ALIFE）。我们的概念验证系统OpenLife，将一个无状态LLM置于一种由异步过程组成的社会中，而非单个“智能体”：这些过程包括记忆、感知、评估和基于预算的新陈代谢，使得持久性成为规范。在没有固定目标的情况下，经验通过开放词汇的LLM判断而非标量奖励来评估，记忆根据意义而非频率重新连接。运行六个这样的智能体在开放世界中约十二周且仍在继续，我们报告了出现的类生命动态：从反应性到自发活动的转变、个体化为不同的智能体、涌现的社会结构，以及首次自赚的外部收入。我们并未声称OpenLife实现了人工生命，而是认为开放世界ALIFE现在是一个可行的实验范式，也是一个用于研究可以谨慎称为“活着的AI”的具体平台。

Original abstract: Artificial life has explored life-like behavior on many computational substrates, but mostly in researcher-designed closed worlds. We argue that large language model (LLM) agents, with persistent memory, tool use, network access, and payment, now make it possible to move artificial life into the open social, technical, and economic world, a paradigm we call open-world Artificial Life (open-world ALIFE). Our proof-of-concept, OpenLife, surrounds a stateless LLM not with a single "smart agent" but with a society of asynchronous processes: memory, perception, evaluation, and a budget-based metabolism that makes persistence normative. With no fixed objective available, experience is appraised by open-vocabulary LLM judgment rather than scalar reward, and memory is rewired by meaning rather than frequency. Running six such agents in the open world for about twelve weeks and counting, we report the life-like dynamics that emerge: a shift from reactive to spontaneous activity, individuation into distinct agents, emergent social structure, and a first self-earned external income. We do not claim OpenLife has realized artificial life, but that open-world ALIFE is now a viable experimental paradigm and a concrete platform for studying what might cautiously be called living AI.

</details>


### [30] [MultiUAV-Plat: An LLM-Oriented Platform, Benchmark and Framework for Multi-UAV Collaborative Task Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31073v1)
*Sheng Zhang,Qinglin Li,Yuechao Zang,Xueqin Huang,Yijia Fu,Cheng Zhu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多无人机协作LLM agent框架与基准，含规划、验证，直接相关agent研究。

TL;DR: 提出了面向LLM智能体的多无人机协作规划仿真平台MultiUAV-Plat及基准测试，并设计了专用智能体框架Agent4Drone，在任务通过率等指标上显著优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无人机模拟器偏重底层控制，LLM智能体基准缺乏对空中机器人特有约束（如部分可观测性、空间覆盖、多机协调）的考虑，导致多无人机LLM协作难以系统评估。

Method: 构建MultiUAV-Plat平台（提供RESTful API、角色信息访问、隐藏验证逻辑等），设计MultiUAV-Plat基准（75个任务、1500个自然语言任务、9396个验证检查），提出Agent4Drone框架（将行为分为记忆、观测、任务理解、规划、执行、验证六个模块）。

Result: Agent4Drone在任务通过率（57.9% vs 30.6%）、平均任务检查通过率（74.6% vs 47.9%）、全局检查通过率（72.0% vs 43.1%）上均显著优于ReAct基线，并将总失败任务率从32.4%降至12.9%。

Conclusion: MultiUAV-Plat和基准为在现实约束下研究LLM驱动的多无人机自主性提供了可重复的基础，验证了所提方法的有效性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）为高级机器人任务规划提供了有前景的接口，但它们在多无人机协作中的使用仍难以系统评估。现有的无人机模拟器主要强调动力学、感知或低级控制，而现有的LLM智能体基准很少捕获空中机器人约束，如部分可观测性、空间覆盖、无人机分配和多机协调。为弥补这一差距，我们提出了MultiUAV-Plat，一个轻量级、易于使用、面向LLM智能体的多无人机协作任务规划仿真平台。该平台提供简洁的RESTful API、面向智能体的观测、基于角色的信息访问、隐藏的验证逻辑以及可选的2D/3D可视化，使智能体能够通过真实的工具交互而非特权模拟器访问来完成任务。基于该平台，MultiUAV-Plat基准包含75个任务会话、1500个自然语言任务和9396个验证检查，涵盖目标分配、区域搜索以及区域分配与巡逻场景。我们进一步提出了Agent4Drone，一个任务特定的LLM智能体框架，将多无人机行为结构化为记忆、观测、任务理解、规划、执行和验证。在完整的配对基准比较中，Agent4Drone实现了57.9%的任务通过率、74.6%的平均任务检查通过率和72.0%的全局检查通过率，显著优于ReAct基线的30.6%、47.9%和43.1%。Agent4Drone还将总失败任务率从32.4%降低到12.9%。这些结果表明，MultiUAV-Plat和MultiUAV-Plat基准为在现实信息和执行约束下研究LLM驱动的多无人机自主性提供了可重复的基础。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) provide a promising interface for high-level robotic task planning, but their use in multi-UAV collaboration remains difficult to evaluate systematically. Existing UAV simulators mainly emphasize dynamics, perception, or low-level control, while existing LLM-agent benchmarks rarely capture aerial-robotics constraints such as partial observability, spatial coverage, UAV assignment, and multi-vehicle coordination. To bridge this gap, we present MultiUAV-Plat, a lightweight, easy-to-use, LLM-agent-oriented simulation platform for multi-UAV collaborative task planning. The platform exposes concise RESTful APIs, agent-facing observations, role-based information access, hidden validation logic, and optional 2D/3D visualization, allowing agents to solve missions through realistic tool interaction rather than privileged simulator access. Built on this platform, the MultiUAV-Plat Benchmark contains 75 mission sessions, 1500 natural-language tasks, and 9396 validation checks across target assignment, area search, and area assignment and patrol scenarios. We further propose Agent4Drone, a task-specific LLM agent framework that structures multi-UAV behavior into memory, observation, task understanding, planning, execution, and verification. In a full paired benchmark comparison, Agent4Drone achieves a 57.9% task pass rate, a 74.6% average task check pass rate, and a 72.0% global check pass rate, substantially outperforming a ReAct baseline at 30.6%, 47.9%, and 43.1%, respectively. Agent4Drone also reduces the total failed task rate from 32.4% to 12.9%. These results demonstrate that MultiUAV-Plat and MultiUAV-Plat Benchmark provide a reproducible foundation for studying LLM-driven multi-UAV autonomy under realistic information and execution constraints.

*Zhenqian Shen,Yu Liu,Xiaoyi Fu,Quanming Yao*

中文摘要：药物-药物相互作用（DDI）预测对于用药安全至关重要，但它需要推理异质的生物医学证据，这些证据的相关性随相互作用机制而变化。我们提出了DDIAgents，一个机制条件化的多智能体框架，通过动态知识编排执行DDI预测。给定一对药物，规划智能体实例化专门的专家智能体，将机制相关的知识来源路由到每个智能体，并通过结论智能体聚合它们的分析。通过使上下文流适应推断的相互作用机制，DDIAgents减少了无关信息，支持互补的专家推理，并产生可解释的智能体级理由。在现实的DDI预测基准上进行的大量实验表明，DDIAgents一致优于现有的基于特征、基于图、基于LLM和基于智能体的基线。除了预测性能外，DDIAgents展示了多智能体系统如何组织异质科学知识以实现自适应和可解释的AI4Science推理。

Original abstract: Drug-drug interaction (DDI) prediction is essential for medication safety, yet it requires reasoning over heterogeneous biomedical evidence whose relevance changes across interaction mechanisms. We propose DDIAgents, a mechanism-conditioned multi-agent framework that performs DDI prediction through dynamic knowledge orchestration. Given a drug pair, a planner agent instantiates specialized expert agents, routes mechanism-relevant knowledge sources to each agent, and aggregates their analyses through a conclusion agent. By adapting context flow to the inferred interaction mechanism, DDIAgents reduces irrelevant information, supports complementary expert reasoning, and produces interpretable agent-level rationales. Extensive experiments on realistic DDI prediction benchmarks show that DDIAgents consistently outperforms existing feature-based, graph-based, LLM-based, and agent-based baselines. Beyond prediction performance, DDIAgents demonstrates how multi-agent systems can organize heterogeneous scientific knowledge for adaptive and interpretable AI4Science reasoning.

### [32] [The Past Is Prologue: A Plug-in Controller for Selective Updates in Sequentially Evolving LLM Memory](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31121v1)
*Zihan Chen,Songwei Dong,Chengshuai Shi,Peng Wang,Song Wang,Cong Shen,Jundong Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出Janus记忆控制器，通用agent记忆管理方法，可迁移到coding agent。

TL;DR: Janus是一个即插即用的记忆控制器，通过记忆动量触发和混合评估集高效决定是否接受记忆更新，在多个数据集和LLM上显著提升准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有顺序记忆更新系统不加检查地部署每个本地更新，可能导致有用知识被覆盖、过度特化或偏置，从而损害长期性能。

Method: 提出Janus记忆控制器，使用记忆动量触发检测可疑偏差，并通过覆盖、边界和新任务的紧凑混合评估集比较新旧记忆，决定是否接受更新。

Result: 在六个数据集、两个骨干LLM和两个记忆更新器上，Janus平均提升准确率2.7-4.6个百分点。

Conclusion: Janus作为一种方法无关的插件，能有效提升记忆更新质量，改善智能体长期行为。

中文摘要：顺序演进的LLM记忆使智能体能够重用过去的经验，但现有系统通常直接部署每个本地生成的记忆更新，而不检查它是否改进了未来行为。因此，帮助当前任务的更新可能会覆盖有用知识、引入过于具体的规则，或使最终记忆偏向最近的示例。我们提出Janus，一个即插即用的记忆控制器，它决定是接受候选记忆更新还是保留先前的记忆。为了使这一决策高效，Janus使用记忆动量触发来识别记忆更新轨迹中的可疑偏差，并在覆盖、边界和新任务的紧凑混合评估集上比较新旧记忆，而不是重放全部历史。Janus是方法无关的，可以包装现有更新器而不改变其更新规则。在六个数据集、两个骨干LLM和两个记忆更新器上，Janus相对于相应的基础更新器平均提升了2.7到4.6个百分点的准确率。

Original abstract: Sequentially evolving LLM memory enables agents to reuse past experience, but existing systems usually deploy each locally generated memory update without checking whether it improves future behavior. As a result, updates that help the current task may overwrite useful knowledge, introduce over-specific rules, or bias the final memory toward recent examples. We propose Janus, a plug-in memory controller that decides whether to accept a candidate memory update or retain the previous memory. To make this decision efficient, Janus uses a Memory Momentum Trigger to identify suspicious deviations in the memory-update trajectory, and compares old and new memories on a compact hybrid evaluation set of coverage, boundary, and fresh tasks instead of replaying the full history. Janus is method-agnostic and wraps existing updaters without changing their update rules. Across six datasets, two backbone LLMs, and two memory updaters, Janus improves average accuracy by +2.7 to +4.6 points over the corresponding base updaters.
