### [33] [Beyond the Library: An Agentic Framework for Autoformalizing Research Mathematics](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31134v2)
*Arshia Soltani Moakhar,Iman Gholami,Max Springer,Mahdi JafariRaviz,MohammadTaghi Hajiaghayi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自动形式化数学证明的多agent框架，涉及验证、规划，直接相关coding agent。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在数学推理中常产生细微错误，而形式化语言如Lean可机械验证，因此需要自动形式化方法将自然语言数学翻译为可验证代码。

Method: 构建一个以协调器为核心的多智能体流水线，使用通用编码LLM；针对现有库外的概念，动态扩展类型定义并通过新颖的辅助引理技术验证，再形式化主要定理。

Result: 在PutnamBench上为32个随机问题生成了验证的Lean证明；在STOC五篇论文中成功形式化了主要定理和证明，其中两个证明仅依赖Lean内核，无额外公理。

Conclusion: 该框架能有效处理研究级数学的自动形式化，利用通用LLM的优势生成可验证的形式化证明。

中文摘要：尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）在数学推理方面展示了卓越的能力，但它们经常产生难以被人类察觉的细微错误。像Lean 4这样的形式化数学语言提供了机械化的证明检查，这强烈推动了自动形式化的需求：将自然语言数学自动翻译为可验证的代码。最近的趋势表明，为标准编程高度优化的通用LLMs现在超越了专门为Lean微调的较小模型。利用这一转变，我们引入了一个由通用编码LLMs驱动的智能体自动形式化框架。我们系统的核心是一个协调器，它管理着一个专为研究级数学量身定制的多智能体流水线。由于前沿研究经常依赖于现有库（如Mathlib）范围之外的概念，我们的系统动态扩展必要的类型定义，并通过一种新颖的辅助引理技术进行验证，然后形式化主要定理。我们将我们的方法应用于PutnamBench，为随机抽取的32个问题生成了机器检查的Lean证明。此外，我们在ACM计算理论研讨会（STOC）的五篇论文上评估了我们的系统，涵盖组合数学、通信复杂度、机制设计、学习理论等领域，成功形式化了它们的主要定理，并与人类专家一起验证了生成的形式化结果；对于所有五篇论文，我们还形式化了证明以及陈述，值得注意的是其中两个证明除了Lean的内核外没有使用任何公理。我们的所有形式化结果可在 https://beyondthelibrary.github.io/formal_arxiv 获取。

Original abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated exceptional capabilities in mathematical reasoning, they frequently produce subtle errors that evade human detection. Formal mathematical languages like Lean 4 offer mechanical proof checking, strongly motivating the need for autoformalization: the automatic translation of natural language mathematics into verifiable code. Recent trends indicate that general-purpose LLMs, heavily optimized for standard programming, now outperform smaller models explicitly fine-tuned for Lean. Leveraging this shift, we introduce an agentic autoformalization framework powered by general coding LLMs. At the core of our system is an orchestrator that manages a multi-agent pipeline tailored for research-level mathematics. Because cutting-edge research frequently relies on concepts outside the scope of existing libraries like Mathlib, our system dynamically extends necessary type definitions and validates them via a novel Auxiliary Lemma technique before formalizing the primary theorems. We applied our approach to PutnamBench, producing machine-checked Lean proofs for a random sample of 32 problems. Furthermore, we evaluate our system on five papers from the ACM Symposium on Theory of Computing (STOC) spanning combinatorics, communication complexity, mechanism design, and learning theory, successfully formalizing their main theorems and validating the generated formalizations with human experts; for all five we also formalize the proofs alongside the statements, and notably two of them are proved with no axioms beyond Lean's kernel. All of our formalizations are available at https://beyondthelibrary.github.io/formal_arxiv .

### [34] [ClawArena-Team: Benchmarking Subagent Orchestration and Dynamic Workflows in Language-Model Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31174v2)
*Kaiwen Xiong,Haonian Ji,Shi Qiu,Zeyu Zheng,Cihang Xie,Xinyu Ye,Huaxiu Yao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: ClawArena-Team benchmark专注于子Agent编排，直接相关agent评测。

TL;DR: 提出ClawArena-Team基准评估LLM作为管理者的能力，发现权限授予是主要瓶颈，成本与质量解耦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准无法衡量单个LLM作为领导者管理多个子智能体的能力。

Method: 构建41个多轮多模态多目录场景，主智能体受限，通过SMS评分（任务正确性×最小权限×模态路由因子）评估管理能力。

Result: 管理瓶颈是权限授予而非感知；成本与管理质量解耦，分数集中但编排行为差异大。

Conclusion: LLM管理能力仍有提升空间，代码已开源以促进研究。

中文摘要：生产级大型语言模型（LLM）智能体日益被部署为管理者而非孤立的解题者：一个主模型创建专门的子智能体，分配任务，并通过动态工作流协调它们的并行、异步返回。一个模型是否真的能运行这样一个团队在很大程度上尚未被衡量：现有基准要么评估策略自身的任务解决能力，要么评估固定多智能体系统的涌现行为，但没有一个基准能孤立地衡量作为领导者的单个LLM的管理能力。我们引入ClawArena-Team，一个包含41个多轮、多模态、多目录场景的基准，涵盖258个评估轮次和72个阶段性更新，用于衡量这种管理能力。主智能体被有意约束：它原生仅感知文本，并仅直接访问部分工作空间。它指挥一个固定的、本地服务的子智能体池，因此分数差异反映的是管理技能而非原始能力。所有评分基于执行，无LLM评判器：总体分数——子智能体管理分数（SMS）——将任务正确性乘以最小权限和模态路由因子。在十二个专有、社区托管和自托管模型上的实验表明，管理瓶颈是权限授予而非感知（没有模型在工作空间权限精确度上超过50%）；成本和管理质量是解耦的（API成本差异超过100倍，而总体分数差异低于4倍，最便宜的开源模型位于帕累托前沿）；以及大多数排行榜分数聚集在一个9.9分的带宽内，而编排行为差异超过一个数量级。代码可在https://github.com/aiming-lab/ClawArena获取。

Original abstract: Production large language-model (LLM) agents are increasingly deployed not as lone problem-solvers but as managers: a main model creates specialized subagents, delegates work, and orchestrates their parallel, asynchronous returns through dynamic workflows. Whether one model can actually run such a team is largely unmeasured: existing benchmarks score a policy's own task-solving or a fixed multi-agent system's emergent behavior, but none isolate the management ability of the single LLM acting as leader. We introduce ClawArena-Team, a benchmark of 41 multi-turn, multimodal, multi-directory scenarios spanning 258 evaluation rounds and 72 staged updates that measures this management ability. The main agent is deliberately constrained: it natively perceives only text and directly accesses only part of the workspace. It commands a fixed, locally served subagent pool, so score differences reflect management skill, not raw capability. All scoring is execution-based with no LLM judge: an overall score -- the Subagent-Management Score (SMS) -- multiplies task correctness by a least-privilege and modality-routing factor. Across twelve proprietary, community-hosted, and self-hosted models, experiments show that the management bottleneck is privilege granting rather than perception (no model exceeds 50% workspace-permission precision); that cost and management quality are decoupled (API cost spans over 100 times while the overall score spans under 4 times, with the cheapest open models on the Pareto frontier); and that most leaderboard scores cluster within a 9.9-point band while orchestration behaviors diverge by more than an order of magnitude. Code is available at https://github.com/aiming-lab/ClawArena.

</details>


### [35] [HealthAgentBench: A Unified Benchmark Suite of Realistic Agentic Healthcare Environments for Challenging Frontier AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31179v1)
*Qianchu Liu,Sheng Zhang,Guanghui Qin,Jeya Maria Jose Valanarasu,Maximilian Rokuss,Mingyu Lu,Timothy Ossowski,Juan Manuel Zambrano Chaves,Cliff Wong,Peniel Argaw,Yashna Hasija,Mu Wei,Wen-wai Yim,Qin Liu,Zilin Jing,Jason Entenmann,Naoto Usuyama,Tristan Naumann,Hoifung Poon*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HealthAgentBench是一个包含54个医疗任务的基准，评估AI智能体在复杂临床工作流中的表现，当前最强智能体成功率仅约42%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要严格且全面的评估来衡量AI智能体在真实世界医疗应用中的进展。

Method: 创建了包含54个任务、7个类别、每个任务有独特环境的基准套件，要求智能体根据最小指令探索原始数据、操作复杂环境并执行多步解决方案，报告任务成功率。

Result: 前沿智能体整体成功率低，Codex GPT-5.5表现最好但仅约42%。智能体在EHR建模方面有潜力，医学成像对Claude Code模型困难，组合推理和大搜索空间任务对所有智能体困难。

Conclusion: HealthAgentBench是一个具有挑战性和现实性的基准，未来有巨大进步空间。

中文摘要：随着AI智能体在复杂、长期推理方面变得越来越有能力，严格而全面的评估对于衡量向真实世界医疗应用进展至关重要。我们引入了HealthAgentBench，这是一个包含54个智能体医疗任务的基准套件，涵盖7个类别，每个类别有其独特的环境。该基准套件涵盖了患者旅程中的多样化工作流程以及广泛的模态。每个任务旨在复制端到端的临床工作流程：给定最少的指令，智能体必须探索原始医疗数据，在复杂环境中操作，并执行超越简单提示的多步解决方案。最终报告任务成功率，为每个智能体在HealthAgentBench上的整体表现提供单一可解释的指标。在HealthAgentBench上评估前沿智能体时，我们发现整体任务成功率仍然很低，突显了该套件的难度。最强且最具成本效益的智能体Codex GPT-5.5仅达到约42%的成功率。除了总体表现，HealthAgentBench还揭示了不同任务类别中细微的优劣势。前沿智能体在自动开发基于EHR数据的研究建模流程方面显示出潜力，但医学成像仍然特别具有挑战性，尤其是对于Claude Code模型，而Codex GPT-5.5显示出新兴能力。结合大搜索空间和组合推理需求的任务对当前所有智能体仍然困难。这些结果共同表明，HealthAgentBench提供了一个具有挑战性和现实性的基准，未来还有很大的进步空间。我们在https://github.com/microsoft/HealthAgentBench上发布了我们的基准。

Original abstract: As AI agents become increasingly capable of complex, long-horizon reasoning, rigorous and holistic evaluation is essential for measuring progress toward real-world healthcare applications. We introduce HealthAgentBench, a suite of 54 agentic healthcare tasks across 7 categories each with its unique environment. The benchmark suite spans diverse workflows throughout the patient journey and a broad range of modalities. Each task is designed to replicate an end-to-end clinical workflow: given minimal instructions, an agent must explore raw healthcare data, operate within a complex environment, and execute multi-step solutions that go beyond naive prompting. A final task success rate is reported to provide a single, interpretable metric for HealthAgentBench overall performance for each agent. Evaluating frontier agents on HealthAgentBench, we find that overall task success rate remains low, underscoring the difficulty of the suite. The strongest and the most cost effective agent, Codex GPT-5.5, achieves only approximately 42% success rate. Beyond aggregate performance, HealthAgentBench reveals nuanced strengths and weaknesses across task categories. Frontier agents show promise in automatically developing research modeling pipelines over EHR data, but medical imaging remains especially challenging, particularly for Claude Code models, while Codex GPT-5.5 shows emerging capability. Tasks that combine large search spaces with compositional reasoning requirements remain difficult for all current agents. Together, these results suggest that HealthAgentBench provides a challenging and realistic benchmark with substantial room for future progress. We release our benchmark at https://github.com/microsoft/HealthAgentBench.

</details>


### [36] [AI-Assisted Discovery of Convex Relaxations via Dual Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31182v1)
*Sungyoon Kim,Mert Pilanci*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 双agent框架自动发现凸松弛，直接相关coding agent与自动优化。

TL;DR: 通过凸松弛和自动研究范式改进两个优化常数的下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作主要改进上界，本文关注下界的改进，通过凸松弛方法获得更强的下界。

Method: 采用自动研究范式，编码代理提出收紧约束，理论代理验证并搜索反例，通过显式对偶可行点在区间算术中认证下界。

Result: 将第一个自相关不等式下界从1.28改进到1.2937，将Erdős最小重叠常数下界从0.379005改进到0.37912。

Conclusion: 验证了自动研究范式在改进下界方面的有效性，为优化常数问题提供了新方法。

中文摘要：近期工作表明，LLM代理可以通过搜索极值构造来改进sharp-constant不等式，这给出了上界。我们处理互补的一面：下界对所有可容许函数成立，并且来自非凸问题的凸松弛，更紧的松弛给出更强的界。我们实例化自动研究范式来发现这样的松弛：一个编码代理提出有效的收紧约束，一个理论代理验证每个约束并搜索反例，并且每个报告的界都通过一个在严格区间算术中检查的显式对偶可行点进行认证。在Tao等人(2025)研究的两个优化常数——第一个自相关不等式（$C_{6.2}$）和Erdős最小重叠常数（$C_{6.5}$）上，我们将认证下界分别从$1.28$改进到$1.2937$和从$0.379005$改进到$0.37912$。

Original abstract: Recent work shows that LLM agents can improve sharp-constant inequalities by searching for extremal constructions, which yield upper bounds. We address the complementary side: a lower bound holds for every admissible function and follows from a convex relaxation of the nonconvex problem, with tighter relaxations giving stronger bounds. We instantiate the autoresearch paradigm to discover such relaxations: a coding agent proposes valid tightening constraints, a theory agent verifies each one and searches for counterexamples, and every reported bound is certified by an explicit dual-feasible point checked in rigorous interval arithmetic. On two optimization constants studied by \citet{tao2025alphaevolve} - the first autocorrelation inequality ($C_{6.2}$) and the Erdős minimum-overlap constant ($C_{6.5}$) - we improve the certified lower bounds from $1.28$ to $1.2937$ and from $0.379005$ to $0.37912$, respectively.

### [37] [Agentic RAG-VLM: Affordance-Aware Retrieval-Augmented Generation with Self-Reflective Planning for Robotic Grasping](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31200v1)

Motivation: 现有VLM方法依赖视觉相似性，忽视物理可供性（如手柄可抓取性、材料易碎性），且开环运行缺乏空间推理和故障恢复，在密集或物理多样场景中效果有限。

Method: 提出三个组件：1. 层次化可供性感知RAG（HAA-RAG），编码四维可供性描述符并按功能兼容性检索；2. 场景图约束推理器，构建空间关系图并调整抓取参数；3. 智能体自我反思管道，含14种故障分类和三级自适应重试。

Result: 在12任务基准（360次试验/配置）上整体成功率78.3%，相比VLM基线提升53.3个百分点。

Conclusion: 可供性感知检索、场景图推理和智能体恢复三者联合对于鲁棒操作至关重要。

中文摘要：在杂乱环境中进行可泛化的机器人抓取对于在非结构化人类空间中部署机械臂至关重要，然而现有基于VLM的方法依赖于视觉相似性进行物体匹配，忽视了物理可供性，如手柄可抓取性和材料易碎性，并且以开环方式运行，缺乏空间推理或故障恢复，从而限制了它们在物体密集或物理多样性场景中的有效性。我们提出Agentic RAG-VLM，这是一个统一的框架，通过将检索增强生成（RAG）与视觉语言模型（VLM）和智能体自我反思规划相结合，桥接了基于VLM的语义理解和物理基础的抓取执行。Agentic RAG-VLM引入了三个紧密耦合的组件：（1）层次化可供性感知RAG（HAA-RAG），它编码了四维可供性描述符，包括类型、材料、易碎性和可抓取区域，并根据功能可供性兼容性而非视觉外观检索策略；（2）场景图约束推理器，它从VLM感知构建空间关系图，并将邻近、遮挡和支撑约束转化为具体的抓取参数调整；（3）智能体自我反思管道，具有14种故障分类和三级自适应重试，用于闭环抓取优化。在包含12个任务的基准测试上进行评估，涵盖单次抓取、交互式和长视野场景，每种配置进行360次试验，Agentic RAG-VLM实现了78.3%的整体成功率，相比纯VLM基准线绝对提升了53.3个百分点，表明可供性感知检索、场景图推理和智能体恢复对于稳健操作都是至关重要的。

Original abstract: Generalizable robotic grasping in cluttered environments is essential for deploying manipulators in unstructured human spaces, yet existing VLM-based methods rely on visual similarity for object matching, neglecting physical affordances such as handle graspability and material fragility, and operate open-loop without spatial reasoning or failure recovery, limiting their effectiveness when objects are densely packed or physically diverse. We present Agentic RAG-VLM, a unified framework that bridges VLM-based semantic understanding and physically grounded grasp execution by integrating retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) with vision-language models (VLMs) and agentic self-reflective planning. Agentic RAG-VLM introduces three tightly coupled components: (1) a Hierarchical Affordance-Aware RAG (HAA-RAG) that encodes four-dimensional affordance descriptors, including type, material, fragility, and graspable region, and retrieves strategies by functional affordance compatibility rather than visual appearance; (2) a Scene Graph Constraint Reasoner that constructs spatial relationship graphs from VLM perception and translates proximity, occlusion, and support constraints into concrete grasp parameter adjustments; and (3) an Agentic Self-Reflective Pipeline with a 14-type failure taxonomy and three-level adaptive retry for closed-loop grasp refinement. Evaluated on a 12-task benchmark spanning single-grasp, interactive, and long-horizon scenarios with 360 trials per configuration, Agentic RAG-VLM achieves 78.3 percent overall success, a 53.3 percentage-point absolute gain over VLM-only baselines, demonstrating that affordance-aware retrieval, scene graph reasoning, and agentic recovery are jointly essential for robust manipulation.

### [38] [Thinking Before Retrieving: Robust Zero-Shot Composed Image Retrieval via Strategic Planning and Self-Criticism](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31222v1)
*Gunho Jung,Jeong-Woo Park,Seon Bin Kim,Seong-Whan Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出Planner-Executor-Critic架构，通用agent推理框架可迁移。

TL;DR: PEC-CIR是一个无需训练的零样本组合图像检索框架，通过规划器-执行器-批评家架构进行多阶段查询构建，减少语义错误并提高检索稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有单次生成策略难以检测或纠正语义失真和遗漏，导致参考属性的保持和文本要求的整合相互干扰，降低检索精度。

Method: 提出PEC-CIR框架，采用规划器-执行器-批评家架构，将查询构建分解为多阶段推理：规划器提取显式约束，执行器生成多个候选目标描述，批评家根据约束符合性评估候选。

Result: 通过在检索前显式评估候选查询，减少生成错误的传播，提高检索稳定性。

Conclusion: PEC-CIR通过多阶段推理和评估机制有效提升了组合图像检索的准确性和稳定性。

中文摘要：组合图像检索要求通过结合参考图像和文本修改指令从图库中识别目标图像。在无需训练的零样本设置下，该任务依赖于在推理时在冻结的视觉-语言嵌入空间中构建面向检索的文本查询。现有方法主要采用单次生成策略，将参考上下文和修改文本融合成统一描述。这种策略难以检测或纠正生成过程中的语义失真和遗漏。因此，参考属性的保持和文本要求的整合相互干扰，降低了检索精度。为了应对这些挑战，我们提出了PEC-CIR，一个无需训练的框架，将查询构建结构化为多阶段推理管道。该框架通过规划器-执行器-批评家架构运作，其中规划器提取显式约束，执行器生成多个候选目标描述，批评家根据约束符合性评估这些候选。通过将查询构建重新表述为阶段性推理过程而非单次输出，PEC-CIR通过在检索前显式评估候选查询来减少生成错误的传播，从而提高了检索稳定性。

Original abstract: Composed image retrieval requires identifying a target image from a gallery by integrating a reference image with a textual modification instruction. In a training-free zero-shot setting, this task relies on constructing a retrieval-oriented textual query within a frozen vision--language embedding space at inference time. Existing approaches predominantly rely on a single-pass generation strategy that fuses the reference context and modification text into a unified description. This strategy makes it difficult to detect or correct semantic distortions and omissions during generation. Consequently, the preservation of reference attributes and the integration of textual requirements interfere with each other, which degrades retrieval precision. To address these challenges, we introduce PEC-CIR, a training-free framework that structures query construction as a multi-stage reasoning pipeline. The framework operates through a Planner--Executor--Critic architecture where the Planner extracts explicit constraints, the Executor generates multiple candidate target descriptions, and the Critic evaluates these candidates based on constraint compliance. By reframing query construction as a staged inference process instead of a single-pass output, PEC-CIR reduces the propagation of generative errors by explicitly evaluating candidate queries before retrieval, thereby improving retrieval stability.

Original abstract: Ideation plays a pivotal role in scientific discovery. Recent LLM, especially AI Scientist systems, show promising potential for automated ideation. This constraint severely limits the flexibility required to navigate the vast search space of scientific literature and the complex action space of research reasoning. Recently, training Agentic LLMs has emerged as a promising direction, offering flexible reasoning frameworks and the capability for autonomous tool utilization. However, there remains a non-trivial challenge: applying previous agentic data synthesis methods to scientific ideation suffers from prohibitively high data synthesis cost. To bridge this gap, we propose Agentic-Ideation, a novel framework comprising an automated trajectory synthesis pipeline and a specialized agentic LLM trained for scientific ideation. Specifically, we first define a comprehensive tool space incorporating three external tools and three cognitive tools. Then we introduce an Oracle-Guided Data Synthesis strategy. By leveraging a reference idea as oracle guidance, this approach steers the multi-agent system to efficiently reconstruct the logical reasoning and tool invocation paths, transforming aimless trial-and-error into directed trajectory generation. Finally, we train the agent on these synthesized trajectories, employing a masking strategy on tool execution results. This ensures the model focuses on decision-making logic without interference from external feedback. Experimental results demonstrate that our method outperforms the SOTA workflow-based baseline by \textbf{11.91\%} in overall quality. Furthermore, our approach improves the sample efficiency of high-quality data synthesis by \textbf{over 10$\times$}.

We present Embodied CAD, solver-grounded LLM agents for parametric B-Rep assembly modeling. Instead of generating a complete script in one pass, the agent iteratively selects actions from a stratified L0-L4 CAD skill library, resolves them into typed geometric operations, executes them in a CAD backend, and uses solver feedback to plan, repair, and learn. The framework combines action grammar constraints, deterministic parameter resolution, and solver-derived rewards for supervised warm-up and GRPO-style refinement. We evaluate Embodied CAD on multi-step mechanical, industrial equipment, and mold-oriented assembly tasks using solver-aligned metrics: executable rate, skill accuracy, operation-family accuracy, exact policy accuracy, and task completion success. Original abstract: Human reasoning is inherently multimodal: when problems become difficult, we rarely think in words alone. We often externalize our reasoning by sketching diagrams or drawing grids to understand the underlying conceptual structure and avoid mistakes. We address these questions by introducing a switching metric based on trustworthiness and complexity signals, which estimates when grounding a spatial story into structure is likely to improve performance. This takes a first step toward principled modality selection in Large Language Model (LLM) reasoning. Across our settings, switching from natural language-based reasoning to a grid-based representation improves LLM performance by up to 42%, highlighting the importance of modality choice in shaping reasoning outcomes.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索LLMs在静态软件代码中检测和分类浮点错误的潜力，以弥补传统方法的不足。

Method: 构建InterFLOPBench基准（90个C内核，1130个样本），将浮点错误检测作为多标签分类任务，使用F1分数评估14个LLMs的性能。

Result: Qwen 3等最新模型整体F1>0.88；除零错误F1平均0.8479，下溢和取消错误F1分别平均0.6059和0.6164。

Conclusion: LLMs在浮点错误检测上表现良好，但对微妙数值错误（如下溢、取消）的检测仍需改进。

中文摘要：本文研究了大型语言模型（LLMs）在软件代码中静态检测和分类浮点错误的能力。我们引入了InterFLOPBench，一个包含90个C内核和1 130个测试样本的基准测试，旨在评估LLMs在六类浮点错误上的表现：取消、比较、除零、溢出、下溢和NaN，并在14个LLMs之间进行比较。评估框架将浮点错误检测视为多标签分类问题，并使用F1分数指标来衡量性能。结果表明，最新模型（Qwen 3 32b、Gemini 2.5 Flash、Phi 4 Reasoning、DeepSeek R1T2以及gpt-oss 20b和120b）的整体F1分数达到0.88以上。不同错误类别之间的性能存在差异，例如显式操作如除零（平均F1分数：0.8479）与更微妙的数值现象如下溢（平均F1分数：0.6059）和取消（平均F1分数：0.6164）。

Original abstract: This paper investigates the capability of Large Language Models (LLMs) to detect and classify floating-point errors statically in software code. We introduce InterFLOPBench, a benchmark of 90 C kernels with 1 130 test samples designed to evaluate LLMs across six categories of floating-point error: cancellation, comparison, division by zero, overflow, underflow and NaN, compared across 14 LLMs. The evaluation framework treats floating-point error detection as a multi-label classification problem and employs the F1-score metric to measure performance. Results demonstrate that latest models (Qwen 3 32b, Gemini 2.5 Flash, Phi 4 Reasoning, DeepSeek R1T2, and gpt-oss 20b and 120b) achieve a performance greater than 0.88 overall F1-score. Performance varies between error categories, between explicit operations such as division by zero (Average F1-score: 0.8479) and more subtle numerical phenomena such as underflow (Average F1-score: 0.6059) and cancellation (Average F1-score: 0.6164).

### [44] [ReGRPO: Reflection-Augmented Policy Optimization for Tool-Using Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31392v1)
*Binjie Zhang,Mike Zheng Shou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: ReGRPO：反思增强的RL用于工具agent，高度相关

TL;DR: 提出ReGRPO框架，通过反思引导纠正训练工具增强VLM以提升鲁棒性，在GTA/GAIA上达到SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具增强VLM在失败后缺乏恢复信号，SFT仅依赖成功轨迹，RL奖励稀疏难以定位失败步骤。

Method: 构建反思数据引擎生成失败三元组，用其进行SFT预热，再通过组相对优势联合优化反思与纠正动作，并加入反思成本项。

Result: 在相同骨干与工具集下，ReGRPO在GTA和GAIA上持续优于强开源基线，取得最佳结果。

Conclusion: 反思引导的纠正机制能显著提升工具使用VLM的鲁棒性和性能。

中文摘要：工具增强的视觉语言模型（VLM）可以通过调用外部工具解决多模态、多步骤任务，但在实践中仍然脆弱。现有工作存在两个常见缺陷。监督微调（SFT）主要基于成功轨迹构建，在工具失败后几乎没有恢复信号，而稀疏的轨迹级强化学习奖励对哪一步失败以及如何修复提供的指导有限。我们提出了ReGRPO（反思增强的组相对策略优化），这是一个在工具使用智能体中学习反思引导纠正的框架。ReGRPO从一个结构化的反思数据引擎开始：我们执行近乎失败的动作以收集基于实际的失败观察，然后构建反思思维三元组（错误类型、证据、修复计划），并与纠正后的动作配对用于预热SFT。然后，我们使用组相对优势在局部轨迹内联合优化反思令牌和纠正动作，并加入反思成本项以减少不必要的反思。在GTA和GAIA上的实验表明，在相同的骨干网络和工具套件下，ReGRPO持续优于强开源基线，并在比较的开源控制器中取得了最佳结果。代码和RoT数据可在https://github.com/showlab/ReGRPO获取。

Original abstract: Tool-augmented vision-language models (VLMs) can solve multimodal, multi-step tasks by calling external tools, yet they remain fragile in practice. Existing works have two common gaps. Supervised fine-tuning (SFT) is built mostly on successful trajectories and offers little signal for recovery after tool failures, while sparse trajectory-level RL rewards provide limited guidance on which step failed and how to repair it. We introduce ReGRPO (Reflection-augmented Group Relative Policy Optimization), a framework that learns reflection-guided correction in tool-using agents. ReGRPO starts with a structured reflective data engine: we execute near-miss actions to collect grounded failure observations, then build Reflection-of-Thought triplets (ErrorType, Evidence, FixPlan) paired with corrected actions for warm-start SFT. We then optimize reflection tokens and corrective actions jointly within local trajectories using group-relative advantages, and include a reflection-cost term to reduce unnecessary reflection. Experiments on GTA and GAIA show that, under the same backbone and tool suite, ReGRPO consistently outperforms strong open-source baselines and achieves the best results among the compared open-source controllers. Code and RoT data are available at https://github.com/showlab/ReGRPO.

### [45] [World-Model Collapse as a Phase Transition](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31399v2)
*Xinyuan Song,Zekun Cai*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 长程语言agent世界模型崩溃研究，直接针对agent瓶颈

TL;DR: 长时域语言代理在隐式世界模型中存在类似水沸腾的相变现象，在临界边界附近微小的变化会导致世界模型突然崩溃。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究长时域语言代理是否在隐式世界模型中存在类似于水沸腾的相变，即从近似不变到突然崩溃的转变。

Method: 在具有精确每步黄金状态的确定性任务族中，通过大规模网格搜索状态基数、依赖密度、时域、分支、观察模式和突变率等参数，绘制相图，并分析每步跟踪。

Result: 相图显示存在已解决高原、窄过渡带和崩溃底部；世界状态保真度先于动作有效性失效，导致代理从被破坏的世界中行动；更强的模型平移临界边界但不消除定性转变。

Conclusion: 世界模型崩溃是长时域代理的一个可衡量的瓶颈。

中文摘要：水在变暖时看起来没有变化，然后在某个临界点它沸腾了。我们探究长时域语言代理是否在其隐式世界模型中也表现出类似的转变。在一些参数设置下，稍微改变状态负载或增加一个步骤的时域，行为几乎不变；在临界边界附近，同样的微小变化会导致突然的世界崩溃。我们在一个具有精确每步黄金状态的确定性任务族中研究了这一效应。对状态基数、依赖密度、时域、分支、观察模式和突变率的大规模网格搜索揭示了一个相图：一个已解决的高原、一个狭窄的过渡带和一个崩溃底部。每步跟踪显示了机制：世界状态保真度在动作有效性之前失效，因此代理不仅仅是选择了坏动作；它是从一个被破坏的世界中行动的。更强的模型平移了临界边界，但没有消除定性的转变。这些结果使世界模型崩溃成为长时域代理的一个可衡量的瓶颈。

Original abstract: Water looks unchanged as it warms, then at a critical point it boils. We ask whether long-horizon language agents show an analogous transition in their implicit world models. In some parameter settings, changing state load by a small amount, or adding a single step of horizon, leaves behavior nearly unchanged; near a critical boundary, the same small change causes a sudden world collapse. We study this effect in a deterministic task family with exact per-step gold state. A large grid search over state cardinality, dependency density, horizon, branching, observation mode, and mutation rate reveals a phase diagram: a solved plateau, a narrow transition band, and a collapse floor. Per-step traces show the mechanism: world-state fidelity fails before action validity, so the agent is not merely choosing a bad action; it is acting from a corrupted world. Stronger models translate the critical boundary but do not remove the qualitative transition. These results make world-model collapse a measurable bottleneck for long-horizon agents.

### [46] [Wisdom Of The (AI) Crowd: Investigating Artificial Swarm Intelligence In Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31404v1)
*Justin Brenne,Christian Meske*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM群体智能聚合，多agent协作方法

TL;DR: 本研究通过实验验证了通过模型内和模型间聚合，LLMs可以显著降低估计误差，并且LLMs在评估不确定性时具有元认知意识。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类群体智能成本高、协调难，研究旨在检验LLMs是否可通过人工群体模拟群体智能，填补AI聚合机制的理解空白。

Result: 聚合策略使MAPE最高降低37个百分点，相对置信区间宽度与估计误差呈正相关（ρ=0.242-0.568，p<0.001）。

Conclusion: LLMs群体可有效用于组织决策，具有元认知能力，研究提供了实践指导。

中文摘要：人类群体智能展示了显著的集体准确性，但在成本、协调和时间方面面临可扩展性限制。我们研究大型语言模型（LLMs）是否可以通过人工群体来近似群体智能效应，从而解决理解基于AI的聚合机制的关键空白。我们进行了一项受控实验，使用960个手动执行的提示，涉及三个专有模型（GPT-5、Gemini 2.5 Pro、Claude Sonnet 4.5），在八个估计任务上测试了模型内采样和模型间聚合。结果显示，通过模型内和模型间聚合，误差持续降低，不同聚合策略下MAPE显著降低高达37个百分点。我们观察到相对置信区间宽度与相对估计误差之间的正相关性具有小到大的效应量（Spearman的ρ=0.242-0.568，所有p<0.001），表明LLMs在评估不确定性时具有元认知意识。我们讨论了研究和实践的意义，为在组织决策中部署LLM群体提供了可操作的见解。

Original abstract: Human swarm intelligence demonstrates remarkable collective accuracy but faces scalability constraints in cost, coordination, and time. We investigate whether large language models (LLMs) can approximate swarm intelligence effects through artificial swarms, addressing a critical gap in understanding AI-based aggregation mechanisms. We conducted a controlled experiment with 960 manually executed prompts across three proprietary models (GPT-5, Gemini 2.5 Pro, Claude Sonnet 4.5), testing intra-model sampling and inter-model aggregation on eight estimation tasks. Results reveal consistent error reduction through intra- and inter-model aggregation, with significant error reductions up to 37 percentage points in MAPE across different aggregation strategies. We observed small to large effect sizes for positive correlations (Spearman's $ρ=0.242-0.568$, all $p<0.001$) between relative confidence interval widths and relative estimation errors, suggesting LLMs possess metacognitive awareness when assessing uncertainty. We discuss implications for research and practice, providing actionable insights for deploying LLM swarms in organizational decision-making.

### [47] [Xiaomi-GUI-0 Technical Report](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31410v2)
*Wanxia Cao,Chengzhen Duan,Pei Fu,Pengzhi Gao,Niu Lian,Fazhan Liu,Hui Liu,Heng Qu,Qinzhuo Wu,Zhehao Yu,Tongbo Chen,Shiqi Cui,Anan Du,Shukai Jia,Yuanfa Li,Wei Liu,Yike Liu,Wenchao Lu,Zhenbo Luo,Haoyuan Sun,Jiatong Sun,Cheng Tan,Yajie Wang,Changqiao Wu,Tao Xiong,Jiahui Yang,Yuxuan Yuan,Ruoceng Zhang,Shaojie Zhang,Jian Zhu,Jian Luan,Cong Zou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 真实环境GUI agent，直接相关coding agent

TL;DR: 提出Xiaomi-GUI-0，一个在真实设备闭环中训练和评估的多模态GUI代理，通过真实设备主导的混合基础设施、多源数据飞轮和三阶段训练，在真实移动环境中取得72.0%和78.9%的成功率，显著提升执行稳定性和异常状态识别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GUI代理在模拟环境和标准化基准上训练评估，与真实应用在布局、交互逻辑和异常状态分布上存在巨大差异，导致基准分数与实际可用性之间存在持续差距，无法真实反映执行稳定性。

Method: 提出真实设备主导的混合基础设施（物理设备为主、沙箱为辅），构建多源训练数据（高频任务、长尾意图、能力增强）和错误驱动数据飞轮，采用三阶段训练流水线（监督微调、步骤级强化学习、智能体强化学习）。

Result: 在内部RealMobile上达到72.0%成功率，在AndroidWorld上达到78.9%成功率，同时在真实世界任务中显著提高了执行稳定性和异常状态识别。

Conclusion: Xiaomi-GUI-0通过真实设备闭环训练和多源数据飞轮有效缩小了基准与真实可用性之间的差距，实现了在真实移动环境中的高成功率和稳定性。

中文摘要：图形用户界面（GUI）代理基于视觉语言模型，通过点击、滑动、文本输入和导航等界面操作，在真实应用中端到端完成用户任务。然而，现有的GUI代理主要基于离线轨迹、模拟环境和标准化基准进行训练和评估。这些与真实应用在界面布局、交互逻辑和异常状态分布上存在显著差异，无法真实反映实际使用中的执行稳定性——在真实世界中，账户状态、权限对话框、支付认证和风险控制不断重塑状态分布，导致基准分数与实际可用性之间存在持续差距。为缩小这一差距，我们提出了Xiaomi-GUI-0，一个面向真实移动环境的原生多模态GUI代理，在真实设备闭环内进行训练和评估。其核心是一个以真实设备为主的混合基础设施，物理设备作为主要执行环境，沙箱提供辅助支持，使得数据收集、训练、部署和评估共享接近实际部署的执行分布。我们构建了涵盖高频头部任务、长尾意图的高泛化数据以及反思和记忆的能力增强数据的多源训练数据，并引入了一个错误驱动的数据飞轮，将失败轨迹转化为纠正动作、反思解释和恢复演示。该模型通过一个渐进的三阶段流水线进行训练：监督微调、步骤级强化学习和智能体强化学习。在公开基准和我们的内部RealMobile上评估，Xiaomi-GUI-0在RealMobile上达到72.0%的成功率，在AndroidWorld上达到78.9%，同时在真实世界任务中显著提高了执行稳定性和异常状态识别。

Original abstract: Graphical user interface (GUI) agents build on vision-language models to complete user tasks end-to-end in real applications through interface actions such as tapping, swiping, text entry, and navigation. However, existing GUI agents are trained and evaluated largely on offline trajectories, simulated environments, and standardized benchmarks. These differ substantially from real applications in interface layout, interaction logic, and abnormal-state distribution, and cannot faithfully characterize execution stability in real-world use, where account states, permission dialogs, payment authentication, and risk control continually reshape the state distribution and open a persistent gap between benchmark scores and real usability. To close this gap, we propose Xiaomi-GUI-0, a native multimodal GUI agent for real mobile environments, trained and evaluated within a real-device closed loop. At its core is a real-device-dominant hybrid infrastructure, where physical devices are the primary execution environment and sandboxes provide auxiliary support, so that data collection, training, rollout, and evaluation share an execution distribution close to real deployment. We construct multi-source training data spanning high-frequency head tasks, high-generalization data for long-tail intents, and capability-enhancement data for reflection and memory, and introduce an error-driven data flywheel that turns failure trajectories into corrected actions, reflective explanations, and recovery demonstrations. The model is trained through a progressive three-stage pipeline of supervised fine-tuning, step-level reinforcement learning, and agentic reinforcement learning. Evaluated on public benchmarks and our in-house RealMobile, Xiaomi-GUI-0 achieves 72.0% success on RealMobile and 78.9% on AndroidWorld, while substantially improving execution stability and abnormal-state recognition in real-world tasks.

</details>


### [48] [Ask the World Before Acting: Environment Probing for Calibrated Agent World Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31422v2)
*Xinyuan Song,Zekun Cai*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出环境探测策略校准agent世界模型，直接贡献agent规划与信念维护

TL;DR: 提出EnvProbe策略，通过预算化环境探测修复智能体信念漂移，提升长时程任务准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长时程语言智能体的信念漂移无法通过推理或自我反思修复，需主动探测环境证据，但探测有代价，需优化决策。

Method: 将环境探测建模为预算决策问题，提出EnvProbe评分策略，综合任务关键性、信念陈旧性、不确定性及依赖角色，选择最优查询字段。

Result: 在三个受控环境中，EnvProbe相比周期性探测提升终端准确率：程序性任务11.76%，空间任务3.79%，总体6.45%。

Conclusion: 智能体校准应作为环境证据驱动的动作选择问题，而非仅模型内部推理；任务结构信息比自报不确定性更可靠。

中文摘要：在长时程中行动的具身智能体必须维护关于工具状态、物体位置、图边和子目标依赖的信念。当这些信念发生偏离时，无论是更长的推理轨迹还是普通的自我反思都无法修复失败，因为缺失的证据存在于环境中。我们将环境探测形式化为结构化智能体世界模型的一个预算决策问题：在执行动作之前，智能体可以查询一个信念字段的当前值，更新其表格，并支付一个交互步骤。我们提出了EnvProbe，一种简单的评分策略，结合了任务关键性、陈旧性、口头表达的不确定性以及依赖角色。一个类型分层分析将信念修复的收益与置换的任务动作成本分开，并预测了程序性信念和空间信念的不同行为。在三个具有黄金信念状态的受控环境中，EnvProbe在终端世界状态准确率上比周期性探测提高了程序性工具依赖任务11.76个百分点，空间任务3.79个百分点，总体6.45个百分点。消融实验表明，任务结构项是收益的主要来源，而自我报告的不确定性在自信的错误信念下不可靠。结果表明，智能体校准应被视为一个基于环境证据的动作选择问题，而不仅仅是模型内部的推理问题。

Original abstract: Language agents acting over long horizons must maintain beliefs about tool states, object locations, graph edges, and subgoal dependencies. When these beliefs drift, failures can be fixed neither by longer reasoning traces nor by ordinary self-reflection, since the missing evidence lies in the environment. We formulate environment probing as a budgeted decision problem for structured agent world models: before acting, the agent may query the current value of one belief field, update its table, and pay one interaction step. We introduce EnvProbe, a simple scoring policy that combines task criticality, staleness, verbalized uncertainty, and dependency role. A type-stratified analysis separates the benefit of belief repair from the cost of displaced task actions and predicts different behavior for procedural and spatial beliefs. In three controlled environments with gold belief states, EnvProbe improves terminal world-state accuracy over periodic probing by 11.76 percentage points on procedural tool-dependency tasks, 3.79 points on spatial tasks, and 6.45 points overall. Ablations show that task-structural terms are the main source of the gains, while self-reported uncertainty is unreliable under confident wrong beliefs. The results suggest that agent calibration should be treated as an action-selection problem over environment evidence, not only as a model-internal reasoning problem.

</details>


### [49] [CDR-Bench: Evaluating Faithful Execution of Compositional, Order-Sensitive Data Refinement Recipes](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31435v1)
*Yuchen Huang,Xiang Li,Zhenqing Ling,Sijia Li,Qianli Shen,Daoyuan Chen,Yi R. Fung,Yaliang Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 评估LLM执行组成有序数据精炼配方的benchmark，启发agent多步任务评测

TL;DR: 提出CDR-Bench基准测试，发现LLM在组合性和顺序敏感的数据精炼任务中表现不佳，缺乏过程忠实性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准无法评估LLM直接执行组合性、顺序敏感的数据精炼配方的能力。

Method: 构建包含3,462个任务、四个领域、29个算子的CDR-Bench，在原子、顺序无关和顺序敏感设置下评估LLM。

Result: 10多个LLM在组合设置中性能下降，顺序敏感配方成功率低。

Conclusion: 当前LLM缺乏可靠组合数据精炼所需的过程忠实性。

中文摘要：数据精炼涉及在多步配方中执行不断演变的文本状态，其中处理算子的组合和执行顺序共同决定结果。现有基准要么孤立地处理文本编辑，要么将其与代码和工具执行纠缠在一起，尚不清楚LLM是否能直接且忠实地执行这些组合性、对顺序敏感的数据精炼配方。为填补这一空白，我们引入了CDR-Bench，一个全面的基准测试，包含3,462个高质量任务，涵盖四个真实世界数据精炼领域和29个不同算子。我们的基准在原子设置、顺序无关设置和顺序敏感设置下评估模型，利用确定性参考输出进行精确评估。在10多个最先进的LLM上的实验揭示了一致的失败模式：在组合设置中性能急剧下降，顺序敏感的配方成功率崩溃。这些发现突显了当前LLM缺乏可靠组合数据精炼所需的过程忠实性。

Original abstract: Data refinement involves executing multi-step recipes over evolving text states, where both composition and execution order of processing operators determine the outcome. While existing benchmarks either isolate text editing or entangle it with code and tool execution, it remains unclear whether LLMs can directly and faithfully execute these compositional, order-sensitive data refinement recipes. To fill this gap, we introduce CDR-Bench, a comprehensive benchmark featuring 3,462 high-quality tasks spanning four real-world data refinement domains and 29 distinct operators. Our benchmark evaluates models across atomic, order-agnostic, and order-sensitive settings, leveraging deterministic reference outputs to enable exact evaluation. Experiments on 10+ state-of-the-art LLMs reveal consistent failure patterns: performance degrades sharply in compositional settings, and order-sensitive recipe success collapses. These findings underline that current LLMs lack the procedural faithfulness required for reliable compositional data refinement.

### [50] [CSTrader: A Testbed for Language-Grounded Trading in a Community-Driven Virtual Asset Market](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31461v1)
*Yao Shi,Kingfung Luo,Nan Tang,Yuyu Luo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多智能体交易框架，包含规划、风险控制等组件，可迁移至一般agent设计

TL;DR: 提出CSTrader多智能体框架，在CS2皮肤市场中利用LLM和多种信号实现7.58%的累计收益，优于下跌市场指数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建CSTrader多智能体框架，集成技术分析、流动性、事件、反向情感等信号，并通过风险控制和交易摩擦智能体生成交易决策。

Result: 在真实高波动数据上，CSTrader实现最高7.58%累计收益，而市场指数下跌15.62%，且优于简单LLM基线。

Conclusion: 流动性、反向情感和交易摩擦智能体是关键组件；利基语言驱动市场可作为语言到行动研究的有用基准。

中文摘要：利基资产市场，例如《反恐精英2》（CS2）武器皮肤，规模小、波动大，且严重受社区讨论和平台规则驱动。这些特性使得传统量化模型难以处理，但却为研究大型语言模型（LLM）如何将非结构化文本转化为交易行为提供了理想测试平台。本文提出CSTrader，一个用于CS2皮肤市场中语言驱动交易的多智能体框架。该系统首先整合来自多种来源的异构信号，然后使用专门智能体进行技术分析、流动性分析、事件分析和（反向）情感分析，最后应用风险控制、交易摩擦和投资组合管理智能体，在真实交易摩擦下生成买入、卖出或持有决策。我们构建了一个类似实时的评估环境，使用高波动时期的真实CS2数据，并评估了多种最新LLM骨干模型。在所有模型中，CSTrader均持续优于下跌的市场指数（-15.62%）和简单的单提示LLM基线，在可控风险下实现了高达7.58%的累计收益。消融研究表明，流动性、反向情感和交易摩擦智能体对于将嘈杂的语言信号转化为稳定利润至关重要，这表明利基、语言驱动的市场可作为未来语言到行动研究的有用基准。代码可在以下网址获取：https://github.com/IatomicreactorI/CSGOTrading?tab=readme-ov-file#quick-start

Original abstract: Niche asset markets, such as Counter-Strike 2 (CS2) weapon skins, are small, volatile, and heavily driven by community discussions and platform rules. These properties make them hard for traditional quantitative models, but provide an ideal testbed for studying how large language models (LLMs) turn unstructured text into trading actions. We present CSTrader, a multi-agent framework for language-grounded trading in the CS2 skin market. The system first integrates heterogeneous signals from various sources, then uses specialized agents for technical analysis, liquidity, events, and (reversed) sentiment, and finally applies risk control, transaction friction, and portfolio management agents to produce buy, sell, or hold decisions under realistic trading frictions. We build a live-like evaluation environment with real CS2 data from a highly volatile period and evaluate several recent LLM backbones. Across models, CSTrader consistently outperforms both a falling market index (-15.62%) and simple single-prompt LLM baselines, achieving up to a 7.58% cumulative return with controlled risk. Ablation studies show that liquidity, reversed sentiment, and transaction friction agents are crucial for turning noisy language signals into stable profits, suggesting that niche, language-driven markets are a useful benchmark for future language-to-action research. Code is available at: https://github.com/IatomicreactorI/CSGOTrading?tab=readme-ov-file#quick-start

### [51] [One Reflection Is Not Enough: Self-Correcting Autonomous Research via Multi-Hypothesis Failure Attribution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31478v1)
*Jie Ma,Binfei Chu,Jie Gao,Jinlu Zhang,Yiwei Ma,Yi Tan,Jiayi Ji,Xiaoshuai Sun,Rongrong Ji*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出多假设失败归因的自我纠正研究agent，直接贡献agent反思与结构化修复

TL;DR: SAGE通过结构化故障归因和约束报告机制，显著提升了自主科研智能体在实验失败时的恢复能力和工件质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自主研究智能体在实验失败时依赖单一自由反思进行恢复，导致局部试错或丢弃有用上下文，恢复效果脆弱。

Method: SAGE核心是Multi-Hypothesis Failure Attribution (MHFA)，通过分析动态轨迹特征生成多证据解释、独立评估严重性并确定路由到正确干预级别；同时采用基于上下文的报告机制约束结果至实测值。

Result: 在12主题5领域基准上，指标输出从42%提升至92%，工件质量从5.00升至6.75/10，盲评超过AI-Scientist-v2（52.0 vs 48.2），优势在代码开发和执行。

Conclusion: SAGE通过结构化恢复与明确约束的结合，显著超越整体反思范式，为自主研究建立了高度可信的基础。

中文摘要：自主研究智能体现在可以起草假设、编写代码、运行实验并撰写论文，但当实验失败时它们仍然脆弱。在主流范式下，故障恢复通常委托给单一的自由形式反思：一个丰富的度量、日志和设计选择轨迹被压缩成一个口头批评，这往往导致局部的试错或硬性转向，丢弃有用的上下文。我们提出SAGE，一个自我纠正、自主、基于实验的实验者，以解决这一故障恢复瓶颈。其核心机制，多假设故障归因（MHFA），将恢复视为结构化的因果诊断。通过分析动态轨迹特征，MHFA系统地生成多个基于证据的故障解释，独立评估其严重性，并将验证的根因确定性地路由到正确的干预级别（假设、实验设计或实现）。为了保证科学诚实性，SAGE进一步采用基于上下文的报告机制，明确地将起草的结果约束为实际测量值，删除幻觉数字。在一个12主题、5领域的基准测试中，SAGE将产生指标的输出从42%提高到92%，超过反思基线，将工件质量从5.00提高到6.75/10，并且在盲评中超过AI-Scientist-v2（52.0对48.2），优势集中在代码开发和执行上。虽然完全自主的科学写作和生成会议级论文对整个领域来说仍然是臭名昭著的困难开放问题，但SAGE成功地生成了显著更可靠和更高质量的科研工件。最终，通过将结构化恢复与明确的约束相结合，SAGE显著优于整体反思范式，为未来的自主研究建立了高度可信的基础。

Original abstract: Autonomous research agents can now draft hypotheses, write code, run experiments, and produce papers, but they remain brittle when experiments fail. Under the prevailing paradigm, failure recovery is usually delegated to a single free-form reflection: a rich trajectory of metrics, logs, and design choices is compressed into one verbal critique, which often leads either to localized trial-and-error or to hard pivots that discard useful context. We propose SAGE, a Self-correcting, Autonomous, Grounded Experimenter, to tackle this failure-recovery bottleneck. Its core mechanism, Multi-Hypothesis Failure Attribution (MHFA), treats recovery as a structured causal diagnosis. By analyzing dynamic trajectory features, MHFA systematically generates multiple evidence-grounded explanations for a failure, independently evaluates their severity, and deterministically routes the verified root cause to the correct intervention level (hypothesis, experimental design, or implementation). To guarantee scientific honesty, SAGE further employs a grounded reporting mechanism that explicitly constrains drafted results to actual measured values, redacting hallucinated numbers. On a 12-topic, 5-domain benchmark, SAGE increases metrics-bearing outputs from 42% to 92% over a reflection baseline, improves artifact quality from 5.00 to 6.75/10, and blindly outscores AI-Scientist-v2 (52.0 vs. 48.2), with gains concentrated in code development and execution. While fully autonomous scientific writing and generating conference-ready papers remain notoriously difficult open problems for the entire field, SAGE successfully produces significantly more reliable and higher-quality scientific artifacts. Ultimately, by coupling structured recovery with explicit grounding constraints, SAGE significantly outperforms monolithic reflection paradigms, establishing a highly trustworthy foundation for future autonomous research.

</details>


### [52] [Surprise as a Signal for Plasticity and Metacognition](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31495v1)
*Louis Mouchon*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 利用惊讶信号作为可塑性与元认知的机制，可启发agent记忆与自我改进

TL;DR: 同一预测误差信号在两种系统中分别用于控制情景记忆的写入和调节视觉-语言模型的行为，实现了持续学习中的记忆保留和少样本学习，以及基于不确定性的主动学习和记忆巩固。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索单一的预测误差信号如何同时作为可塑性门控和元认知基础，以解决持续学习中的灾难性遗忘和提升模型在不确定情况下的适应性行为。

Method: 构建两个系统：1) 非参数情景记忆使用冻结编码器上的小型预测器计算惊喜度，仅在惊喜度高时写入新概念，并通过离线重放整合到慢速线性读取器；2) 在共享文本-图像空间中使用同一惊喜度信号调节视觉-语言模型的回答策略（自信、含糊、拒绝），并实现单次学习。

Result: 对于DINOv2和I-JEPA，重放分别恢复17.7和51.3个点的保留率；少样本5-way 1-shot达到91.6%；新颖性检测AUROC为0.966，远高于模型自身置信度0.618；睡眠后回忆99.2%的事实，而基础模型为0%。

Conclusion: 该预测误差信号在两种系统中均有效，作为概念验证展示了其在持续学习和主动学习中的潜力，但存在局限性，需进一步研究其可扩展性和实际应用。

中文摘要：我们研究了一个在两种设置中相同的想法：由冻结编码器潜在空间上的小型预测器计算的预测误差信号，既可以作为可塑性的门控，也可以作为元认知的基质。在第一个系统中，非参数化情景记忆仅当这种惊喜度较高时才写入新概念，并且定期的离线重放阶段将最近的痕迹整合到慢速线性读取器中。在具有冻结的DINOv2或I-JEPA骨干网络的1000个ImageNet类别的持续流上，整合阶段对于DINOv2恢复了17.7个点的最旧类别保留率，对于I-JEPA恢复了51.3个点（单种子运行），消融实验表明仅重放最近窗口比不重放更差。在少样本评估中，相同记忆在5-way 1-shot mini-ImageNet上达到91.6%，高于任务特定基线，而更困难的500-way设置暴露了真正的难度。在第二个系统中，相同的惊喜信号在共享文本-图像空间中计算，调节视觉-语言模型的行为：当概念已知时自信地回答，部分熟悉时含糊其辞，当概念新颖时拒绝识别物体并请求解释，通过单个用户话语学习该概念。外部检测器以0.966的AUROC（95%置信区间±0.024）区分已知和新颖概念，远高于模型自身的口头化置信度（0.618），而其令牌级置信度在贪婪解码下低于随机水平；经过清空快速存储的睡眠阶段后，系统从整合存储中回忆了五十个已教导事实的99.2%，而基础模型未恢复任何事实。我们报告这两个系统作为概念验证，并明确局限性，将第二个系统与最近的情景记忆和个性化VLM工作进行对比。

Original abstract: We study a single idea across two settings: that a prediction-error signal, computed by a small predictor over the latent space of a frozen encoder, can serve both as a gate on plasticity and as a substrate for metacognition. In the first system, a non-parametric episodic memory writes a new concept only when this surprise is high, and a periodic offline replay phase consolidates recent traces into a slow linear readout. On a continual stream of 1000 ImageNet classes with a frozen DINOv2 or I-JEPA backbone, the consolidation phase recovers 17.7 points of retention on the oldest classes for DINOv2 and 51.3 points for I-JEPA (single-seed runs), and an ablation shows that replaying only a recent window is worse than no replay at all. In few-shot evaluation the same memory reaches 91.6% on 5-way 1-shot mini-ImageNet, above a task-specific baseline, while a harder 500-way regime exposes the true difficulty. In the second system, the same surprise signal, computed in a shared text-image space, modulates the behaviour of a vision-language model: it answers assertively when a concept is known, hedges when it is partially familiar, and refuses to identify the object and asks for an explanation when it is novel, learning the concept from a single user utterance. The external detector separates known from novel concepts at an AUROC of 0.966 (95% CI +/-0.024), far above the model's own verbalised confidence (0.618), while its token-level confidence sits below chance under greedy decoding; after a sleep phase that empties the fast store, the system recalls 99.2% of fifty taught facts from the consolidated store while a base model recovers none. We report both systems as proof-of-concept, with explicit limitations, and position the second against recent episodic-memory and personalised-VLM work.

</details>

### [54] [Modality-Driven Search with Holistic Trace Judging for ARC-AGI-2](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31543v1)
*Johan Land*

Selection reason: 多模态推理求解器，包含代码通道，对agent多模态搜索与评判有启发。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在抽象推理中常生成流畅但错误的推理，需要有效的候选选择机制，而现有自一致性或多数投票等方法在模态答案错误时失效。

Method: 两个核心原则：1) 将推理模态（文本、图像、代码）作为搜索算子，独立生成多样候选；2) 上下文保留的整体评判，在单长提示中联合比较所有候选推理轨迹。

Result: 在半私有评估集上达到72.9%（$38.99/任务），超过GPT-5.2 Pro（54.2%）和Gemini 3 Pro（54.0%）18.7个百分点；公共集上76.1%（$19.69/任务）。

Conclusion: 该方法有效提升正确假设的恢复能力，开源代码并发现规定性提示和迭代细化会降低多样性，为未来工作提供指导。

中文摘要：大型语言模型能够在抽象推理任务中生成流畅、内部一致的推理轨迹，但仍然自信地犯错——因此，在候选方案中进行选择（而不仅仅是生成）成为核心挑战。我提出了一个针对ARC-AGI-2（一个少样本视觉推理基准）的求解器，它基于两个原则：(i) 将推理模态视为搜索算子，通过文本、图像和代码通道独立生成多样化的候选方案；(ii) 上下文保留的整体评判，其中评判模型在单个长上下文提示中联合比较所有候选推理轨迹。与自一致性或多数投票不同，该方法能够在模态答案错误的任务中可靠地恢复正确的少数假设。在ARC Prize半私有评估集上，该求解器以每个任务38.99美元的成本达到72.9%的准确率——这是当时经过验证的排行榜上的最高分，超过了最好的独立前沿模型GPT-5.2 Pro（54.2%）和Gemini 3 Pro（54.0%），高出18.7个百分点。在公共评估集上，它达到76.1%的准确率，每个任务成本19.69美元。我发布了完整的源代码，并记录了大量的负面结果，包括发现规定性提示模板和迭代细化会系统地降低假设多样性并损害性能。

Original abstract: Large language models can produce fluent, internally coherent reasoning traces for abstract reasoning tasks while still being confidently wrong - making selection among candidates, not just generation, the central challenge. I present a solver for ARC-AGI-2, a few-shot visual reasoning benchmark, built around two principles: (i) treating reasoning modalities as search operators, generating diverse candidates independently across text, image, and code channels, and (ii) context-preserving holistic judging, in which a judge model jointly compares all candidate reasoning traces within a single long-context prompt. Unlike self-consistency or majority voting, this approach reliably recovers correct minority hypotheses on tasks where the modal answer is wrong.
  On the ARC Prize semi-private evaluation set, the solver achieves 72.9 percent at USD 38.99 per task - the highest score on the verified leaderboard at the time of writing, exceeding the best standalone frontier models, GPT-5.2 Pro at 54.2 percent and Gemini 3 Pro at 54.0 percent, by +18.7 percentage points. On the public evaluation set, it achieves 76.1 percent at USD 19.69 per task. I release the full source code and document extensive negative results, including the finding that prescriptive prompting templates and iterative refinement systematically reduce hypothesis diversity and degrade performance.

</details>


### [55] [ACE: Pluggable Adaptive Context Elasticizer across Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31564v1)
*Ning Liao,Zihao Long,Xiaoxing Wang,Xue Yang,Yaoming Wang,Ziyuan Zhuang,Xunliang Cai,Rongxiang Weng,Junchi Yan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自适应上下文弹性器，直接用于LLM agent上下文管理，可插拔模块。

TL;DR: 提出ACE模块，通过可逆的上下文弹性化策略，在不丢失关键信息的情况下优化LLM代理的上下文使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有上下文管理技术（截断、摘要）的不可逆性导致关键信息丢失，无法满足长轨迹任务需求。

Method: 提出ACE模块，包含无损消息维护层和上下文编排层，动态为每个历史步骤分配类型（原始、抽象或丢弃），实现可逆的上下文弹性化。

Result: 在四个代理框架上，ACE始终优于截断和摘要基线，带来一致性能提升。

Conclusion: ACE是一种有效的、无需训练的即插即用模块，解决了长轨迹LLM代理的上下文管理问题。

中文摘要：代理任务日益复杂导致轨迹长度快速增长，这给基于固定上下文窗口的大型语言模型（LLM）代理带来了重大挑战。现有的上下文管理技术（如截断和摘要）存在固有的不灵活性和不可逆性：一旦信息被丢弃或压缩，即使它在后续决策步骤中变得关键相关，也无法恢复。为了解决这些局限性，我们提出了自适应上下文弹性化器（ACE），一个即插即用模块，它在每个决策步骤弹性地编排历史步骤信息到代理的上下文中。ACE维护了一个无损消息维护层，存储每个历史步骤的原始消息和压缩抽象，同时一个上下文编排层根据当前任务状态，在每个决策步骤自适应地为每个步骤分配弹性类型（原始、抽象或丢弃）。这种可逆设计确保主LLM始终接收到紧凑但信息丰富的上下文。我们将ACE适应于四个不同的代理框架，包括ReAct、DeepAgent、WebThinker和MiroFlow，无需训练或架构修改。实验表明，ACE始终优于截断和摘要基线，并在所有四个代理框架上带来一致的性能提升。

Original abstract: The increasing complexity of agentic tasks has led to rapidly growing trajectory lengths, which poses significant challenges for large language model (LLM) based agents with fixed context windows. Existing context management techniques, such as truncation and summarization, suffer from inherent inflexibility and irreversibility: once information is discarded or compressed, it cannot be recovered even when it becomes critically relevant in later decision steps. To address these limitations, we propose the Adaptive Context Elasticizer (ACE), a plug-and-play module that elastically orchestrates historical step information into the agent's context at each decision step. ACE maintains a lossless message maintenance layer that stores both raw messages and compressed abstractions for each historical step, while a context orchestration layer adaptively assigns each step an elastic type as raw, abstract, or drop, at every decision step based on the current task state. This reversible design ensures that the main LLM always receives a compact yet information-rich context. We adapt ACE to four diverse agent frameworks, including ReAct, DeepAgent, WebThinker, and MiroFlow, without training or architectural modifications. Experiments show that ACE consistently outperforms truncation and summarization baselines, and brings consistent performance gains across all four agent frameworks.

</details>


### [56] [Which Tokens Matter? Adaptive Token Selection for RLVR with the Relative Surprisal Index](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31575v1)
*Outongyi Lv,Yanzhao Zheng,Yuanwei Zhang,Zhenghao Huang,Xingjun Wang,Baohua Dong,Hangcheng Zhu,Yingda Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: RLVR token过滤方法，可迁移至agent训练机制。

TL;DR: 本文提出相对惊奇指数（RSI）和RSI选择（RSI-S）方法，通过耦合熵与概率调和RLVR中的矛盾范式，在AIME和AMC基准上提升avg@32准确率2-3%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR研究对高熵词元和低概率词元的重要性存在矛盾观点，且单独评估概率或熵不足以捕捉策略优化动态。

Method: 提出相对惊奇指数（RSI）作为信息论度量，并基于此设计熵自适应词元过滤方法RSI-S，保留稳定RSI区间内的词元。

Result: 在Qwen2.5-1.5B、3B和7B模型上，RSI-S在AIME和AMC基准测试中avg@32准确率相比GRPO提升2-3个百分点。

Conclusion: RSI为RLVR改进提供了有前景的视角，有效调和了先前矛盾的训练范式。

中文摘要：强化学习（RL）已成为推动大型语言模型（LLMs）超越基于模仿的训练，向更强大的推理能力迈进的有力工具。在现有方法中，基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已成为推进LLM推理的关键范式。尽管取得了实证成功，但近期研究提出了不同的见解。一条研究路线主张在训练中优先考虑高熵词元位置，而另一视角则警告不要让低概率词元主导梯度更新。值得注意的是，尽管高熵词元通常与低概率相关，但两种范式在实证上都取得了显著的性能提升。在这项工作中，我们认为单独评估采样词元的概率或熵不足以捕捉策略优化动态。为了解决这一矛盾，我们引入了相对惊奇指数（RSI），这是一种基于信息论的原则性度量，自然地耦合了词元的熵与所选词元的概率。我们表明，在温和条件下，RSI与选定logit扰动下logit梯度范数和预测熵的一阶变分之间的局部比率相关。基于RSI，我们提出了RSI选择（RSI-S），一种熵自适应的词元过滤方法，它保留稳定RSI区间内的词元。RSI-S成功调和了先前矛盾的范式，并过滤掉冗余的低惊奇词元和不稳定的高惊奇尾部词元。实证评估表明，在AIME和AMC基准测试上，RSI-S在不同模型规模（Qwen2.5-1.5B、3B和7B）下实现了更高的avg@32准确率：RSI-S相比GRPO提高了2-3个百分点。总体而言，RSI为RLVR改进提供了一个有前景的视角。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has become a powerful tool for propelling Large Language Models (LLMs) beyond imitation-based training towards more robust reasoning capabilities. Among existing approaches, RL with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has emerged as a pivotal paradigm for advancing LLM reasoning. Despite its empirical success, recent studies have offered different insights. One line of inquiry advocates prioritizing high-entropy token positions during training, while another perspective cautions against allowing low-probability tokens to dominate gradient updates. Notably, although high-entropy tokens are usually correlated with low probability, both paradigms empirically yield substantial performance gains. In this work, we argue that evaluating sampled-token probability or entropy in isolation is insufficient to capture the policy optimization dynamics. To resolve this tension, we introduce the Relative Surprisal Index (RSI), a principled, information-theoretic metric that naturally couples the token's entropy with the probability of the selected token. We show that, under mild conditions, RSI is related to the local ratio between the first-order variations of the logit-gradient norm and predictive entropy under a selected-logit perturbation. Building on RSI, we propose RSI Selection (RSI-S), an entropy-adaptive token filtering method that retains tokens within a stable RSI interval. RSI-S successfully reconciles previous contradictory paradigms and filters out both redundant low-surprisal tokens and unstable high-surprisal tail tokens. Empirical evaluations show that RSI-S achieves higher avg@32 accuracy across different model scales (Qwen2.5-1.5B, 3B, and 7B) on AIME and AMC benchmarks: RSI-S improves avg@32 accuracy by 2--3 percentage points over GRPO. Overall, RSI offers a promising perspective for RLVR improvement.

</details>

Original abstract: We present LuckyStar 111B, a 111B-parameter hybrid reasoning model developed through a collaboration between Cohere and LG CNS for Korean-English enterprise agents under practical memory and serving constraints. The model trains from Cohere's fully post-trained Command A model rather than a new pretraining run, and uses preamble conditioning to switch between concise non-reasoning behavior and longer tool-oriented reasoning. We study four choices for scaling tool-using agents efficiently: multilingual supervised fine-tuning, reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards for multi-step tool-use tasks, language-consistency rewards for Korean user-facing responses, and 4-bit quantization for single-GPU serving. The adapted model improves mathematical reasoning, function calling, and agentic natural-language-to-SQL (NL2SQL) performance while preserving general Korean and English instruction-following quality. These results provide a practical recipe and failure-mode analysis for adapting post-trained multilingual models to verifiable agentic workflows under memory-constrained deployment.

Original abstract: Recent automated research systems show that language-model agents can generate hypotheses, run experiments, and write complete manuscripts, but most evidence still comes from selected examples, human-framed topics, or a few pre-defined research tasks. We present FARS (Fully Automated Research System), a fully automated AI-for-AI research system designed to operate across research topics at scale. FARS autonomously generates and advances projects through ideation, planning, experimentation, and writing, using stage-specific agents coordinated through a shared workspace that records proposals, code, logs, results, and manuscripts. In its first public deployment, FARS produced 166 complete research papers spanning 67 fine-grained AI/ML topics while preserving intermediate artifacts as an auditable corpus rather than a curated set of successes. We evaluate this corpus with 282 structured reviews from volunteer reviewers covering 140 papers, including overall ratings, sub-scores, integrity checks, and LLM-use disclosure. The reviews indicate that FARS can produce review-worthy and occasionally strong AI/ML research artifacts in a large-scale public deployment, while also exposing recurring failure modes in narrow experimental scope, methodological limitations, and integrity issues.

### [59] [A Self-Evolving Agentic System for Automated Generation and Execution of Biological Protocols](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31763v2)
*Yankai Jiang,Weiting Tang,Haoran Sun,Zhenyu Tang,Yuejie Hou,Yingnan Han,Rubo Wang,Yueyuxiao Yang,Cheng Liang,Lilong Wang,Wenjie Lou,Xiaosong Wang,Lei Bai,Meng Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自进化多agent系统用于生物实验协议生成与执行，含通用多agent编排与反馈修正方法。

TL;DR: ProtoPilot是一个自进化多智能体系统，能将湿实验协议自动转化为可执行代码并基于反馈迭代优化，通过专家评估和物理实验验证实现了高通过率和可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有湿实验自动化系统仅生成看似合理的协议文本，未能真正对齐生物学意图、定量程序、设备约束和实验反馈，导致无法实现自主实验。需要一种能够从协议设计到物理执行保持一致性并动态修正的系统。

Method: 开发了ProtoPilot，包含多智能体编排、层间可验证性和运行时更新的技能库；同时构建了基于98个金标准协议的294个任务的评估框架，包括专家评分、设备级门控和真实湿实验测试。

Result: ProtoPilot在Top@3专家偏好率、协议到代码门控通过率和Opentrons通过率上分别达到90.2%、89.5%和88.24%，远超OpenTrons-AI的32.35%；湿实验验证获得可解释读数和Sanger确认产物。

Conclusion: 评估框架有效捕获了自主湿实验自动化的执行需求，ProtoPilot通过将协议和代码生成转化为可验证执行和反馈驱动修订，实现了高可靠性的自主实验。
}

中文摘要：自主湿实验需要不仅仅是看似合理的协议文本：生物学意图、定量程序、设备限制和实验反馈必须从协议和SOP设计到代码和物理执行保持一致。我们开发了ProtoPilot，一个自进化多智能体系统，以及一个专家基础的基准和评估框架，用于测试这种转换作为实验自动化问题。该框架涵盖来自98个金标准协议的294个合成生物学和分子生物学任务，湿实验室专家评分标准，设备级有效性门控和真实实验测试。ProtoPilot包含层间可验证性、多智能体编排和运行时更新的技能库，以生成协议、扩展SOP、合成SDK兼容代码并根据湿实验室反馈修订工作流程。它实现了Top@3专家偏好率90.2%，整体协议到代码门控通过率89.5%，Opentrons通过率88.24%，而OpenTrons-AI为32.35%。湿实验室验证产生了可解释的读数、Sanger确认产品和反馈校正的PCA组装DNA目标，建立了一条通往自主实验的可验证路径。总之，这些结果表明评估框架捕获了自主湿实验室自动化的执行相关要求，并且ProtoPilot能够通过将协议和代码生成转化为验证的执行和反馈引导的修订来满足这些要求。

Original abstract: Autonomous wet-lab experimentation requires more than plausible protocol text: biological intent, quantitative procedures, device constraints and experimental feedback must remain aligned from protocol and SOP design to code and physical execution. We developed ProtoPilot, a self-evolving multi-agent system, together with an expert-grounded benchmark and evaluation framework for testing this conversion as an experimental automation problem. The framework spans 294 synthetic-biology and molecular-biology tasks derived from 98 gold-standard protocols, wet-lab expert rubrics, device-level validity gates and real experimental tests. ProtoPilot incorporates layer-wise verifiability, multi-agent orchestration and a runtime-updated skill library to generate protocols, expand SOPs, synthesize SDK-compliant code and revise workflows from wet-lab feedback. It achieved a Top@3 expert-preference rate of 90.2%, an overall protocol-to-code gate pass rate of 89.5% and an Opentrons pass rate of 88.24%, compared with 32.35% for OpenTrons-AI. Wet-lab validation produced interpretable readouts, Sanger-confirmed products and feedback-corrected PCA-assembled DNA targets, establishing a verifiable route to autonomous experimentation. Together, these results show that the evaluation framework captures execution-relevant requirements for autonomous wet-lab automation, and that ProtoPilot can meet them by converting protocol and code generation into validated execution and feedback-guided revision.

</details>


### [60] [RAISE: LLM-based Automated Heuristic Design with Robust Adversary Instance Search](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31801v1)
*Fei Liu,Alessio Figalli,Patrick Owen,Nicola Serra*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 基于LLM的自动启发式设计，结合对抗实例搜索增强鲁棒性，方法可直接迁移至自动代码优化。

TL;DR: 提出RAISE框架，通过约束对抗性实例搜索将最坏情况实例集成到LLM进化循环中，显著提升AHD在分布偏移下的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM-based AHD方法在固定训练集上优化，但在真实分布偏移下性能灾难性下降，需要鲁棒的启发式设计方法。

Method: RAISE将鲁棒AHD建模为约束对抗性实例搜索问题，外循环用LLM进化启发式，内循环无LLM地在训练集epsilon球内搜索困难实例（使用基分布参数化和边界投影）。

Result: 在OBP、OJSP和OVRP的五个分布族上，现有方法性能下降高达19倍，而RAISE在所有分布和规模上保持强劲性能。

Conclusion: RAISE有效提高了AHD在分布偏移下的鲁棒性，优于现有方法。

中文摘要：基于大型语言模型（LLM）的自动启发式设计（AHD）在发现高质量启发式方法方面取得了显著进展。然而，现有的基于LLM的AHD方法针对固定的训练实例集优化启发式方法，当部署在真实世界的分布偏移下时可能会灾难性地失败。我们提出了鲁棒对抗实例搜索（RAISE），这是一个框架，它将训练分布原则性邻域内的约束最坏情况实例搜索集成到基于LLM的进化搜索循环中。RAISE将鲁棒AHD视为一个约束对抗性实例搜索问题：外循环通过LLM算子进化启发式方法，而内循环（无LLM）使用具有边界投影的基分布参数化，高效识别训练实例集周围epsilon球内的困难实例。在在线装箱（OBP）、在线作业车间调度（OJSP）和在线车辆路径规划（OVRP）上，跨五个分布族的综合实验表明，现有的基于LLM的AHD方法在分布偏移下性能下降高达19倍，而RAISE在所有测试的分布和问题规模上始终保持着强劲的性能。

Original abstract: Automated Heuristic Design (AHD) with Large Language Models (LLMs) has shown remarkable progress in discovering high-quality heuristics. However, existing LLM-based AHD methods optimize heuristics for a fixed training instance set and may fail catastrophically when deployed under real-world distributional shifts. We propose Robust Adversary Instance Search (RAISE), a framework that integrates constrained worst-case instance search within a principled neighborhood of the training distribution into the LLM-based evolutionary search loop. RAISE treats robust AHD as a constrained adversarial instance search problem: the outer loop evolves heuristics via LLM operators, while an LLM-free inner loop efficiently identifies hard instances within an epsilon-ball around the training instance set using a basis distribution parameterization with boundary projection. Comprehensive experiments on Online Bin Packing (OBP), Online Job Shop Scheduling (OJSP), and Online Vehicle Routing (OVRP) across five distribution families demonstrate that existing LLM-based AHD methods degrade by up to 19 times under distribution shift, while RAISE consistently maintains strong performance across all tested distributions and problem scales

</details>


### [61] [Adaptive Cluster-First Route-Second Decomposition for Industrial-Scale Vehicle Routing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31820v1)
*Oguzhan Karaahmetoglu,Hyong Kim*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM引导的自适应车辆路径规划分解，提出通用agent决策与工具选择方法。

TL;DR: 提出一种基于大语言模型的自适应先聚类后路径系统，通过迭代决策过程联合划分客户和车辆，在高达50万客户的CVRP实例上表现出更好的可扩展性和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CFRS方法依赖固定规则或学习策略，在不同特征实例上表现不一致，且难以适应大规模问题。

Method: 利用大语言模型作为高层决策者，根据分解状态选择聚类、平衡和细化操作，实现自适应联合划分客户和车辆。

Result: 在基准规模实例上性能有竞争力，在更大规模问题（50万客户）上表现出改进的可扩展性和鲁棒路由质量。

Conclusion: LLM引导的自适应决策支持为工业规模车辆路径和大规模物流规划提供了一种实用且有效的方法。

中文摘要：大规模容量受限车辆路径问题（CVRPs）通常采用先聚类后路径（CFRS）的方法来解决，这种方法将路由实例拆分为更小、计算上易于处理的子问题。现有的拆分方法通常依赖于固定的划分规则、预定义的优化目标或学习策略，这些方法在不同空间、需求和操作特征下的实例中可能表现不一致。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种自适应CFRS系统，该系统将分解过程形式化为迭代决策过程。受大语言模型（LLMs）在推理和工具选择方面最近成功的启发，该系统采用LLM作为高层决策者，分析演化的分解状态，并选择性地应用进一步的聚类、平衡和细化操作。所提出的算法联合划分客户和车辆，实现容量感知聚类，同时根据每个问题的特征调整划分决策。我们在包含多达50万个客户的合成和基准衍生CVRP实例上评估了该方法。实验结果表明，该方法在基准规模实例上表现出竞争性性能，同时在更大规模问题上展现出改进的可扩展性和稳健的路由质量。这些结果突显了自适应、LLM引导的决策支持作为工业规模车辆路径和大规模物流规划的实用方法的潜力。

Original abstract: Large-scale capacitated vehicle routing problems (CVRPs) are commonly addressed using cluster-first route-second (CFRS) approaches that split a routing instance into smaller, computationally tractable subproblems. Existing splitting methods typically rely on fixed partitioning rules, predefined optimization objectives, or learned policies, which may perform inconsistently across instances exhibiting different spatial, demand, and operational characteristics. In this work, we propose an adaptive CFRS system that formulates a decomposition procedure as an iterative decision-making process. Motivated by the recent success of large language models (LLMs) in reasoning and tool selection, the system employs an LLM as a high-level decision maker that analyzes the evolving decomposition state and selectively applies further clustering, balancing, and refinement operators. The proposed algorithm jointly partitions customers and vehicles, enabling capacity-aware clustering while adapting partitioning decisions to the characteristics of each problem. We evaluate the approach on synthetic and benchmark-derived CVRP instances containing up to 500,000 customers. Experimental results demonstrate competitive performance on benchmark-scale instances while exhibiting improved scalability and robust routing quality on substantially larger problems. These results highlight the potential of adaptive, LLM-guided decision support as a practical approach for industrial-scale vehicle routing and large-scale logistics planning.

Original abstract: High-throughput plant phenotyping now generates image derived datasets far faster than scientists can analyze them. We present an end-to-end agentic AI framework that turns the facility from a data factory into an interactive autonomous, discovery platform, where scientists partner with AI agents to accelerate time to insight. A conversational Co-Scientist Agent translates a scientist's natural-language question into a structured analysis plan, and a headless Compute Agent dispatches Vision Transformer segmentation and trait extraction on the Frontier exascale supercomputer. The two agents run in separate security and resource domains and communicate over a secure, token-authenticated streaming channel, a design that accounts for the federation, data-movement, and provenance realities cloud-native agentic frameworks ignore, ensuring end-to-end provenance is captured for every interaction. The framework turns a days- to weeks-long analysis process into an interactive loop where agents reason over results, recommend next analyses, and respond to follow-up questions in seconds.

Original abstract: Human-labeled data are widely used as reference annotations in ML, despite known variability across annotators in many expert-driven domains. We propose a multi-agent system (MAS) that orchestrates expert decision trees with Vision-Language Models (VLMs), treating the decision tree as a structural prior while VLMs perform localized semantic perception at individual nodes, with multi-agent voting to mitigate VLM stochasticity. We formalize a Decoupled Declarative Decision (D3) Framework that enables zero-modification generalization across diverse expert-defined decision structures. On a tree bias classification testbed, our framework outperforms supervised ML baselines and reduces the amount of expert labeling effort required. These results suggest that agentic orchestration of VLMs with expert priors can reproduce expert-defined labeling procedures at substantially lower annotation cost while maintaining interpretability.

Original abstract: Policy-grounded document review requires determining whether a target document complies with organization-specific policies, guidelines, or playbooks. While large language models can assist with policy interpretation and document analysis, end-to-end prompting leaves the applied policy logic implicit, making compliance decisions difficult to inspect, update, and test. We present PolicyGuard, a neuro-symbolic framework for policy-grounded document compliance review. PolicyGuard converts organizational policy guidance into an executable review engine consisting of typed relational logic rules and atom-level extraction questions. During review, LLMs answer these local questions using retrieved document evidence, and a symbolic evaluator applies the formal rules to detect non-compliance. We instantiate and evaluate PolicyGuard on company-specific NDA compliance review, where contract clauses must be checked against organization-specific negotiation policies. By separating policy formalization, local document interpretation, and symbolic compliance evaluation, PolicyGuard makes document review more explicit, maintainable, and systematically testable.

Original abstract: We study agentic code generation in Dafny, where a model must generate both executable code and the proof artifacts for verification. We present AxDafny, a verifier-guided repair framework that iteratively generates implementations, invariants, assertions, and termination arguments. We also introduce LiveCodeBench-Pro-Dafny (LCB-Pro-Dafny), a benchmark of 250 competition-style programming problems translated into Dafny with formal specifications and a verifier-based evaluation harness. On LCB-Pro-Dafny, AxDafny substantially improves verification success over baseline GPT-5.5 performance. On DafnyBench, AxDafny achieves 92.7\% verification success, outperforming the strongest previously reported proof-hint baseline by 6.5 percentage points. Lastly, we show that verification success and runtime test performance measure different aspects of generated code.

Method: 提出RareDxR1模型，采用渐进式端到端训练框架，结合知识内化将碎片化罕见病知识直接嵌入模型参数；提出反射增强推理采样（RERS）合成专家诊断轨迹；采用双层课程强化学习逐步提升诊断能力。

Result: 在多个基准测试上取得最先进准确率，显著突破开放域罕见病诊断性能。

Conclusion: RareDxR1通过端到端推理中心设计克服了现有方法局限，为开放域罕见病诊断提供了高效、准确的解决方案，代码和数据集将公开以促进研究。

中文摘要：罕见病鉴别诊断是一项关键但艰巨的临床任务，要求医生从复杂、非结构化的患者症状中识别精确的表型，并在庞大的搜索空间中执行复杂的推理。然而，现有的人工智能方法通常依赖于基于管道的表型提取或检索增强生成，由于预定义本体、检索瓶颈和缺乏诊断逻辑，这些方法遭受了关键信息损失。为了解决这些挑战，我们引入了RareDxR1，一个端到端的以推理为中心的大语言模型，旨在直接从非结构化临床笔记中进行开放域罕见病诊断。我们设计了一个渐进式端到端训练框架，通过协同知识内化与自主进化学习，从而绕过了对结构化表型和封闭集决策的依赖。为了克服RAG和表型限制的局限性，我们实现了将碎片化的罕见病知识直接深度内化到模型参数中。此外，为了弥合模型生成与专家推理之间的差距，我们提出了反射增强推理采样（RERS）策略，该策略通过从失败中学习而无需人工注释，合成专家级诊断轨迹。另外，我们提出了一种双层课程强化学习方法，以逐步掌握罕见病诊断。实验结果表明，RareDxR1在不同基准测试中均达到了最先进的准确率，标志着开放域罕见病诊断的重大突破。我们的代码和数据集将公开提供。

Original abstract: Rare disease differential diagnosis is a critical yet arduous clinical task, requiring physicians to identify precise phenotypes from complex, unstructured patient symptoms and execute intricate reasoning within a vast search space. However, existing AI approaches typically rely on pipeline-based phenotype extraction or retrieval-augmented generation, which suffer from critical information loss due to predefined ontologies, retrieval bottlenecks, and a lack of diagnostic logic. To address these challenges, we introduce RareDxR1, an end-to-end reasoning-centric large language model designed for open-domain rare disease diagnosis directly from unstructured clinical notes. We design a progressive end-to-end training framework by synergizing knowledge internalization with autonomous evolutionary learning, thereby bypassing reliance on structured phenotypes and closed-set decision-making. To overcome the limitations of RAG and phenotype restriction, we enabled the deep internalization of fragmented rare-disease knowledge directly into the model's parameters. Moreover, to bridge the gap between model generation and expert reasoning, we propose Reflection-Enhanced Reasoning Sampling (RERS), a strategy that synthesizes expert-level diagnostic trajectories by learning from failures without human annotation. Additionally, we propose a dual-level curriculum reinforcement learning approach for gradually mastering rare disease diagnosis. Experimental results demonstrate that RareDxR1 achieves state-of-the-art accuracy across different benchmarks, marking a significant breakthrough in open-domain rare disease diagnosis. Our code and dataset will be publicly available.

</details>


### [67] [A Contextual-Bandit Oversight Game with Two-Sided Informational Asymmetry](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00155v1)
*Yunjin Tong*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 形式化人类监督agent的信息不对称博弈，对agent安全控制有启发。

TL;DR: 研究双向信息不对称下的人类-AI运行时监督，建立上下文赌博团队博弈模型，揭示团队最优与短视规则之间的可避免伤害板，证明该差距是不可信监督沟通的代价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实场景中AI拥有行动质量私密信息，人类拥有奖励私密信息，导致监督困境，需要理论分析这种不对称性对监督有效性的影响。

Method: 基于合作逆强化学习（CIRL）和监督博弈，构建具有双向信息不对称的上下文赌博团队博弈，引入play/ask/trust/oversee界面，进行一次性刻画和动态分析。

Result: 得到了团队最优和短视规则的精确刻画，发现其差距构成可避免伤害板；该差距源于非可信监督沟通，并通过被动学习和一期滞后监督响应的主动信号在重复博弈中动态演化。

Conclusion: 揭示了人类-AI运行时监督中双向信息不对称的根本挑战，为非可信监督沟通的代价提供了理论刻画，为设计可信监督机制提供了依据。

中文摘要：我们研究当私人信息双向流动时，人类对AI智能体的运行时监督：人类私下知道自己的奖励函数，而AI私下知道其提议行动的质量。这种不对称性自然出现在自主机器人或软件代理已经检查了其人类监督员无法直接评估的情况时。基于合作逆强化学习（CIRL）和监督博弈，我们引入了一个具有双向不对称信息和play/ask/trust/oversee界面的上下文赌博团队博弈。赌博结构去除了物理状态转移，从而在完整POMDP设置中仍属推测性的精确一次性刻画得以实现，尽管共同信念在各轮次间仍然是动态控制的状态。我们给出了两种一次性刻画，一个团队最优和一个行为上自然的短视规则，其差距是一块可避免的伤害板：一个区域，其中AI私下知道提议的行动有害且关闭会有所帮助，但短视的人类信任其先验而拒绝监督。我们表明这一差距是不可信监督沟通的代价，并给出了一个部分分析，解释其如何通过被动学习和具有一期滞后监督响应的主动信号在重复回合中动态解决。

Original abstract: We study runtime human oversight of an AI agent when private information runs in both directions: the human privately knows her reward function, while the AI privately knows the quality of the action it proposes. This is the kind of asymmetry that arises naturally when an autonomous robot or software agent has inspected a situation its human supervisor cannot directly assess. Building on Cooperative Inverse Reinforcement Learning (CIRL) and the Oversight Game, we introduce a contextual-bandit team game with two-sided asymmetric information and a play/ask/trust/oversee interface. The bandit structure removes physical state transitions and thereby yields exact one-shot characterizations that would remain conjectural in the full POMDP setting, though the common belief remains a dynamically controlled state across rounds. We give two one-shot characterizations, a team optimum and a behaviorally natural myopic rule, whose gap is a slab of avoidable harm: a region in which the AI privately knows the proposed action is harmful and shutdown would help, yet a myopic human, trusting her prior, declines to oversee. We show this gap is the price of non-credible oversight communication, and give a partial analysis of how it resolves dynamically over repeated rounds through passive learning and active signaling with a one-period-lagged oversight response.

</details>


### [68] [From Signals to Structure: How Memory Architecture Drives Language Emergence in LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00233v1)
*Yashar Talebirad,Eden Redman,Ali Parsaee,Osmar R. Zaiane*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究记忆架构对多智能体语言涌现的影响，其外部化记忆和稳定约定的机制对coding agent的长期记忆与检索设计有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 在Lewis信号游戏中，记忆架构比通道容量更重要。持久私人笔记本防止了高容量崩溃，而信息瓶颈点（容量=8）反而是脆弱区域。通道容量和记忆架构共同决定信号的语言化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解两个智能体如何仅凭交互历史从头发明共享语言，并探究记忆架构和通道容量对协调的影响。

Method: 在Lewis信号博弈中，使用LLM智能体，比较五种记忆架构（包括多轮对话、持久笔记本等）在不同通道容量下的协调表现。

Result: 具有持久笔记本的智能体在容量=25时达到最高协调分数0.867±0.023；无状态智能体在中等容量时最优，容量过高时退化；信息瓶颈点（容量=8）导致脆弱性，剩余容量更优。

Conclusion: 通道容量单独无法预测协调，记忆架构决定交互历史是否能转化为稳定约定，两者都是理解信号语言化的关键维度。

中文摘要：两个智能体如何从头开始发明一种共享语言？在Lewis信号博弈中，发送者和接收者必须仅凭交互历史来协调编码。我们研究了具有LLM智能体的五种记忆架构在不同通道配置下的表现，发现记忆架构比通道容量更重要。拥有持久私人笔记本的智能体受益于剩余通道容量，避免了无状态智能体的高容量崩溃，实现了最可靠的协调（容量=25时为0.867±0.023）。无状态智能体在中等容量时达到峰值，然后随着词汇增长超出滚动上下文窗口的跟踪能力而退化。笔记本将学习到的约定外化，使智能体无需每轮重新推导编码。一个受信息瓶颈启发的论证预测最优容量等于物体数量；然而，瓶颈（容量=8）被证明是一个脆弱点，而剩余容量通常更好。我们表明，通道容量单独无法预测协调；记忆架构决定了智能体是否将交互历史转化为稳定的约定，这两个维度对于理解信号如何成为语言都是必需的。

Original abstract: How do two agents invent a shared language from scratch? In a Lewis signaling game, a sender and receiver must coordinate on a code using only their interaction history. We study five memory architectures across varying channel configurations with LLM agents and find that memory architecture matters more than channel capacity. Agents with a persistent private notebook benefit from surplus channel capacity and avoid the high-capacity collapse seen in stateless agents, achieving the most reliable coordination ($0.867 \pm 0.023$ at capacity = 25). Stateless agents peak at moderate capacity and then degrade as the vocabulary grows beyond what a rolling context window can track The notebook externalizes learned conventions, freeing agents from having to re-derive codes each round. An information bottleneck-inspired argument predicts an optimal capacity equal to the number of objects. Instead, the bottleneck (capacity = 8) proves to be a fragility point, and surplus capacity is generally better. We show that channel capacity alone cannot predict coordination; memory architecture determines whether agents turn interaction history into stable conventions, and both dimensions are needed to understand how signals become language.

</details>


### [69] [Mnemosyne: Agentic Transaction Processing for Validating and Repairing AI-generated Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00269v2)
*Edward Y. Chang,Longling Geng,Emily J. Chang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出事务处理模型验证和修复AI生成的工作流，直接涉及agent动作的准入、补偿和回滚，可迁移到coding agent的动作验证与可靠执行。

TL;DR: 提出ATP事务模型，将LLM生成的动作视为不可信提议，通过约束集C确定性准入，实现提交状态正确性与提议层无关；在Mnemosyne运行时实现，验证了安全性和低开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM生成的动作可能语法正确但存在过期、不可行、冲突或破坏证据等问题，需要一种机制来确保动作的正确执行。

Method: 引入Agentic Transaction Processing (ATP)模型，将生成动作视为不可信提议，通过声明的可执行约束集C进行确定性准入。运行时负责准入和提交，发生中断时进行边界内反应式修复。在Mnemosyne中实现，使用仅追加日志、有效状态投影等。

Result: 在九个证伪测试中拒绝违规，开销低于6%，局部修复操作比全局重新计算少一个数量级。在实时试点中，80个提议全通过准入，40个修复提议中24个通过，16个被拒（4个安全拒绝）。

Conclusion: ATP模型有效确保了LLM生成动作的正确性和安全性，Mnemosyne实现展示了低开销和高效修复。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地生成工作流动作、修复和计划，但生成的 action 可能语法有效，却过期、不可行、冲突或破坏触发修复的证据。我们引入智能体事务处理（ATP），一种事务模型，将生成的 action 视为不可信提议，直到它们通过声明的可执行约束集 C 下的确定性准入。其治理原则是双重的：提议不是真理，没有提议能预见所有中断。任何事物都可以提议，但只有运行时可以准入和提交；当未预见的中断发生时，它在边界内反应式修复，而不是信任新的提议。相对于 C，提交状态正确性变得与提议层的胜任力、诚实或学习无关。我们在 Mnemosyne 中实现 ATP，这是一个具有仅追加转换日志、有效状态投影、依赖安全补偿和活动提交记录的运行时，并证明了相对于 C 的四个安全属性（权限分离、串行等价生成性准入、证据保留修复、义务约束）以及有界反应式修复保证（LCRP）。一个可复现的工件在九个证伪测试中拒绝目标违规，同时仍准入有效工作，开销低于 6%，且局部修复编辑的操作数量比全局重新计算少一个数量级。在实时提议者试点中，来自四个异构 LLM 的 80 个静态计划进入和中执行修复提议通过了相同的准入边界，由外部跨剧集测试工具评分，零无效提交；门控准入 40 个实时修复提议中的 24 个，拒绝 16 个，其中四个是明确的过度回滚安全拒绝。Mnemosyne 是开源的：https://github.com/eyuchang/Mnemosyne/tree/mnemosyne-atp-postgres-rerun

Original abstract: LLMs increasingly generate workflow actions, repairs, and plans, but a generated action may be syntactically valid yet stale, infeasible, conflicting, or destructive of the evidence that triggered a repair. We introduce Agentic Transaction Processing (ATP), a transaction model that treats generated actions as untrusted proposals until they pass deterministic admission under a declared, executable constraint set C. The governing principle is two-sided: a proposal is not truth, and no proposal foresees every disruption. Anything may propose, but only the runtime admits and commits; when an unforeseen disruption strikes, it repairs reactively within bounds rather than trusting a fresh proposal. Relative to C, committed-state correctness becomes independent of the competence, honesty, or learning of the proposing layer. We realize ATP in Mnemosyne, a runtime with an append-only transition log, effective-state projection, dependency-safe compensation, and active commitment records, and prove four safety properties relative to C (authority separation, serial-equivalent generative admission, evidence-preserving repair, and obligation containment) plus a bounded-reactive-repair guarantee (LCRP). A reproducible artifact rejects the targeted violations across nine falsification tests while still admitting valid work, at under 6% overhead, and local repair edits an order of magnitude fewer operations than global recompute. In live-proposer pilots, 80 static plan-entry and mid-execution repair proposals from four heterogeneous LLMs pass the same admission boundary, scored by an external cross-episode harness with zero invalid commits; the gate admits 24 of 40 live repair proposals and rejects 16, four as explicit safety rejections of over-broad rollback. Mnemosyne is open source: https://github.com/eyuchang/Mnemosyne/tree/mnemosyne-atp-postgres-rerun

</details>
