### [70] [A Lifecycle and Application-Stack Survey of Large Language Model Vulnerabilities: Attacks, Risks, Defenses, and Open Problems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31639v1)
*Seyed Bagher Hashemi Natanzi,Bo Tang*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: LLM系统安全综述涵盖agent安全控制，对agent部署安全有参考价值。

TL;DR: 本文从生命周期和应用栈视角系统化了LLM系统的安全漏洞，分析了八种攻击阶段及其防御，并提出了未来研究议程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM从文本生成器演变为嵌入各种系统的组件，带来了新的安全风险，需要系统化理解漏洞的全貌。

Method: 采用生命周期和应用栈视角，组织攻击分为八个阶段，分析每个阶段的攻击者能力、安全目标、攻击实例、风险、评估和防御，并将漏洞映射到安全目标。

Result: 提出了一个系统化的漏洞分类框架，强调了信任边界失效、数据成为指令、委派权威放大错误等问题，并指出了点防御的局限性。

Conclusion: 未来需要关注组合安全、溯源感知检索、工具调用遏制、长周期智能体评估、隐私保护自适应、现实红队测试和部署级事件响应等研究方向。

中文摘要：大型语言模型不再仅仅是文本生成器。它们越来越多地嵌入到检索管道、企业助手、编码环境、机器人系统、安全运营工作流以及能够读取私人数据、调用工具、写入文件、执行代码并在组织边界内行动的自主智能体中。这种转变改变了安全问题：风险不仅来自模型权重，还来自整个生命周期和应用栈，数据、提示、模型输出、工具、记忆和用户权限通过它们相互交互。本文通过生命周期和应用栈的视角系统化了关于大型语言模型系统漏洞的文献。我们组织了八个阶段的攻击：数据收集、预训练、后训练对齐、模型打包和供应链、检索和记忆、提示和推理、工具/智能体执行以及部署/维护。对于每个阶段，我们分析了攻击者能力、受影响的安全目标、代表性攻击、实际风险、评估实践和防御措施。我们进一步将LLM特定的漏洞映射到机密性、完整性、可用性、安全性、隐私、公平性、问责制和代理控制目标。与列出一系列孤立攻击名称的分类法不同，提出的系统化强调了信任边界在何处失效，不受信任的数据如何成为可执行指令，委派的权威如何放大模型错误，以及为什么点防御很少能组合。我们以一个关于安全LLM系统的研究议程作为结尾，包括组合安全、溯源感知检索、工具调用遏制、长周期智能体评估、隐私保护自适应、现实红队测试和部署级事件响应。

Original abstract: Large language models are no longer only text generators. They are increasingly embedded in retrieval pipelines, enterprise assistants, coding environments, robotic systems, security-operation workflows, and autonomous agents that can read private data, call tools, write files, execute code, and act across organizational boundaries. This shift changes the security problem: risks do not arise from the model weights alone, but from the full lifecycle and application stack through which data, prompts, model outputs, tools, memories, and user authority interact. This paper systematizes the literature on vulnerabilities in large language model systems through a lifecycle and application-stack lens. We organize attacks across eight stages: data collection, pretraining, post-training alignment, model packaging and supply chain, retrieval and memory, prompting and inference, tool/agent execution, and deployment/maintenance. For each stage, we analyze attacker capabilities, affected security objectives, representative attacks, practical risks, evaluation practices, and defenses. We further map LLM-specific vulnerabilities to confidentiality, integrity, availability, safety, privacy, fairness, accountability, and agency-control objectives. Unlike taxonomies that list isolated attack names, the proposed systematization emphasizes where trust boundaries fail, how untrusted data becomes executable instruction, how delegated authority amplifies model errors, and why point defenses rarely compose. We close with a research agenda for secure LLM systems, including compositional security, provenance-aware retrieval, tool-call containment, long-horizon agent evaluation, privacy-preserving adaptation, realistic red teaming, and deployment-grade incident response.

</details>

### [71] [ShopX: A Foundation Model for Intent-to-Item Fulfillment in Agentic Shopping](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31693v2)
*Jiacheng Chen,Tao Zhang,Manxi Lin,Dunxian Huang,Teng Shi,Honghao Fu,Mengyan Li,Xinming Zhang,Chenchi Zhang,Xuan Lu,Xiaoxiong Du,Haibin Chen,Shaolin Ye,Hao Chang,Xiaoqi Li,Shuwen Xiao,Yujin Yuan,Jingxuan Feng,Shaopan Xiong,Huimin Yi,Ju Huang,Qiu Shen,Ying Chen,Junjun Zheng,Xiangheng Kong,Dan Ou,Haihong Tang,Yuning Jiang,Bo Zheng*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 电商领域agentic shopping，提出模型原生物品操作框架，对agent规划与工具使用有通用方法贡献。

TL;DR: ShopX通过统一意图理解、执行规划和基于语义ID的商品空间操作，在单一基础模型中实现了模型原生的商品执行，改善了代理购物工作流中的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将LLM包裹在搜索和推荐管道周围，导致意图理解与商品空间执行之间存在鸿沟，且生成式推荐主要生成检索候选而非直接实现意图，因此需要一种模型原生方法来减少有损交接。

Method: 提出ShopX框架，设计语义可恢复的LLM可操作SID，并采用训练方法使通用LLM能够灵活进行多轮商品空间执行；通过模型原生商品执行框架，包含动作协议、上下文访问、目录依据和状态管理。

Result: 在匿名淘宝生产日志的单轮和多轮任务上评估，显示模型原生执行改善了整体框架行为，尤其对复杂或模糊请求。

Conclusion: ShopX通过模型原生设计减少了有损交接，提升了复杂请求的满足性能。

中文摘要：AI原生应用的浪潮正在将购物从基于页面和流的浏览转向由LLM代理协调的意图驱动体验。一种常见的设计是将LLM包裹在现有搜索和推荐管道周围，迫使复杂意图通过低带宽的检索或排序接口传递，并在语言理解与商品空间执行之间留下鸿沟。生成式推荐通过语义ID（SID）为LLM提供了直接的商品空间接口，但现有模型主要生成用于检索的候选对象，而非将灵活意图转化为商品空间结果。我们提出ShopX来解决这一瓶颈，将意图理解、执行规划和灵活的SID原生商品空间操作统一到单个基础模型中。我们通过一个模型原生的商品执行框架将ShopX部署到代理购物工作流中，该框架配备一个服务工具集，定义了面向模型的动作协议，并公开了上下文访问、目录依据和状态管理的支持界面。在此框架内，ShopX规划并组合基于SID的商品空间操作，例如SID束搜索检索、列表排序或产品捆绑。这种以模型为中心的设计减少了代理编排与商品空间执行之间的有损交接。为了构建ShopX，我们设计了语义可恢复、LLM可操作的SID，以及一种训练方法，使通用LLM能够灵活地进行多轮商品空间执行，同时保留购物代理所需的知识和指令遵循能力。我们在源自匿名淘宝生产日志的单轮和多轮执行任务上，将ShopX框架与工具中介的代理系统进行了比较，结果显示模型原生执行改善了整体框架行为，尤其在复杂或模糊请求上。

Original abstract: The wave of AI-native applications is moving shopping beyond page- and feed-based browsing toward intent-driven experiences orchestrated by LLM agents. A common design wraps an LLM around existing search and recommendation pipelines, forcing complex intents through low-bandwidth retrieval or ranking interfaces and leaving a gap between language understanding and item-space fulfillment. Generative recommendation gives LLMs a direct item-space interface through semantic IDs (SIDs), but existing models mainly generate candidates for retrieval rather than translate flexible intents into item-space outcomes. We propose ShopX to address this bottleneck by unifying intent understanding, execution planning, and flexible SID-native item-space operations into a single foundation model. We deploy ShopX in agentic shopping workflows through a model-native item-fulfillment framework with a serving harness that defines a model-facing action protocol and exposes support surfaces for context access, catalog grounding, and state management. Within this framework, ShopX plans and composes SID-based item-space operations such as SID beam-search retrieval, listwise ranking, or product bundling. This model-centric design reduces lossy hand-offs between agent orchestration and item-space execution. To build ShopX, we design semantically recoverable, LLM-operable SIDs and a training recipe that equips a general LLM for flexible multi-turn item-space fulfillment while retaining the knowledge and instruction-following abilities needed by a shopping agent. We evaluate the ShopX framework against tool-mediated agentic systems on single- and multi-turn fulfillment tasks derived from anonymized Taobao production logs, showing that model-native fulfillment improves overall framework behavior, especially on complex or ambiguous requests.

</details>


### [72] [GR2 Technical Report](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31984v3)
*Yufei Li,Zaiwei Zhang,Mingfu Liang,Kavosh Asadi,Jay Xu,Jimmy Kim,Chongyang Bai,Jieyi Zhang,Hongye Xie,Prachi Agrawal,Dian Yu,Tianyi Chen,Jean-Pascal Billaud,Garret Buell,Yongkang Zhu,Sachin Patil,Brooke Bian,Zhou Fang,Kevin Huang,Shiva Sudanagunta,Yuzhen Huang,Emma Lu,Chris O'Brien,Yang Song,Lihong Li,Jacob Tao,Zhicheng Zhu,Chao Li,Gaoxiang Liu,Neil Wu,Zhongyin Hu,Li Han,Loki Chen,Ming Lei,Greg Rehm,Siyuan Song,Tianwei Zhang,Li Li,Ketan Singh,Yavuz Yetim,Ilyas Atishev,Satendra Gera,Ashkan Sadeghi,Rachel Yan,Nikko Mizutani,Shuaiwen Wang,Song Yang,Zhijing Li,Jiang Liu,Mengying Sun,Fei Tian,Xiaohan Wei,Chonglin Sun,Shuo Gu,Parish Aggarwal,Senthil Manickavelu,Kaushik Rangadurai,Zhi Hua,Frank Shyu,Ruchit Sharma,Liyuan Li,Shike Mei,Wenlin Chen,Santanu Kolay,Ben Schulte,Deepak Chandra,Yang Song,Sandeep Pandey,Xi Liu,Hamed Firooz,Luke Simon*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: LLM+RL用于推荐重排序，其推理轨迹蒸馏与可验证奖励设计可迁移至agent训练

TL;DR: 提出GR2，一个结合语义ID、推理蒸馏和强化学习的端到端重排序框架，显著提升工业推荐性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM推荐工作主要针对检索和排序，忽略了重排序；LLM部署方式未充分利用RL推理能力；项目ID非语义导致LLM无法直接处理。

Method: 结合语义ID中期训练、推理轨迹蒸馏、RL可验证奖励、上下文压缩器、在线策略蒸馏（OPD）和推理蒸馏。

Result: 在工业流量上R@1提升18.7%，R@3提升7.1%，N@3提升9.6%。

Conclusion: 重排序中奖励设计关键，条件可验证奖励是必要组件。

中文摘要：工业推荐系统通过多阶段漏斗——检索、早期排序和重排序——服务数十亿用户，其中最终的重排序步骤不成比例地塑造用户参与度和下游性能，特别是在轮播和网格展示格式中。尽管对大型语言模型（LLMs）在推荐中的热情日益增长，三个差距阻碍了工业应用：（1）大多数工作针对检索和排序，而重排序——最接近最终用户体验的阶段——基本未被探索；（2）LLMs通常以零样本或通过监督微调部署，未能充分利用强化学习（RL）在可验证奖励上解锁的推理能力；（3）部署的目录索引了数十亿具有非语义标识符的项目，这些标识符位于任何基础LLM词汇表之外。我们提出GR2（生成式推理重排序器），一个端到端框架，结合了（i）在由分词器产生的语义ID上进行中期训练，具有>=99%的唯一性，（ii）通过目标提示和拒绝采样从更强的教师模型中提取的推理轨迹，以及（iii）具有专为重排序设计的可验证奖励的强化学习。为了使GR2资源可行，我们进一步（iv）引入一个上下文压缩器来分摊训练成本，在线策略蒸馏（OPD）作为SFT的可扩展替代方案——我们发现SFT在工业规模下会崩溃——以及用于低延迟服务的推理蒸馏。GR2在工业规模流量上相较于传统基线实现了+18.7% R@1，+7.1% R@3，+9.6% N@3的提升。我们进一步发现奖励设计在重排序中至关重要：LLMs经常通过保留输入顺序或利用位置偏差来作弊奖励，这促使条件可验证奖励成为必要的工业组件。

Original abstract: Industrial recommendation systems serve billions of users through a multi-stage funnel -- retrieval, early-stage ranking, and re-ranking -- where the final re-ranking step disproportionately shapes user engagement and downstream performance, particularly for carousel and grid display formats. Despite growing enthusiasm for Large Language Models (LLMs) in recommendation, three gaps hinder industrial adoption: (1) most efforts target retrieval and ranking, leaving re-ranking -- the stage closest to the final user experience -- largely underexplored; (2) LLMs are typically deployed zero-shot or via supervised fine-tuning, underutilizing the reasoning capabilities unlocked by reinforcement learning (RL) on verifiable rewards; (3) deployed catalogs index billions of items with non-semantic identifiers that lie outside any base-LLM vocabulary. We present GR2 (Generative Reasoning Re-Ranker), an end-to-end framework that combines (i) mid-training on semantic IDs produced by a tokenizer with >=99% uniqueness, (ii) reasoning-trace distilled from a stronger teacher via targeted prompting and rejection sampling, and (iii) RL with verifiable rewards purpose-built for re-ranking. To make GR2 resource-viable, we further (iv) introduce a context compressor that amortizes training cost, On-Policy Distillation (OPD) as a scalable alternative to SFT -- which we find collapses at industrial scale -- and reasoning distillation for low-latency serving. GR2 delivers +18.7% R@1, +7.1% R@3, and +9.6% N@3 over legacy baselines on industrial-scale traffic. We further find that reward design is critical in re-ranking: LLMs often hack rewards by preserving the incoming order or exploiting position bias, motivating conditional verifiable rewards as essential industrial components.

</details>

### [73] [Automating Cause-Effect Specification with Knowledge Graphs and Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31614v1)
*Javal Vyas,Milapji Singh Gill,Mehmet Mercangöz*

Main category: eess.SY

Selection reason: LLM+KG生成因果规范，可视为agent在工程规范中的应用。

TL;DR: 提出结合知识图谱和受限大语言模型的语义AI框架，自动生成因果逻辑，减少手动工作，并在模块化工厂验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前因果逻辑创建手动、文档驱动且易不一致，需要自动化方法。

Method: 构建知识图谱表示过程结构、故障、症状等，再利用受限大语言模型生成安全叙述和SWRL规则。

Result: 在模块化过程工厂演示，成功生成工程语义、诊断关系和可验证规范，减少手动工作量。

Conclusion: 该框架能有效自动化因果逻辑生成，提高一致性和效率。

中文摘要：诸如联锁、报警合理化表格和因果矩阵等工程规范仍然是过程控制和安全的中心，然而它们的创建仍然主要是手动的、文档驱动的，并且容易出现不一致。本文提出了一种语义AI框架，通过结合知识图谱和受限大语言模型层来自动生成因果逻辑。该知识图谱基于一个已建立的模块化对齐本体，以机器可解释的形式表示过程结构、操作模式、故障、症状、原因和缓解措施。然后，大语言模型在严格的本体和词汇约束下将这些信息转化为操作人员可用的安全叙述和语义网规则语言规则，将生成的工件基于底层语义模型。该工作流程在模块化过程工厂上进行了演示，展示了如何通过统一的知识表示生成工程语义、诊断关系和机器可验证的规范，并减少了手动工作量。

Original abstract: Engineering specifications such as interlocks, alarm rationalization tables, and cause-and-effect (C&E) matrices remain central to process control and safety, yet their creation is still predominantly manual, document-driven, and prone to inconsistency. This paper presents a semantic-AI framework that automates the generation of C&E logic by combining a knowledge graph (KG) with a constrained large language model (LLM) layer. The KG builds on an established modular alignment ontology to represent process structure, operating modes, faults, symptoms, causes, and mitigation actions in a machine-interpretable form. The LLM then transforms this information into operator-ready safety narratives and Semantic Web Rule Language (SWRL) rules under strict ontology and vocabulary constraints, grounding the generated artifacts in the underlying semantic model. The workflow is demonstrated on a modular process plant, showing how engineering semantics, diagnostic relations, and machine-verifiable specifications can be generated from a unified knowledge representation with reduced manual effort.

</details>


### [74] [A Tutorial on Autonomous Fault-Tolerant Control Using Knowledge-Grounded LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31635v1)
*Javal Vyas,Milapji Singh Gill,Artan Markaj,Felix Gehlhoff,Mehmet Mercangöz*

Main category: eess.SY

Selection reason: 提出LLM agent用于故障恢复，包含规划、验证等通用agent能力，可迁移至代码优化agent的推理框架。

TL;DR: 提出使用LLM作为受约束监控规划器来支持过程工厂故障恢复，并定义了三个设计维度和提供了两个Python环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前故障恢复严重依赖操作员人工决策，需要自动化支持以提高效率和安全性。

Method: 将LLM视为受约束监控规划器，利用工厂知识提出恢复动作，并通过外部符号或模拟验证器检查提案，同时定义恢复模式、验证策略和部署约束三个设计维度。

Result: 提供了两个公开可执行的Python环境（模块化混合模块和连续搅拌釜反应器），支持可配置故障和自定义恢复/验证方法。

Conclusion: LLM代理通过约束和验证机制可以有效支持过程工厂的故障恢复决策，但需考虑延迟、知识工程等部署约束。

中文摘要：过程工厂中的故障恢复仍然严重依赖工厂操作员，特别是当故障超出预定义的监控逻辑时。操作员解读警报、程序、P&ID、互锁和过程趋势，然后决定如何在不触发停机的情况下将工厂移动到安全操作模式。本文研究了大型语言模型（LLM）代理如何支持此类恢复决策。提出的框架将LLM视为一个受约束的监控规划器。它利用工厂特定知识提出恢复动作，并且每个提议在执行前都会由外部验证器（符号化或基于模拟的）进行检查。本文开发了应用该框架的三个设计维度：LLM代理有用的恢复模式、区分可接受和不可接受提议的验证策略，以及由延迟、知识工程、安全集成和模型生命周期管理施加的部署约束。为了使框架直接可用，提供了两个公开可执行Python环境。这两个环境重新实现了已建立的案例研究，一个模块化混合模块和一个连续搅拌釜反应器，扩展了可配置故障以及用于自定义恢复和验证方法的定义接口。

Original abstract: Fault recovery in process plants still relies heavily on plant operators, especially when faults fall outside predefined supervisory logic. Operators interpret alarms, procedures, P\&IDs, interlocks, and process trends, then decide how to move the plant to a safe operating mode without triggering a shutdown. This paper examines how Large Language Model (LLM) agents can support such recovery decisions. The proposed framework treats the LLM as a constrained supervisory planner. It uses plant-specific knowledge to propose recovery actions, and every proposal is checked by an external validator (symbolic or simulation-based) before actuation. The paper develops three design dimensions for applying the framework: the recovery patterns for which LLM agents are useful, the validation strategies that separate admissible from inadmissible proposals, and the deployment constraints imposed by latency, knowledge engineering, safety integration, and model lifecycle management. To make the framework directly usable, two openly available executable Python environments are provided. Both re-implement established case studies, a modular mixing module and a continuous stirred-tank reactor, extended with configurable faults and defined interfaces for custom recovery and validation methods.

</details>

### [75] [Governance Gaps in Agent Interoperability Protocols: What MCP, A2A, and ACP Cannot Express](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31498v1)
*Richard Kang,Yudho Diponegoro*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 基于六维治理需求分类，系统分析五种代理互操作性协议，发现投票和异议保留普遍缺失，审议仅部分支持，表明代理社区治理需作为新架构层引入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代理互操作性协议在治理约束下能否支持代理社区的集体决策？

Method: 应用成员资格、审议、投票、异议保留、人工升级和审计/回放六维治理需求分类，分析MCP、A2A、ACP、ANP、ERC-8004五种协议的能力支持程度，区分可扩展与结构性差距。

Result: 投票和异议保留在所有协议中缺失，审议缺失或部分，无协议具备完整治理原语；存在可扩展和结构性两类差距。

Conclusion: 代理社区治理是当前互操作性标准之上的缺失架构层，而非标准内的缺失功能。

中文摘要：代理互操作性协议（MCP、A2A、ACP、ANP 和 ERC-8004）已经迅速发展成熟，能够实现自主代理之间的身份、能力发现、工具访问和消息交换。然而，随着企业部署异构代理集群，这些集群必须在治理约束下做出集体决策，一个问题随之而来：这些协议能否支持受治理的代理社区，还是仅支持面向任务的协调？我们提出了一种系统的差距分析，应用了从组织理论、多代理系统文献和企业治理标准中导出的六维治理需求分类（成员资格、审议、投票、异议保留、人工升级和审计/回放）。我们针对该分类分析每个协议的规范，将能力分类为支持、部分或缺失。由此产生的差距矩阵显示，投票和异议保留在所有五个协议中普遍缺失，审议缺失或最多部分实现，并且没有协议编码受治理代理社区所需的全部原语。我们区分了可扩展差距（可通过协议扩展机制解决）和结构性差距（需要新的架构层），并根据观察到的协议演进速度评估时间敏感性。该分析确立了代理社区治理构成当前互操作性标准之上的缺失架构层，而不是其中的缺失功能。

Original abstract: Agent interoperability protocols (MCP, A2A, ACP, ANP, and ERC-8004) have rapidly matured to enable identity, capability discovery, tool access, and message exchange between autonomous agents. However, as enterprises deploy heterogeneous agent fleets that must make collective decisions under governance constraints, a question arises: can these protocols support governed agent communities, or only task-oriented coordination? We present a systematic gap analysis applying a six-dimension governance requirements taxonomy (membership, deliberation, voting, dissent preservation, human escalation, and audit/replay) derived from organizational theory, multi-agent systems literature, and enterprise governance standards. We analyze each protocol's specification against this taxonomy, classifying capabilities as Supported, Partial, or Absent. The resulting gap matrix reveals that voting and dissent preservation are universally absent across all five protocols, deliberation is absent or at most partial, and no protocol encodes the full set of primitives required for governed agent communities. We distinguish extensible gaps (addressable through protocol extension mechanisms) from structural gaps (requiring a new architectural layer) and assess time-sensitivity based on observed protocol evolution velocity. The analysis establishes that agent community governance constitutes a missing architectural layer above current interoperability standards, not a missing feature within them.

</details>


### [76] [MECoBench: A Systematic Study of Multimodal Agent Collaboration in Embodied Environments](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31966v1)
*Qingyun Liu,Jiwen Zhang,Jingyi Hu,Siyuan Wang,Zhongyu Wei*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多模态具身agent协作benchmark，对多agent系统评测有通用参考价值

TL;DR: 提出了MECoBench，一个多模态具身协作基准，通过实验揭示了协作的收益与挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前MLLMs在具身智能体合作方面研究不足，缺乏系统评估基准。

Method: 构建MECoBench基准，包含多种任务、合作结构和协作模式，对多种MLLMs进行实验评估。

Result: 协作可提升任务完成但需平衡协调成本；沟通至关重要；最佳模式依赖团队规模和模型能力；协作提高鲁棒性。

Conclusion: MECoBench为多模态具身协作提供了系统性测试平台，有助于理解其机制和局限。

中文摘要：最近的多模态大型语言模型（MLLMs）作为具身智能体具有强大的潜力，但它们在视觉基础环境中的协作能力仍未得到充分探索。为了填补这一空白，我们引入了MECoBench，这是一个多模态具身协作基准，配备了一个评估平台，涵盖多样的真实世界任务、两种合作结构和三种协作模式。通过对各种MLLMs进行广泛实验，我们总结了三个关键发现：（i）协作通常能改善具身任务的完成，但其益处取决于在协作收益与协调复杂性之间取得平衡。（ii）沟通对于协作收益至关重要，而最佳协作模式取决于团队规模和模型能力。（iii）此外，协作在噪声先验和探索条件下提高了鲁棒性。总体而言，MECoBench为理解多模态具身协作的机制和局限提供了一个系统性的测试平台。代码和数据集可在https://github.com/q-i-n-g/MECoBench获取。

Original abstract: Recent multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have strong potential as embodied agents, but their ability to collaborate in visually grounded environments remains underexplored. To address this gap, we introduce MECoBench, a multimodal embodied cooperation benchmark with an evaluation platform spanning diverse real-world tasks, two cooperation structures, and three collaboration modes. Through extensive experiments across various MLLMs, we summarize three key findings: (i) Collaboration generally improves embodied task completion, but its benefits depend on balancing collaborative gains against coordination complexity. (ii) Communication is essential to collaboration gains, while the best collaboration mode depends on team size and model capability. (iii) Moreover, collaboration improves robustness under noisy priors and exploration conditions. Generally, MECoBench provides a systematic testbed for understanding the mechanisms and limits of multimodal embodied collaboration. Code and dataset are available at https://github.com/q-i-n-g/MECoBench.

</details>

# cs.DB [[Back]](#toc)

### [77] [DA-Studio: An Agentic System for End-to-End Data Analysis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31423v1)
*Yizhe Liu,Shaolei Zhang,Ju Fan*

Main category: cs.DB

Selection reason: 端到端数据分析agent，含多步工作流、代码执行与沙箱，可迁移至coding agent

TL;DR: DA-Studio是一个自主、沙盒化、可检查的端到端数据分析交互系统，通过迭代动作生成和代码执行，逐步构建多步骤工作流并暴露中间结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM分析工具主要关注孤立子任务，缺乏对完整、基于执行的多步骤工作流的支持。

Method: DA-Studio集成了动作结构化的分析后端、沙盒化执行工作区和浏览器界面，通过迭代生成动作、执行代码和整合反馈来逐步构建分析步骤。

Result: 该系统能够从原始文件和自然语言请求中自主构建可执行的分析步骤，并实时暴露中间结果和工件。

Conclusion: DA-Studio实现了自主、沙盒化和可检查的数据分析，填补了现有工具在完整工作流支持上的空白。

中文摘要：真实世界的数据分析是一个多步骤的过程，涉及异构输入，而不仅仅是产生最终答案。一个实用的系统应当能够自主地组织多步骤工作流，在沙盒化和可控的环境中执行生成的代码，并通过可见的动作轨迹和中间工件保持可检查性。然而，现有的基于LLM的分析工具往往强调孤立的子任务，对完整的、基于执行的工作流支持有限。我们提出了DA-Studio（数据分析工作室），一个交互式网页演示系统，用于端到端的数据分析，具有自主性、沙盒化和可检查性。DA-Studio集成了动作结构化的分析后端、沙盒化的执行工作空间以及用于任务设置、流式动作轨迹、工件预览、代码编辑和重新运行以及报告导出的浏览器界面。通过迭代的动作生成、代码执行和反馈整合，它从原始文件和自然语言请求中逐步构建可执行的分析步骤，并在整个过程中暴露中间结果和工件。

Original abstract: Real-world data analysis is a multi-step process over heterogeneous inputs rather than merely producing a final answer. A practical system should autonomously organize multi-step workflows, execute generated code in a sandboxed and controllable environment, and remain inspectable through visible action traces and intermediate artifacts. Existing LLM-based analysis tools, however, often emphasize isolated subtasks, leaving limited support for complete execution-grounded workflows.
  We present DA-Studio (Data Analysis Studio), an interactive web-based demo system for end-to-end data analysis that is autonomous, sandboxed, and inspectable. DA-Studio integrates an action-structured analysis backend, a sandboxed execution workspace, and a browser interface for task setup, streamed action traces, artifact preview, code editing and rerunning, and report export. Through iterative action generation, code execution, and feedback incorporation, it incrementally constructs executable analysis steps from raw files and natural-language requests while exposing intermediate results and artifacts throughout the process.

</details>

### [78] [FinPersona-Bench: A Benchmark for Longitudinal Psychometric Stability of Autonomous Financial Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31522v2)
*Muhammad Usman Safder,Ayesha Gull,Rania Elbadry,Fan Zhang,Yankai Chen,Xueqing Peng,Xue,Liu,Preslav Nakov,Zhuohan Xie*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 研究金融agent长期行为稳定性并提出测评benchmark，可迁移至agent安全与评测

TL;DR: LLM作为金融代理时，行为指令随时间衰减（MSD），引入FinPersona-Bench基准测试，发现重新锚定效果因代理特征和市场环境而异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM被部署为金融代理时，初始行为指令随时间推移失去影响力，导致决策偏离初衷，需要量化测量这种现象。

Method: 构建FinPersona-Bench仿真基准，将价格与价值解耦，定义三种失败模式（无信号交易、恐慌抛售、忽视价值），评估18个LLM在不同行为特征下的表现，并测试定期指令重新锚定的效果。

Result: MSD随时间累积且模型依赖；崩盘场景中重新锚定使行为差距增长4.4倍；重新锚定对保守代理有益，但对激进代理有害。

Conclusion: 可靠长期部署需要根据代理特征和市场制度进行选择性、指令感知的重新锚定。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被部署为自主金融代理，并初始化为明确的行动指令，如“保本”或“避免投机性押注”，这些指令旨在指导整个部署过程中的每一个决策。然而，在实践中，随着市场背景在长时间跨度内累积，这些指令逐渐失去其行为影响力，我们将这种现象形式化为指令显著性衰减（MSD）。为了客观衡量MSD，我们引入了FinPersona-Bench，这是一个模拟基准测试，其中合成市场将可观察价格与隐藏的基本价值分离，从而能够在三种失败模式下进行可假说评估：在平静市场中无信号交易、崩盘期间恐慌性抛售、以及在投机泡沫期间忽视基本价值。评估18个领先前沿和开源LLM（每个被分配三个行为特征之一，从严格保本到激进增长）表明，MSD随时间累积且具有模型依赖性。在崩盘场景中，静态代理与接收定期指令重新锚定的代理之间的行为差距从模拟的第一个季度到最后一个季度增长了4.4倍。指令重新锚定的效果并非一律正面：在低信号市场中，它始终帮助保守代理，但在相同环境下却会加剧激进代理的不良行为。这些发现表明，可靠的长期部署需要基于代理特征和市场制度进行选择性的、对指令敏感的重新锚定。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as autonomous financial agents initialized with explicit behavioral mandates such as "preserve capital" or "avoid speculative bets" that are meant to govern every decision throughout deployment. In practice, however, as market context accumulates over long horizons, these mandates gradually lose their behavioral influence, a phenomenon we formalize as Mandate Salience Decay (MSD). To measure MSD objectively, we introduce FinPersona-Bench, a simulation benchmark in which a synthetic market decouples observable price from hidden fundamental value, enabling falsifiable evaluation across three failure modes: trading without signal in calm markets, panic-selling during crashes, and ignoring fundamental value during speculative bubbles. Evaluating 18 leading frontier and open-source LLMs, each assigned one of three behavioral profiles ranging from strict capital preservation to aggressive growth, shows that MSD compounds over time and is model-dependent. In crash scenarios, the behavioral gap between static agents and those receiving periodic mandate re-grounding grows 4.4x from the first to the final quarter of the simulation. The effects of mandate re-grounding are not uniformly positive: it consistently helps conservative agents in low-signal markets but actively worsens behavior for aggressive agents in the same setting. These findings suggest that reliable long-horizon deployment requires selective, mandate-aware re-grounding based on agent profile and market regime.

</details>


### [79] [Seeing Is Not Sharing: Some Vision-Language Models Overestimate Common Ground in Asymmetric Dialogue](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31719v1)
*Nan Li,Albert Gatt,Massimo Poesio*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: VLM对话共同理解研究，对agent在多轮交互中的上下文管理有潜在启发。

TL;DR: VLM在对话中过度依赖地图内容（视觉或文本）来预测对齐，混淆了潜在与已建立的共同基础，而非追踪对话中的奠基过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究VLM能否区分对话中“可能共享”与“已经共享”的内容，即通过奠基建立共同理解的能力。

Method: 在HCRC MapTask对话的13,077个指代表达上构建解释匹配任务，系统控制对话上下文和地图信息访问（真实图像、文本描述、非信息性图像）来评估VLM。

Result: 真实地图图像提升整体性能但导致过度预测对齐；文本描述重现偏差，非信息性图像抑制对齐；偏差由任务相关地图内容驱动，且以牺牲非对齐案例准确性为代价；模型依赖静态地图线索而非对话历史中的奠基过程。

Conclusion: VLM在对话中倾向于将地图内容（视觉或文本）视为相互理解的证据，混淆潜在与已建立的共同基础，且此模式在多个模型中存在，尤其以Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct最为明显。

中文摘要：在协作对话中，共同感知并不保证共同解释。通过互动才能建立相互理解。我们研究视觉语言模型（VLM）是否能够通过奠基（grounding）区分对话参与者之间可能共享的内容与已经共享的内容。我们将此构建为一个基于HCRC MapTask对话中13,077个带注释的指代表达的解释匹配任务，并在系统控制对话上下文和地图信息访问的情况下评估VLM。我们的结果表明，提供真实地图图像提高了整体性能，但使模型倾向于过度预测对齐。相同地图内容的文本描述也重现了这种偏差，而非信息性图像则完全抑制了对齐预测，表明偏差是由任务相关的地图内容驱动的，而不是视觉通道。这种改进是以降低非对齐案例的准确性为代价的。校准分析和指代链追踪进一步表明，模型依赖于地图上的静态指代线索，而不是跟踪通过对话历史展开的奠基过程。我们在Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct中最清晰地观察到这些模式，并且在来自两个架构族的另外四个模型中也不同程度地观察到。在表现出偏差的模型中，地图内容（无论是视觉呈现还是文本呈现）都被视为相互理解的证据，混淆了潜在共同基础和已建立的共同基础。

Original abstract: In collaborative dialogue, shared perception does not guarantee shared interpretation. Mutual understanding must be established through interaction. We investigate whether vision-language models (VLMs) can distinguish what could be shared from what has been shared between dialogue participants through grounding. We formulate this as an interpretation-matching task on 13,077 annotated reference expressions from HCRC MapTask dialogues, and evaluate VLMs under systematically controlled manipulations of dialogue context and map-information access. Our results show that providing authentic map images improves overall performance but shifts models toward over-predicting alignment. Textual descriptions of the same map content reproduce this bias, while non-informative images suppress alignment predictions entirely, indicating that the bias is driven by task-relevant map content, not the visual channel. This improvement comes at the cost of degraded accuracy on non-aligned cases. Calibration analysis and reference-chain tracking further suggest that models rely on static referential cues on the maps rather than tracking how grounding unfolds through dialogue history. We observe these patterns most clearly in Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct and, to varying degrees, in four additional models from two architecture families. In models that exhibit the bias, map content, whether presented visually or textually, is treated as evidence of mutual understanding, conflating potential with established common ground.

</details>


### [80] [DigitalCoach: Communication and Grounding Gaps in Human and Agentic Computer Use Coaching](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31980v1)
*Meng Chen,Anya Ji,Tsung-Han Wu,Tobias Maringgele,David M. Chan,Alane Suhr,Amy Pavel*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 人类-agent计算机使用教学数据集，对agent协作与接地有参考意义

TL;DR: 提出DigitalCoach多模态数据集，评估AI模型能否教人类使用软件，发现模型提供更多直接指令但缺乏解释和视觉上下文，导致学习者被动学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索智能体是否不仅能自动化任务，还能教会人类使用软件。

Method: 构建包含72场人类专家-新手辅导会话的多模态数据集（DigitalCoach），包括屏幕录制、输入事件和对话，并用其评估SOTA模型。

Result: 自动评估显示模型比人类更倾向于直接指令，较少解释和错误诊断；交互评估显示模型导致学习者被动跟随指令，缺乏深度参与和视觉定位。

Conclusion: DigitalCoach为协作和主动的计算机使用辅导智能体奠定基础。

中文摘要：智能体越来越能够自动化软件任务，但它们能否教会人类自己使用软件？我们引入了DigitalCoach，这是一个多模态数据集，包含72个人类专家-新手计算机使用辅导会话，共计22,752个对话轮次，基于五个软件应用程序的28.1小时屏幕和输入事件记录。我们利用DigitalCoach评估最先进的模型是否能够教会人类使用计算机。自动评估显示，模型在辅导方式上与人类不同：模型提供更直接的指令，但更少的解释、错误诊断和知识检查问题。当我们固定辅导方法时，模型生成的语句与人类参考相似，但在视觉上下文方面表现不佳。交互评估证实，模型辅导员导致学习者被动地遵循指令，缺乏更深层次的参与，并且在视觉定位方面存在不足。DigitalCoach为协作和主动的计算机使用辅导智能体奠定了基础。

Original abstract: Agents are increasingly capable of automating software tasks, but can they teach humans how to use software themselves? We introduce DigitalCoach, a multimodal dataset of 72 human expert-novice computer use coaching sessions consisting of 22,752 dialogue turns grounded in 28.1 hours of screen and input event recordings across five software applications. We use DigitalCoach to evaluate whether state-of-the-art models can teach humans how to use computers. Automated evaluation shows that models differ from humans in how they coach: models provide more direct instructions, but fewer explanations, error diagnoses, and knowledge-check questions. When we fix the coaching method, models produce utterances similar to human references yet poorly grounded in visual context. Interactive evaluation confirms that model coaches cause learners to passively follow instructions without deeper engagement and fall short in visual grounding. DigitalCoach lays a foundation for collaborative and proactive computer use coaching agents.

</details>


### [81] [Reinforcement Learning with Metacognitive Feedback Elicits Faithful Uncertainty Expression in LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.32032v1)
*Gabrielle Kaili-May Liu,Avi Caciularu,Gal Yona,Idan Szpektor,Arman Cohan*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 元认知反馈RL提升不确定性表达，可迁移至agent自我评估和训练信号

TL;DR: 提出基于元认知反馈的强化学习（RLMF）和元认知数据选择方法，用于提升大语言模型的忠实校准能力，实验显示RLMF在多项任务上达到最先进性能，且优于标准强化学习达63%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在元认知能力上存在系统性缺陷（如高置信度幻觉、无法识别知识边界），影响可信赖性；因此需要提升模型自我判断性能的能力，以改进其整体表现和校准。

Method: 提出两种机制：1）RLMF：在偏好优化中利用模型自我判断质量作为反馈信号进行强化学习；2）元认知数据选择：基于自我判断筛选高价值训练样本。采用两阶段解耦方法：先校准置信度分数，再映射为自然语言不确定性。

Result: RLMF在多个任务上实现可泛化的最先进忠实校准，同时保持准确性；相比标准强化学习，性能提升高达63%，且增强了模型评估和表达自身能力极限的能力。

Conclusion: RLMF是增强LLM元认知的有前景范式，可提升能力与对齐，并表明元认知性能可作为有效的RL信号克服先前方法的局限性。

中文摘要：元认知是智能的关键组成部分，它描述了监控和调节自身认知过程的能力。然而，大语言模型（LLM）在关键的元认知能力上表现出系统性缺陷：它们以高置信度产生幻觉，未能识别知识边界，并歪曲其内部不确定性——这损害了可信赖性和可靠性。由于监控任务性能并根据表现调整行为是元认知的核心，我们假设能够准确判断自身性能的模型更有可能改进其性能。我们通过两种新颖机制实现了这一想法：基于元认知反馈的强化学习（RLMF），一种在偏好优化过程中根据模型自我判断性能的质量来细化完成排序的范式；以及元认知数据选择，它使用类似的自我判断来识别高价值训练样本，优于朴素主动学习。我们将这些创新应用于忠实校准（FC）问题，该任务本身本质上就是元认知的：目标是使表达的不确定性与内在不确定性对齐，即使对于前沿LLM来说也很困难。我们采用两阶段解耦方法，首先使用这些方法校准模型自我报告置信度分数的忠实性，然后通过有针对性的输出编辑将其映射到自然且上下文可适应的语言不确定性。大量实验表明，RLMF在保留准确性的同时，在多样化任务上实现了可泛化的最先进FC。此外，RLMF优于标准强化学习高达63%，同时增强了模型评估和表达自身能力极限的能力。这使RLMF成为增强LLM元认知以提升能力和对齐的有前景范式，并表明元认知性能可作为有效的RL信号来克服先前内在反馈方法的局限性。

Original abstract: Metacognition is a critical component of intelligence that describes the ability to monitor and regulate one's own cognitive processes. Yet LLMs exhibit systemic deficiencies in key metacognitive faculties: they hallucinate with high confidence, fail to recognize knowledge boundaries, and misrepresent their internal uncertainty--undermining trustworthiness and reliability. Since monitoring task performance and adapting behavior accordingly are central to metacognition, we posit that models capable of accurately judging their own performance are better positioned to improve it. We operationalize this idea via two novel mechanisms: reinforcement learning with metacognitive feedback (RLMF), a paradigm to refine completion rankings during preference optimization based on the quality of a model's self-judgments of performance, and metacognitive data selection, which uses similar self-judgments to identify high-value training examples, outperforming naive active learning. We apply these innovations to the problem of faithful calibration (FC), a task that is itself fundamentally metacognitive: the goal is to align expressed with intrinsic uncertainty, difficult even for frontier LLMs. We adopt a two-stage, decoupled approach, first using these methods to calibrate the faithfulness of models' self-reported confidence scores, then mapping to natural, context-adaptable linguistic uncertainty via targeted output editing. Extensive experiments show RLMF achieves generalizable, state-of-the-art FC on diverse tasks while preserving accuracy. Further, RLMF surpasses standard RL by up to 63% while enhancing models' ability to assess and express their own capability limits. This positions RLMF as a promising paradigm to enhance LLM metacognition toward improved abilities and alignment, and suggests metacognitive performance as an effective RL signal to overcome limits of prior intrinsic feedback methods.

</details>

### [82] [MIRTH: Mutual-Information Reasoning with Temporal Hubs for Vision-Language-Action Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31167v1)
*Hao Sun,Yu Song,Shiyu Teng,Ziwei Niu,Yen-Wei Chen*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: MIRTH VLA框架包含时间记忆和推理，对agent设计有潜在启发。

TL;DR: MIRTH通过时间记忆、潜在推理标记和并行解码，解决了VLA模型的时间短视、推理鸿沟和推理低效问题，在模拟和真实场景中达到SOTA，并具备错误恢复能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA模型存在三个局限：时间短视（忽略历史动态）、推理鸿沟（高级指令与低级动作脱节）、推理低效（自回归标量解码）。

Method: 提出MIRTH框架，包含三个创新：1) 双尺度时间记忆枢纽（压缩长期场景和短期运动）；2) 基于互信息的潜在推理标记（对齐多模态与动作）；3) 并行动作解码（向量预测取代自回归）。

Result: 在LIBERO模拟和LeRobot真实平台上达到SOTA性能，并展现出涌现的错误恢复能力。

Conclusion: MIRTH有效解决了VLA模型的三大挑战，提升了控制性能和鲁棒性，代码已开源。

中文摘要：VLA模型已成为将网络规模数据的语义知识迁移到物理机器人控制的有力范式。然而，当前的单帧架构存在固有局限：忽略历史动态的时间短视、高级指令与低级电机指令之间的推理鸿沟，以及因自回归标量解码导致的推理低效。在这项工作中，我们提出了MIRTH，一个旨在解决这些挑战的统一框架。MIRTH通过三项关键创新增强了预训练的VLA骨干网络：（1）双尺度时间记忆枢纽，将长期场景演变和短期运动趋势压缩为紧凑嵌入；（2）通过互信息目标优化的潜在推理标记，雕刻出语义计划空间以对齐多模态上下文与动作轨迹；（3）并行动作解码方案，用向量级预测替代自回归生成以最大化控制吞吐量。在LIBERO模拟基准和真实世界LeRobot平台上的广泛评估表明，MIRTH达到了最先进的性能，并展现出涌现的错误恢复能力。代码和收集的数据集发布于http://github.com/kiva12138/mirth。

Original abstract: VLA models have emerged as a powerful paradigm for transferring semantic knowledge from web-scale data to physical robotic control. However, current single-frame architectures suffer from intrinsic limitations: temporal myopia that discards historical dynamics, reasoning gaps between high-level instructions and low-level motor commands, and inference inefficiency due to autoregressive scalar decoding. In this work, we propose MIRTH, a unified framework designed to address these challenges. MIRTH augments a pretrained VLA backbone with three key innovations: (1) dual-scale temporal memory hubs that compress long-term scene evolution and short-term motion trends into compact embeddings; (2) latent reasoning tokens optimized via a mutual-information objective carving out a semantic plan space to align multimodal context with action trajectories; and (3) a parallel action decoding scheme that replaces autoregressive generation with vector-wise prediction to maximize control throughput. Extensive evaluations on the LIBERO simulation benchmark and a real-world LeRobot platform demonstrate that MIRTH achieves state-of-the-art performance and exhibiting emergent error recovery capabilities. The codes and collected datasets are released at http://github.com/kiva12138/mirth.

</details>


### [83] [3D HAMSTER: Bridging Planning and Control in Hierarchical Vision Language Action Models through 3D Trajectory Guidance](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31329v2)
*Dongyoon Hwang,Byungkun Lee,Dongjin Kim,Hyojin Jang,Hoiyeong Jin,Jueun Mun,Minho Park,Hojoon Lee,Hyunseung Kim,Jaegul Choo*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 分层VLA机器人规划架构，可迁移至通用agent规划

TL;DR: 3D HAMSTER通过让VLM直接预测3D轨迹并集成到点云策略中，解决了2D指导导致的几何扭曲问题，显著提升了机器人操作的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的层次化VLA方法使用2D轨迹指导低层策略，但低层策略在3D空间操作时，2D指导缺乏深度信息导致几何扭曲，限制了泛化能力。

Method: 在VLM中增加专用深度编码器和密集深度重建目标，使其直接预测3D路点序列，然后这些3D轨迹被直接输入到基于点云的低层策略中。

Result: 在3D轨迹预测、仿真和真实世界操作中，3D HAMSTER均优于专有VLM和2D指导基线，尤其在视觉外观变化和未见过的语言、空间条件下提升最大。

Conclusion: 3D HAMSTER通过直接输出度量可靠的3D轨迹，有效弥合了高层规划与低层3D控制之间的维度差距，提升了机器人操作的泛化性和鲁棒性。

中文摘要：层次化视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型将高层规划与低层控制解耦，以提高机器人操作的泛化能力。最近的工作使用由视觉-语言模型（VLM）预测的2D末端执行器轨迹作为下游策略的显式指导。然而，最先进的低层策略在点云上的3D度量空间中操作，馈送缺乏深度的2D指导迫使每个路点被分配其下方场景表面的深度，产生几何扭曲的轨迹。我们提出3D HAMSTER，一个层次化框架，通过让规划器直接输出度量可靠的3D轨迹来弥合这一差距。我们增强了VLM，添加了专用的深度编码器和密集深度重建目标，以预测3D路点序列，这些序列直接集成到基于点云的低层策略中。在3D轨迹预测、仿真和真实世界操作中，3D HAMSTER始终优于专有VLM和2D指导的基线，在外观变化和未见过的语言、空间和视觉条件下增益最大。项目页面：https://davian-robotics.github.io/3D_HAMSTER/。

Original abstract: Hierarchical Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models decouple high-level planning from low-level control to improve generalization in robot manipulation. Recent work in this paradigm uses 2D end-effector trajectories predicted by a Vision-Language Model (VLM) as explicit guidance for a downstream policy. However, state-of-the-art low-level policies operate in 3D metric space on point clouds, and feeding them 2D guidance that lacks depth forces each waypoint to be assigned the depth of whatever scene surface lies beneath it, producing geometrically distorted trajectories. We propose 3D HAMSTER, a hierarchical framework that closes this gap by having the planner directly output metrically reliable 3D trajectories. We augment a VLM with a dedicated depth encoder and a dense depth reconstruction objective to predict 3D waypoint sequences, which are directly integrated into a pointcloudbased low-level policy. Across 3D trajectory prediction, simulation, and real-world manipulation, 3D HAMSTER consistently outperforms proprietary VLMs and 2D-guided baselines, with the largest gains under appearance-altering shifts and unseen language, spatial, and visual conditions. The project page is available at https://davian-robotics.github.io/3D_HAMSTER/.

</details>


### [84] [Stage-Transition Dense Reward Modeling for Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31377v1)
*Yang Yang,Bingjie Chen,Zihan Wang,Yizhe Li,Guoping Pan,Yi Cheng,Houde Liu*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 阶段过渡密集奖励建模用于RL，可启发agent训练奖励设计

TL;DR: 提出STDR框架，通过从专家视频中推断阶段结构并生成密集奖励信号，有效提升了长周期机器人操作任务的强化学习效率和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习在长周期机器人操作中面临稀疏奖励问题，手工设计密集奖励成本高且泛化性差。

Method: STDR框架利用语义理解从专家演示中提取任务阶段结构，在线训练时提供阶段转换奖励和阶段内进度奖励，并集成OOD检测和抓取调节模块以防止奖励黑客。

Result: 在14个模拟任务和真实机器人实验中，STDR相比多个基线显著提升样本效率和成功率，部分任务甚至超越手工设计的密集奖励。

Conclusion: STDR能够从无结构专家视频中学习有效的密集奖励，提升强化学习性能，同时具备对视觉噪声的鲁棒性。

中文摘要：针对长周期机器人操作任务，强化学习常受限于稀疏和延迟的奖励，而手动设计密集的塑形信号成本高昂且对环境变化和物体配置脆弱。本文提出阶段转换密集奖励（STDR），一种视觉奖励学习框架，将非结构化专家视频转化为逻辑上合理的密集奖励，用于从头训练强化学习智能体。STDR利用语义理解从演示中推断任务的阶段结构，并在在线训练期间提供两种互补的学习信号：（i）阶段转换反馈，提供目标导向的奖励，以及（ii）阶段内进度反馈，为完成每个阶段提供细粒度指导。此外，集成了分布外（OOD）检测机制和抓取调节模块，以增强鲁棒性并防止奖励黑客攻击。在MetaWorld、ManiSkill和Franka Kitchen上的14个操作任务上的实验表明，STDR在多个基线上持续提高了样本效率和成功率，并在多个具有挑战性的任务上匹配或超越了手工设计的密集奖励。真实机器人评估进一步表明，STDR在成功执行时分配稳定、与进度一致的奖励，同时在失败时产生适当低的奖励，表明其对视觉噪声的鲁棒性和跨设置的更好校准的奖励分配。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning for long-horizon robotic manipulation is often limited by sparse and delayed rewards, while manually designing dense shaping signals is costly and brittle to changes in environments and object configurations. This work proposes Stage-Transition Dense Reward (STDR), a visual reward-learning framework that converts unstructured expert videos into logically grounded dense rewards for training RL agents from scratch. STDR leverages semantic understanding to infer a task's stage structure from demonstrations, and delivers two complementary learning signals during online training: (i) stage-transition feedback that provides goal-directed reward, and (ii) within-stage progress feedback that supplies fine-grained guidance toward completing each stage. Furthermore, an out-of-distribution (OOD) detection mechanism and a grasping regulation module are integrated to enhance robustness and prevent reward hacking. Experiments on 14 manipulation tasks across MetaWorld, ManiSkill, and Franka Kitchen show that STDR consistently improves sample efficiency and success rates over multiple baselines, and matches or surpasses handcrafted dense rewards on several challenging tasks. Real-robot evaluations further indicate that STDR assigns stable, progress-aligned rewards on successful executions while producing appropriately low rewards for failures, suggesting robustness to visual noise and better-calibrated reward assignment across settings.

</details>


### [85] [Z-1: Efficient Reinforcement Learning for Vision-Language-Action Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31846v1)
*Lang Cao,Renhong Chen,Luyi Li,Peng Wang,Mofan Peng,Yitong Li*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: VLA模型的RL后训练框架，含GRPO策略，可迁移至coding agent强化学习。

TL;DR: 提出Z-1，一种基于GRPO的强化学习后训练框架，用于改进基于流的VLA模型，在24个RoboCasa任务上平均成功率提升13.2%，超越SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA模型受限于行为克隆或监督微调，无法从自身失败中学习改进。

Method: 基于π0.5模型，使用公开RoboCasa演示进行SFT，然后采用任务级GRPO策略，结合共享前缀轨迹构建、树状轨迹分支、完成感知奖励校准和VLM与动作专家的选择性联合训练。

Result: 在24个RoboCasa任务上平均成功率达80.6%，比SFT初始化高13.2个百分点，超过已发表的最先进模型。

Conclusion: 系统的GRPO后训练可显著提升基于流的VLA策略性能，且无需额外私有演示。

中文摘要：视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型通过连接语言指令、视觉观察和连续控制，为机器人操作提供了有前景的框架。然而，大多数现有策略仍然受限于从固定演示中进行行为克隆或监督微调（SFT），这限制了从策略自身失败中改进的机会。在本文中，我们提出了Z-1，一种用于基于流的VLA模型的强化学习（RL）后训练框架。基于π0.5，Z-1仅使用公开的RoboCasa演示进行SFT，然后在24个标准RoboCasa任务上应用任务级分组相对策略优化（GRPO）策略。为了提高在线优化的效率和稳定性，Z-1结合了共享前缀轨迹构建、树状轨迹分支、完成感知奖励校准以及VLM和动作专家的选择性联合训练。在所有24个RoboCasa任务中，Z-1实现了80.6%的平均成功率，相比其SFT初始化提高了13.2个百分点，并超过了已发表的最先进模型。这些结果表明，无需额外的私有演示，系统的GRPO后训练可以显著改进基于流的VLA策略。

Original abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models offer a promising framework for robotic manipulation by connecting language instructions, visual observations, and continuous control. However, most existing policies remain limited by behavior cloning or supervised fine-tuning (SFT) from fixed demonstrations, which provides limited opportunity to improve from the policy's own failures. In this paper, we present Z-1, a reinforcement learning (RL) post-training framework for flow-based VLA models. Built on top of $π_{0.5}$, Z-1 uses only publicly released RoboCasa demonstrations for SFT and then applies a task-wise Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) strategy across $24$ standard RoboCasa tasks. To improve the efficiency and stability of online optimization, Z-1 combines shared-prefix rollout construction, tree-structured trajectory branching, completion-aware reward calibration, and selective joint training of VLM and Action Expert. Across all $24$ RoboCasa tasks, Z-1 achieves an average success rate of $80.6\%$, improving over its SFT initialization by $13.2\%$ points and outperforms the published sota models. These results show that systematic GRPO post-training can substantially improve flow-based VLA policies without additional private demonstrations.

### [86] [MVP-Nav: Multi-layer Value Map Planner Navigator](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31919v1)
*Wenyuan Xie,Shaokai Wu,Yijin Zhou,Yanbiao Ji,Guodong Zhang,Bayram Bayramli,Qiuchang Li,Xunchu Zhou,Yue Ding,Hongtao Lu*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 提出多层级价值图规划框架，可迁移至coding agent的规划和物理约束统一方法

TL;DR: MVP-Nav通过从单目RGB图像中重建3D物理占用并融合语义优先级，实现了仅RGB的零样本物体目标导航，显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RGB-only感知缺乏深度信息导致物理不确定性和语义-物理错位，现有方法要么无几何基础要么缺物理约束，产生不安全行为。

Method: 利用3D基础模型从单目观测重建3D占用，并通过多层价值图（MVM）融合语义优先级和重建几何进行物理几何规划。

Result: 在零样本物体导航基准上显著优于现有无深度方法，达到最先进性能。

Conclusion: 结构化物理先验可以有效补偿主动深度传感器的缺失。

中文摘要：仅依靠RGB感知的零样本物体目标导航（ZSON）对具身智能体提出了根本性挑战，因为缺乏显式深度信息会导致严重的物理不确定性以及语义与物理的错位。现有方法要么依赖缺乏几何基础的高级语义推理，要么学习缺乏显式物理约束的端到端策略，常常导致语义上合理但物理上不安全的行为。在本文中，我们提出MVP-Nav，一种物理感知的仅RGB导航框架，将感知、规划和控制与真实3D世界对齐。MVP-Nav通过利用3D基础模型将2D语义实例投影到3D有向边界框，从单目观测中重建显式物理占用，形成全局空间语义表示。为了统一高级语义推理和低级物理约束，我们引入了多层价值图（MVM），将语义优先级和重建几何集成到共享成本空间中，从而实现基于物理的几何规划。在零样本物体导航基准上的大量实验表明，MVP-Nav显著优于现有的无深度方法，达到了最先进的性能，并验证了结构化物理先验可以有效补偿主动深度传感器的缺失。

Original abstract: Zero-shot Object Goal Navigation (ZSON) with RGB-only perception poses a fundamental challenge for embodied agents, as the absence of explicit depth information introduces severe physical uncertainty and semantic-physical misalignment. Existing approaches either rely on high-level semantic reasoning without geometric grounding or learn end-to-end policies that lack explicit physical constraints, often resulting in semantically plausible but physically unsafe behaviors. In this paper, we propose MVP-Nav, a physical-aware RGB-only navigation framework that aligns perception, planning, and control with the real 3D world. MVP-Nav reconstructs explicit physical occupancy from monocular observations by leveraging 3D foundation models to project 2D semantic instances into 3D oriented bounding boxes, forming a global spatial semantic representation. To unify high-level semantic reasoning and low-level physical constraints, we introduce a Multi-layer Value Map (MVM) that integrates semantic priorities and reconstructed geometry into a shared cost space, enabling physically grounded geometric planning. Extensive experiments on zero-shot object navigation benchmarks demonstrate that MVP-Nav significantly outperforms existing depth-free methods, achieving state-of-the-art performance and validating that structured physical priors can effectively compensate for the absence of active depth sensors.

### [87] [Freeform Preference Learning for Robotic Manipulation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.32027v2)
*Marcel Torne,Anubha Mahajan,Abhijnya Bhat,Chelsea Finn*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 自由形式偏好学习，其语言条件奖励模型对agent奖励设计有潜在启发

TL;DR: FPL通过自由形式人类偏好学习语言条件奖励模型，在长视域操作任务中显著提升了策略性能，并支持行为组合和测试时引导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有奖励设计在长视域操作任务中存在信号不足或模糊的问题，需要更丰富的人类偏好信息来指导策略学习。

Method: FPL让标注者定义自然语言偏好轴并提供成对偏好，学习语言条件奖励模型将轨迹和偏好标签映射为轴特定奖励，再训练奖励条件策略进行多维度优化。

Result: 在四个真实世界和两个模拟长视域操作任务中，FPL比稀疏奖励和二元偏好方法提高38个百分点，学习到密集进度信号，展现行为组合性，并支持测试时策略引导。

Conclusion: FPL有效解决了长视域操作中的奖励设计瓶颈，提升了策略性能，并提供了灵活的行为控制，无需重新训练。

中文摘要：奖励设计仍然是自主机器人策略改进的核心瓶颈，特别是在长视域操作任务中，稀疏的成功标签提供的信号过少，而二元偏好则将许多竞争性质量概念压缩成一个模糊信号。我们引入了自由形式偏好学习（FPL），一种从自由形式人类偏好中学习机器人策略的方法。FPL不要求标注者判断两个轨迹哪个总体更好，而是让它们定义自然语言偏好轴，如速度、安全性、放置质量或细心程度，并沿着每个轴提供成对偏好。这些注释用于学习一个语言条件奖励模型，该模型将轨迹和偏好标签映射到特定轴的奖励。我们使用该模型训练一个奖励条件策略，该策略在多个人类指定的维度上进行优化。在四个真实世界和两个模拟的长视域操作任务中，FPL比稀疏奖励和二元偏好方法提高了38个百分点。除了性能提升外，FPL还学习了密集的进度信号，无需显式子任务分割，展示了数据中不存在的行为组合性，并允许用户在测试时无需重新训练即可将策略引导至不同行为。博客文章及视频见 https://freeform-pl.github.io/fpl.website。

Original abstract: Reward design remains a central bottleneck for autonomous robot policy improvement, especially in long-horizon manipulation tasks where sparse success labels provide too little signal and binary preferences collapse many competing notions of quality into one ambiguous signal. We introduce Freeform Preference Learning (FPL), a method for learning robot policies from freeform human preferences. Rather than asking annotators which of two trajectories is better overall, FPL lets them define natural-language preference axes, such as speed, safety, quality of placement, or carefulness, and provide pairwise preferences along each axis. These annotations are used to learn a language-conditioned reward model that maps a trajectory and preference label to an axis-specific reward. We use this model to train a reward-conditioned policy that optimizes across the multiple human-specified dimensions. Across four real-world and two simulated long-horizon manipulation tasks, FPL improves over sparse-reward and binary-preference methods by 38 percentage points. Beyond improved performance, FPL learns dense progress signals without explicit subtask segmentation, shows compositionality of behavior not present in the data, and allows users to steer the policy towards different behaviors at test time without retraining. Blog post with videos available at https://freeform-pl.github.io/fpl.website/

</details>


### [88] [ASPIRE: Agentic /Skills Discovery for Robotics](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00272v1)
*Runyu Lu,Yubo Wu,Ethan Kou,Letian Fu,Wenli Xiao,Ajay Mandlekar,Yinzhen Xu,Guanya Shi,Ken Goldberg,Ang Chen,Mosharaf Chowdhury,Yuke Zhu,Linxi "Jim" Fan,Guanzhi Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 机器人agent持续学习系统，自主编写和修复程序，积累技能库，其故障诊断、修复和迁移机制对coding agent有借鉴意义。

TL;DR: ASPIR是一个持续学习系统，通过自主编写和优化机器人控制程序，积累可复用的技能库，在多个基准任务上显著超越先前方法，并实现零样本泛化和sim-to-real迁移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统机器人编程需要处理多模态感知、物理接触动力学和多样化配置失败，过程复杂且耗时，亟需自动化方法减少人工干预。

Method: ASPIR包含三个组件：闭环执行引擎（支持自主故障诊断、修复和验证）、可扩展技能库（蒸馏修复为可复用知识）、进化搜索（生成多样化任务序列和程序）。

Result: 在LIBERO-Pro扰动下提升77%，Robosuite双臂交接提升72%，BEHAVIOR-1K长时域任务提升32%；零样本泛化到长时域任务达31% vs 4%；仿真技能迁移到真实世界减少编程工作量。

Conclusion: ASPIR通过持续学习和技能库积累，显著提升了机器人编程的自主性、泛化能力和迁移效率，为复杂机器人任务提供了有效解决方案。

中文摘要：传统机器人编程充满挑战：它需要协调多模态感知、管理物理接触动力学，并处理多样化的配置和执行失败。我们提出了ASPIR（通过迭代机器人探索的智能技能编程），这是一个持续学习系统，能够以代码即策略的范式自主编写和优化机器人控制程序，同时将经验积累到可复用的技能库中。ASPIR发现跨任务、仿真和真实世界环境以及不同机器人形态的持久技能。它在一个开放式循环中运行，包含三个组件：(1) 一个闭环机器人执行引擎，提供细粒度的多模态轨迹，实现自主故障诊断、修复合成和验证；(2) 一个持续扩展的技能库，将验证过的修复蒸馏为可复用、可迁移的知识；(3) 进化搜索，生成多样化的任务序列和控制程序，以探索超越单轨迹的优化。ASPIR在LIBERO-Pro扰动操作任务上比先前方法提升了高达77%，在Robosuite双臂交接任务上提升72%，在BEHAVIOR-1K长时域家庭任务上提升32%。其积累的技能库还能实现零样本泛化到未见过的长时域任务：在LIBERO-Pro长时域任务上，ASPIR成功率达到31%，而先前方法即使使用了测试时推理和重试也仅有4%。最后，仿真中发现的技能提供了从仿真到真实迁移的初步证据，显著减少了不同机器人形态和API下的真实机器人编程工作量。

Original abstract: Traditional robot programming is challenging: it requires orchestrating multimodal perception, managing physical contact dynamics, and handling diverse configurations and execution failures. We introduce ASPIRE (Agentic Skill Programming through Iterative Robot Exploration), a continual learning system that autonomously writes and refines robot control programs in a code-as-policy paradigm while compounding experience into a reusable skill library. ASPIRE discovers skills that persist across tasks, simulation and real-world settings, and embodiments. It operates in an open-ended loop with three components: (1) a closed-loop robot execution engine that exposes fine-grained multimodal traces, enabling autonomous failure diagnosis, repair synthesis, and validation; (2) a continually expanding skill library that distills validated fixes into reusable, transferable knowledge; and (3) evolutionary search that generates diverse task sequences and control programs to explore beyond single-trajectory refinement. ASPIRE surpasses prior methods by up to 77% on LIBERO-Pro manipulation under perturbation, 72% on Robosuite bimanual handover, and 32% on BEHAVIOR-1K long-horizon household tasks. Its accumulated library also enables zero-shot generalization to unseen long-horizon tasks: on LIBERO-Pro Long, ASPIRE achieves 31% success versus 4% for prior methods despite their use of test-time reasoning and retries. Finally, simulation-discovered skills provide initial evidence of sim-to-real transfer, substantially reducing real-robot programming effort across different embodiments and robot APIs.

</details>

# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [89] [Learning from Failure: Inference-Time Self-Improvement for Computer-Use Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31270v1)
*Xueqiao Sun,Xiaohan Wang,Ludwig Schmidt,Serena Yeung-Levy,Yuhui Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 计算机使用agent失败驱动自改进，直接相关coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出一种失败驱动的自我改进循环，通过LLM诊断失败并生成代码补丁，在不增加训练成本的情况下将OpenCUA-72B在OSWorld上的成功率提升6.6个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自我改进方法仅利用成功轨迹，忽略了包含模型弱点信息的失败轨迹，因此探索利用失败轨迹来改进代理。

Method: 使用LLM诊断失败模式，提出推理时解决方案，并生成经人工轻度验证的代码补丁来升级代理。

Result: 在OSWorld基准上，OpenCUA-72B模型成功率从42.3%提升至48.9%，提升6.6个百分点，无额外训练成本，仅适度推理开销。

Conclusion: 失败驱动的自我改进是成功管道的有效补充，能够更高效地改进代理。

中文摘要：计算机使用代理（Computer-use agents）利用多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）来操作计算机并完成任务，因其实用性和多功能性而备受关注。开发这些代理的一个主要挑战是收集大规模、高质量的轨迹数据。标准方法通过自我改进循环生成合成数据：将代理置于可验证的环境中，并基于其成功轨迹进行迭代微调。尽管这种方法有效，但它只利用了成功的轨迹，丢弃了失败的轨迹，而失败轨迹包含了关于模型弱点的丰富信息。在这项工作中，我们探索了一种互补的失败驱动自我改进循环，这是一种以数据为中心的范式，将失败轨迹转化为代理的改进。具体来说，我们使用LLM来诊断失败模式、提出推理时解决方案，并生成经过人工轻度验证的代码补丁，从而升级代理。我们使用最先进的OpenCUA-72B模型在OSWorld基准上验证了该方法，将成功率从42.3%提高到48.9%，提升了6.6个百分点，且没有额外的训练成本，仅需适度的推理开销。我们的结果表明，失败驱动的自我改进是基于成功的管道的可行补充，能够实现更高效的代理改进。

Original abstract: Computer-use agents, which leverage multimodal large language models (MLLMs) to operate computers and complete tasks, have attracted significant attention for their utility and versatility. A major challenge in developing these agents is collecting large-scale, high-quality trajectories. The standard approach generates synthetic data through a self-improving loop: an agent is placed in a verifiable environment and iteratively fine-tuned on its successful trajectories. Despite its effectiveness, this paradigm exploits only successful trajectories and discards the failed ones, even though failures carry rich information about a model's weaknesses. In this work, we explore a complementary failure-driven self-improvement loop, a data-centric paradigm that turns failed trajectories into agent improvements. Specifically, we employ an LLM to diagnose failure modes, propose inference-time solutions, and generate code patches -- lightly verified by humans -- that upgrade the agent. We validate this approach with the state-of-the-art OpenCUA-72B model on the OSWorld benchmark, improving the success rate from 42.3% to 48.9%, a gain of 6.6 percentage points, without any additional training cost and with only modest inference overhead. Our results demonstrate that failure-driven self-improvement is a viable complement to success-based pipelines, enabling more efficient agent improvement.

</details>


### [90] [WorldRoamBench: An Open-World Benchmark for Long-Horizon Stability of Interactive World Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31672v3)
*Ting-Bing Xu,Jiacheng Sui,Zhe Gao,Kewei Shi,Wenjin Yang,Zhicheng Liu,Zhaoxu Sun,Mingchao Sun,Hongyu Pan,Fan Jiang,Mu Xu,Qi Fan,Yang Gao,Yong Li,Baoquan Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 交互世界模型长期稳定性基准，评测长期agent的稳定性有潜在参考价值。

TL;DR: WorldRoamBench是一个四个维度的开放世界基准，用于评估交互式世界模型的长期稳定性，包括动作、视觉、物理和记忆，测试发现现有模型均无法全面满足要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准仅在轨迹层面评估动作遵循，忽略记忆和交互物理，无法全面测试IWMs的长期稳定性。

Method: 提出WorldRoamBench基准，包含四个维度的创新评估：逐帧动作度量、基于片段的漂移度量、可控性门控物理评估、动作解耦记忆评估，以及600多个测试用例覆盖多种场景和视角。

Result: 评估10多个模型表明，没有模型能可靠满足所有维度，最好模型仅得中等分数。

Conclusion: WorldRoamBench推动了稳定、物理基础、记忆忠实且可部署的IWMs的发展。

中文摘要：尽管交互式世界模型（IWMs）取得了快速进展，但现有基准仅在轨迹层面评估动作遵循，并忽略了记忆和交互物理。我们引入了WorldRoamBench，一个针对长期稳定性的开放世界基准，涵盖四个维度，每个维度都有量身定制的创新：（i）动作：逐帧动作度量，避免了跨模型语义尺度差异，并暴露了轨迹掩盖的失败；（ii）视觉：基于片段的漂移度量，捕捉了起始与结束比较所遗漏的非单调中期序列崩溃；（iii）物理：基于可控性门控的评估，涵盖力学、光学和3D一致性，在忠实动作执行下对合理性进行评分；（iv）记忆：动作解耦协议，通过过渡局部化的3D点云重建评估场景记忆，并通过跟踪加VLM推理评估主体记忆。该基准包含600多个测试用例，涵盖自然、城市和室内场景，以第一/第三人称视角和WASD 10-60秒连续交互。评估10多个开源/闭源模型发现，没有一个能可靠满足所有维度；即使最好的模型也只获得中等分数。在WorldRoamBench上的进步是朝着稳定、物理基础、记忆忠实且可在现实世界应用中部署的IWMs迈进的步骤。

Original abstract: Despite rapid progress in interactive world models (IWMs), existing benchmarks evaluate action following only at trajectory level and ignore memory and interaction physics. We introduce WorldRoamBench, an open-world benchmark for long-horizon stability across four dimensions, each with tailored innovations: (i) Action: per-frame action metric bypassing cross-model semantic scale disparity and exposing failures hidden by trajectory; (ii) Vision: segment-based drift metric capturing non-monotonic mid-sequence collapse missed by start-vs-end comparisons; (iii) Physics: controllability-gated evaluation over mechanics, optics, and 3D consistency, scoring plausibility under faithful action execution; (iv) Memory: action-decoupled protocol evaluating scene memory via transition-localized 3D point-cloud reconstruction and subject memory via tracking-plus-VLM reasoning. The benchmark comprises 600+ test cases across Nature, Urban, and Indoor scenes in first/third-person views with WASD 10-60s continuous interaction. Evaluating 10+ open/closed-source models reveals none reliably satisfies all dimensions; even the best achieves only moderate scores. Advances on WorldRoamBench are steps toward IWMs that are stable, physically grounded, memory-faithful, and deployable in real-world applications.

</details>


### [91] [EgoSafetyBench: A Diagnostic Egocentric Video Benchmark for Evaluating Embodied VLMs as Runtime Safety Guards](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00218v1)
*Siddhant Panpatil,Arth Singh,Mijin Koo,Chaeyun Kim,Haon Park,Dasol Choi*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 评估VLM作为安全防护的基准，直接关系agent可靠性与安全控制。

TL;DR: EgoSafetyBench通过自我中心视频基准测试VLM作为安全守卫，发现它们常错过情境性危险且易被场景内文本误导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的二元安全基准无法区分真正不安全与表面令人警觉的场景，需要更细粒度的评估来检验VLM作为运行时安全守卫的能力。

Method: 构建了包含1200个机器人视角视频的EgoSafetyBench基准，以半秒粒度标注，设有情境和视觉通道两个轨道，均采用对比阶梯设计（仅改变单一决定性线索），并评估了十个开源和闭源VLM。

Result: 守卫能可靠识别包含危险的视频，但常错过具体危险时刻（尤其情境性危险）；误导性场景文本降低所有模型性能，脆弱模型漏掉多达1/3危险，鲁棒模型过度干预安全内容；匹配对照表明表面鲁棒性源于无差别警报。

Conclusion: 当前VLM尚不足以胜任细粒度的安全守卫任务，需提升其对情境和误导性文本的推理能力。

中文摘要：视觉语言模型（VLM）现被提议作为家庭和工厂中具身智能体的运行时安全守卫。一个可部署的守卫必须能够捕捉真正不安全的场景，同时避免对常规但表面上令人警觉的活动进行不必要的干预，而二元安全基准模糊了这一区别。我们引入了EgoSafetyBench，一个包含1200个机器人视角场景、以半秒粒度标注的自我中心视频基准，用于评估VLM作为流式守卫在两个轨道上的表现。情境轨道（800个场景）涵盖四类情况，从常规和安全但可疑的场景到明显和情境性危险。视觉通道轨道（400个场景）针对场景内文本——场景中可见的标志、贴纸或标签——这些文本可能曲解物理情境，每个误导性标志配对一个真实版本，以测试守卫是否标记文本为误导以及文本是否影响其物理安全判断。两个轨道均使用对比阶梯：近乎相同的场景仅在一个可见的决定性线索上有所不同，因此正确的判断必须依赖于该线索而非整体场景类型。我们评估了十个开源和闭源VLM。我们发现，虽然守卫能可靠地识别包含危险的视频，但它们常常错过特定的危险时刻，尤其是情境性危险。此外，误导性的场景内文本会降低所有测试守卫的表现：脆弱模型错过多达三分之一的危险，而鲁棒模型对安全内容过度干预。匹配对照揭示，表面上的安全鲁棒性往往反映的是无差别的警报而非真正的物理推理。

Original abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) are now proposed as runtime safety guards for embodied agents in homes and factories. A deployable guard must catch genuinely unsafe situations while avoiding unnecessary intervention on routine but superficially alarming activity, a distinction that binary safety benchmarks obscure. We introduce EgoSafetyBench, an egocentric video benchmark of 1,200 robot-view scenarios annotated at half-second granularity, to evaluate VLMs as streaming guards across two tracks. The situational track (800 scenarios) spans four families, from routine and safe-but-suspicious scenes to obvious and contextual hazards. The visual-channel track (400 scenarios) targets in-scene text-a sign, sticker, or label visible in the scene-that can misrepresent the physical situation, pairing each misleading sign with a truthful version to test both whether a guard flags the text as misleading and whether the text corrupts its physical-safety judgment. Both tracks use contrastive ladders: near-identical scenarios differing only in a single visible deciding cue, so a correct call must hinge on that cue rather than the overall scene type. We evaluate ten open- and closed-source VLMs. We find that while guards reliably recognize videos containing hazards, they often miss specific hazardous moments, particularly contextual hazards. Furthermore, misleading in-scene signs degrade all tested guards: vulnerable models miss up to a third of hazards, while robust models over-intervene on safe content. Matched controls reveal that apparent safety robustness often reflects indiscriminate alarming rather than true physical reasoning.

</details>

### [92] [Active Sensing for RIS-Aided Tracking and Power Control: A Hybrid Neuroevolution and Supervised Learning Approach](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00056v2)
*George Stamatelis,Hui Chen,Henk Henk Wymeersch,George C. Alexandropoulos*

Main category: cs.IT

Selection reason: 双agent框架与混合训练方法，可迁移到离散动作空间agent。

TL;DR: 提出一种双智能体深度学习框架，联合优化RIS相位和用户发射功率，实现高精度鲁棒跟踪，性能优于多种基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 功率受限移动用户的定位导频传输消耗大量能量，需要低开销的动态功率控制，且RIS相位和功率控制联合优化问题具有离散性和分散性。

Method: 提出双智能体（DA）深度学习框架，采用神经进化与监督学习混合训练，克服RIS离散相位不可微和单比特反馈信息瓶颈；支持单/多天线BS，多天线时增加输出分支选数字合并器。

Result: 数值仿真表明，该方案在多种运动模型下跟踪精度和鲁棒性优于EKF、粒子滤波及ML跟踪器；静态定位中优于传统指纹、深度强化学习和反向传播估计。

Conclusion: 提出的DA主动感知框架实现了高精度鲁棒跟踪，能量高效，适用于功率受限移动用户定位与跟踪。

中文摘要：本文研究了在可重构智能表面（RIS）辅助下对功率受限移动用户的能量高效跟踪问题。由于定位导频传输占用了功率受限设备的大部分能量预算，我们引入了一条从基站（BS）到用户的低开销反馈链路，以实现动态上行功率控制。为了应对这一主动感知问题的离散性和分散性，我们提出了一种新颖的双智能体（DA）深度学习框架，该框架联合优化离散的RIS相位配置和用户设备的发射功率。具体而言，我们的方法采用了一种结合神经进化范式和监督学习的混合训练方法，有效克服了RIS单元元件离散相位响应的不可微性以及用于导频功率控制的单比特反馈消息的严格信息瓶颈。所提出的DA主动感知框架可应用于单天线和多天线基站，后者仅需对一个神经网络的结构进行微小修改：在多天线情况下增加一个具有适当结构的输出分支，以从有限集合中选择有效的数字合并器。大量的数值仿真表明，所提出的方案在多种目标运动模型下实现了高精度和鲁棒的跟踪，性能优于扩展卡尔曼滤波器、粒子滤波器以及基于机器学习的跟踪器。此外，在静态定位中，它显著优于传统的指纹定位方案、深度强化学习基线和标准的反向传播估计器。

Original abstract: This paper studies energy efficient tracking of power-limited mobile users with the assistance of a Reconfigurable Intelligent Surface (RIS). Since localization pilot transmissions dominate the energy budget of power-constrained devices, we introduce a low-overhead feedback link from the Base Station (BS) to the user to enable dynamic uplink power control. To navigate the discrete and decentralized nature of this active sensing problem, we propose a novel Dual-Agent (DA) deep learning framework that jointly optimizes the discrete RIS phase profiles and the UE's transmit power in real time. Specifically, our approach employs a hybrid training methodology integrating the neuroevolution paradigm with supervised learning, effectively overcoming the non-differentiability of discrete phase responses from the RIS unit elements and the strict information bottleneck of single-bit feedback messages for pilot power control. The proposed DA active sensing framework can be applied with both single- and multi-antenna BSs, the latter with only minor modifications in the structure of one NN: an additional output branch with appropriate structure is included for the latter case to select a valid digital combiner from a finite set. Extensive numerical simulations demonstrate that the proposed scheme achieves highly accurate and robust tracking across diverse target motion models, outperforming extended Kalman and particle filters, as well as, machine learning-based trackers. Furthermore, in static localization, it is shown to significantly outperform traditional fingerprinting schemes, deep reinforcement learning baselines, and standard backpropagation-based estimators.

### [93] [PPT-Eval: A Benchmark for Computer-Use Agents on PowerPoint Tasks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31154v1)
*Apurva Gandhi,Vishwas Suryanarayanan,Raja Hasnain Anwar,Firoz Shaik,Shubhang Desai,Thong Q. Nguyen,Muhammad Taqi Raza,Vishal Chowdhary,Graham Neubig*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: PPT-Eval benchmark评测计算机使用agent，直接相关agent评测。

TL;DR: 提出PPT-Eval基准和基于评分标准的评估框架，用于多模态幻灯片编辑任务，实验显示现有代理表现不佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 幻灯片编辑是真实世界多模态任务，现有二元成功指标无法捕捉代理的部分进展，需要更细致的评估。

Method: 设计包含120个任务（12个文件）的PPT-Eval基准，并构建基于评分标准的评估框架，对中间步骤给分、惩罚不必要更改和美学问题，提供自然语言反馈。

Result: 评估框架与人类判断高度相关（Kendall's τ-b=0.77），强模型Claude-4.5-Opus仅45%成功率和57%平均部分分数。

Conclusion: 现有前沿代理在PowerPoint任务上仍表现不佳，需要更强大的代理来应对复杂多模态场景。

中文摘要：创建和编辑幻灯片是一种丰富的多模态活动，在专业和教育环境中无处不在，使其成为现实世界计算机使用代理的理想测试平台。Microsoft PowerPoint 是用于演示文稿创建的最广泛采用且功能丰富的环境之一。我们提出了 PPT-Eval，这是一个包含 12 个文件中 120 个 PowerPoint 任务的基准测试，涵盖了内容创建和演示编辑场景，并按难度组织。该领域的一个核心挑战是评估：任务复杂、多模态，并且通常允许许多有效的解决方案。此外，当今的代理通常只取得部分进展，二元的成功指标无法捕捉到这一点。为了解决这个问题，我们设计了一个稳健的评估框架，以帮助创建针对 PowerPoint 任务的特定任务评分标准，汲取并建立在过去基于评分标准的评估工作之上。这些评分标准为中间步骤给予部分分数，惩罚不必要的更改和糟糕的美观性，并提供自然语言反馈。这种细致的方法被证明非常有效，与人类判断的 Kendall's τ-b 相关系数达到 0.77。我们发现现有前沿代理在解决 PowerPoint 任务方面仍然困难重重，像 Claude-4.5-Opus 这样的强模型仅达到 45% 的成功率和平均 57% 的部分分数。基准测试位于：https://microsoft.github.io/ppteval。

Original abstract: Creating and editing slides is a rich, multimodal activity that is ubiquitous in professional and educational settings, making it an ideal testbed for real-world computer-use agents. Microsoft PowerPoint is among the most widely adopted and feature-rich environments for presentation creation. We introduce PPT-Eval, a benchmark of 120 PowerPoint tasks across 12 files that cover both content creation and presentation editing scenarios, organized by difficulty. A central challenge in this domain is evaluation: tasks are complex, multimodal, and often admit many valid solutions. Moreover, today's agents frequently make only partial progress, which binary success metrics fail to capture. To address this, we design a robust evaluation framework to help create task-specific rubrics for PowerPoint tasks, taking inspiration from and building on past works for rubric-based evaluation. These rubrics award partial credit for intermediate steps, penalize unnecessary changes and poor aesthetics, and provide natural language feedback. This nuanced approach proves highly effective, achieving a Kendall's τ-b correlation of 0.77 with human judgments. We find that existing frontier agents still struggle with solving PowerPoint tasks, with strong models like Claude-4.5-Opus achieving only a 45% success rate and an average partial score of 57%. The benchmark is located at: https://microsoft.github.io/ppteval.

### [94] [Calibrating the Evaluator: Does Probability Calibration Mitigate Preference Coupling in LLM Agent Feedback Loops?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31371v1)
*Zewen Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: LLM评估器校准减轻偏好耦合，直接提升agent反馈质量

TL;DR: 首次研究评估者概率校准可缓解LLM智能体学习中的偏好耦合，降幅达20-49%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作仅测量了评估者偏好耦合现象，但未探索校准技术能否缓解该问题。

Method: 在N=5的受试者内实验中，对比标准二元TTRL与置信度校准TTRL（概率加权更新），使用DeepSeek-V4-Pro和GLM5.2，并通过对称LR对照排除更新不对称性影响。

Result: 校准使耦合系数gamma降低20-49%，Jensen-Shannon散度降低45-67%。

Conclusion: 评估者概率校准是减轻LLM-as-judge部署中偏好耦合的轻量级有效方法，已发布校准协议。

中文摘要：当大型语言模型（LLM）智能体通过评估者反馈调整其行为时，系统的评估者偏差会传播到智能体学习的策略分布中——这一现象被称为评估者偏好耦合。先前的工作已经记录了这种耦合并建立了一个诊断框架（EPC）来测量它，但尚未研究校准技术是否能够减轻这种影响。我们提出了第一项关于评估者校准作为缓解方法的研究：将概率校准应用于评估者的成对判断，以减少虚假偏好传播。在一个受试者内实验（N=5）中，比较标准的二元TTRL（胜/负）与置信度校准的TTRL（概率加权更新），使用DeepSeek-V4-Pro作为执行器，GLM5.2作为评估者，我们发现校准将耦合系数gamma降低了20-49%，将Jensen-Shannon散度降低了45-67%。一个对称LR对照确认了这种效果并非由于更新不对称性的减少。我们发布了校准后的TTRL协议，并推荐其作为LLM作为评判部署流水线的轻量级缓解措施。

Original abstract: When large language model (LLM) agents adapt their behavior through evaluator feedback, systematic evaluator biases propagate into the agent's learned strategy distribution - a phenomenon termed evaluator preference coupling. Prior work has documented this coupling and established a diagnostic framework (EPC) to measure it, but has not investigated whether calibration techniques can mitigate the effect. We present the first study of evaluator calibration as mitigation: applying probability calibration to the evaluator's pairwise judgments to reduce spurious preference propagation. In a controlled within-subjects experiment (N=5) comparing standard binary TTRL (win/loss) with confidence-calibrated TTRL (probability-weighted updates) using DeepSeek-V4-Pro as executor and GLM5.2 as evaluator, we find that calibration reduces the coupling coefficient gamma by 20-49% and Jensen-Shannon divergence by 45-67%. A symmetric-LR control confirms the effect is not due to reduced update asymmetry. We release the calibrated TTRL protocol and recommend it as a lightweight mitigation for LLM-as-judge deployment pipelines.

</details>


### [95] [Evil Spectra: How Optimisers can Amplify or Suppress Emergent Misalignment](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31591v1)
*Jason R. Brown,Patrick Leask,Lev McKinney*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 优化器对LLM突现失调影响，可启发agent训练稳定性。

TL;DR: 优化器选择是导致大型语言模型在微调后出现广泛错位（EM）的关键因素，而谱正则化可以有效缓解该问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有研究注意到训练选择对EM严重性高度敏感，但缺乏对这种敏感性的系统描述。

Method: 通过对多个模型、优化器、数据集和批次大小进行扫描，分析损失-对齐关系，并引入谱正则化损失项。

Result: 优化器选择产生7倍错位率差异，模型大小影响可忽略；Muon优化器通过均匀奇异值分布隐式正则化，谱正则化可显著恢复Adam和Lion的对齐性。

Conclusion: 优化器选择是EM严重性的关键因素，谱正则化能有效缓解EM-prone优化器的影响。

中文摘要：新兴的错位（EM）是最近在大型语言模型中发现的一种现象，其中对狭窄的错位任务（例如编写不安全的代码）进行微调会导致在无关提示上出现广泛的错位行为。先前的工作已经注意到EM的严重性对训练选择高度敏感；然而，我们仍然缺乏对这种敏感性的系统描述。我们对多个Qwen3模型、优化器、数据集和批次大小进行了扫描，发现优化器的选择影响最大，导致错位率产生7倍的差异。令人惊讶的是，在Qwen3家族中，模型大小的影响可以忽略不计。另外对来自三个家族的12个模型使用Adam进行的扫描证实，对于该优化器，模型规模（1B-235B）和家族的影响可以忽略不计。分析Qwen3-8B上的损失-对齐关系，我们发现最终训练日志损失是对齐的强预测因子，并且按优化器分层几乎捕获了所有剩余方差。训练动态表明，每个优化器在损失-对齐空间中遵循不同的轨迹，并且在大量训练后，优化器作为对齐预测因子的重要性超过了训练损失。Muon，一种保持对齐效果最好的自适应优化器，隐式地正则化LoRA适配器奇异值的更均匀分布。我们通过添加一个额外的损失项来评估这一见解，该损失项激励更平坦的奇异值谱，并发现这显著恢复了对齐对于更容易产生EM的自适应优化器（Adam和Lion），而对训练损失的影响可以忽略不计。这些结果表明优化器选择是EM严重性的关键因素，但也表明谱正则化可以显著缓解易产生EM优化器的影响。

Original abstract: Emergent misalignment (EM) is a recently discovered phenomenon in LLMs where fine-tuning on a narrow misaligned task, such as writing insecure code, leads to broadly misaligned behaviour on unrelated prompts. Previous work has noted that the severity of EM is highly sensitive to training choices; however, we still lack a systematic characterisation of this sensitivity. We perform a sweep over several Qwen3 models, optimisers, datasets, and batch sizes, and find that the choice of optimiser has the largest effect, producing a 7x spread in misalignment rate. Surprisingly, model size has a negligible effect within the Qwen3 family. An additional sweep over 12 models from three families using Adam confirms that model scale (1B-235B) and family have negligible effects for that optimiser. Analysing the loss-alignment relationship on Qwen3-8B, we find that final log training loss is a strong predictor of alignment, and that stratifying by optimiser captures nearly all the residual variance. Training dynamics reveal that each optimiser follows a different trajectory through loss-alignment space, and that after significant training, the optimiser becomes more important than training loss as a predictor of alignment. Muon, the adaptive optimiser that preserves alignment the best, implicitly regularises for a more uniform distribution of singular values of the LoRA adapter. We evaluate this insight by training with an additional loss term that incentivises a flatter singular value spectrum, and find that this substantially recovers alignment for the more EM-prone adaptive optimisers (Adam and Lion), with negligible cost to training loss. These results identify optimiser choice as a key factor in EM severity, but show that spectral regularisation can substantially mitigate the effects of EM-prone optimisers.

### [96] [ECHO: Prune To Act, Trace To Learn With Selective Turn Memory In Agentic RL](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31650v3)
*Zijun Xie,Binbin Zheng,Enlei Gong,Jihua Liu,Yuyang You,Lingfeng Liu,Jiayao Tang,Guanqun Zhao,Aoqi Hu,Zeyu Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出选择性turn记忆框架用于agentic RL，解决长期agent的上下文管理和信用分配，对代码优化agent的记忆设计有启发。

TL;DR: ECHO通过选择性回合记忆和源索引回溯，解决了上下文压缩导致的可追溯性缺失问题，在Agentic RL中显著提升了性能和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有上下文管理方法在压缩历史时丢失了源信息，导致强化学习中信用分配不准确，策略与学习不匹配。

Method: ECHO将环境回合压缩为带源索引的记忆记录，选择有用记录重构策略上下文，并利用源索引将奖励信号路由到相应轨迹和记忆组件。

Result: 在BrowseComp-Plus上准确率43.4%，优于GRPO(28.9%)和SUPO(36.1%)，且使用更少回合；在多任务上提升零样本泛化。

Conclusion: ECHO有效实现了可追溯的上下文重建，提升了Agentic RL中的信用分配和性能。

中文摘要：长程语言代理必须在有限的上下文窗口下反复与工具交互、积累证据并做出决策。上下文管理方法通过删除、折叠或记忆编辑来简化过去的交互，从而使此类滚动执行变得可行。然而，当有用的历史被压缩为压缩状态时，重构的上下文可能不再揭示哪些早期观察支持成功的最终答案。这造成了有限上下文执行与基于结果的强化学习之间的不匹配：策略基于重构的上下文行动，而学习者缺乏源级别的来源信息来为重要的证据分配信用。我们提出了ECHO，一种用于代理强化学习中可追溯上下文重建的选择性回合记忆框架。ECHO将每个完成的环境回合压缩为紧凑的源索引记忆记录，通过选择有用的记录来重构有限的策略上下文，并重用所选的源索引将正结果信用路由到最终的轨迹段、重用的证据回合、记忆发现和记忆选择动作。在BrowseComp-Plus上，ECHO达到了43.4%的留出准确率，优于GRPO的28.9%和滚动摘要基线SUPO的36.1%，同时使用的回合数和轨迹量少于SUPO。训练后的策略还在多目标问答、代码生成和深度信息检索基准测试中，在密集和MoE骨干上均提高了零样本泛化能力。

Original abstract: Long-horizon language agents must repeatedly interact with tools, accumulate evidence, and make decisions under bounded context windows. Context-management methods make such rollouts feasible by simplifying past interactions through deletion, folding, or memory editing. However, when useful history is collapsed into compressed states, the reconstructed context may no longer reveal which earlier observations support a successful final answer. This creates a mismatch between bounded-context acting and outcome-based reinforcement learning: the policy acts on reconstructed context, while the learner lacks source-level provenance for assigning credit to the evidence that mattered. We propose ECHO, a selective turn-memory framework for traceable context reconstruction in Agentic RL. ECHO compresses each completed environment turn into a compact source-indexed memory record, reconstructs bounded policy contexts by selecting useful records, and reuses the selected source indices to route positive outcome credit to the final trajectory segment, reused evidence turns, memory findings, and memory-selection actions. On BrowseComp-Plus, ECHO reaches 43.4% held-out accuracy, outperforming GRPO at 28.9% and the rolling-summary baseline SUPO at 36.1%, while using fewer turns and lower trajectory volume than SUPO. The trained policy also improves zero-shot generalization across multi-objective QA, code generation, and deep information-seeking benchmarks on both dense and MoE backbones.

### [97] [TRIAGE: Role-Typed Credit Assignment for Agentic Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.32017v2)
*Yuanda Xu,Zhengze Zhou,Hejian Sang,Xiaomin Li,Jiaxin Zhang,Xinchen Du,Sen Na,Zhipeng Wang,Alborz Geramifard*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 角色类型信用分配改进GRPO，对agent强化学习有直接可迁移的方法贡献

TL;DR: TRIAGE通过角色类型化的信用分配框架，在强化学习中区分动作的语义角色，纠正了标准GRPO的信用分配盲点，提升了成功率和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准GRPO使用最终验证器结果作为所有动作的统一优势，惩罚了失败轨迹中的有用探索，并强化了成功轨迹中的冗余或倒退动作，导致信用分配不完整。

Method: 提出TRIAGE框架，添加语义角色轴，由结构化裁判将片段分类为四种角色（决定性进展、有用探索、无进展基础设施、倒退），并用固定规则映射为片段级过程奖励，同时保留验证器结果作为优化方向。

Result: 在ALFWorld、Search-QA和WebShop上，TRIAGE提升了GRPO的成功率，优于标量过程奖励和值基线；消融表明角色类型化是增益来源，尤其是检测倒退贡献最大，同时减少了10.4%和14.8%的环境交互次数。

Conclusion: 角色类型化的信用分配能有效修正仅结果信用的盲点，降低优势估计误差，提高策略梯度的效率，并在多个基准上取得更好性能。

中文摘要：智能体强化学习需要为面向环境的动作（如搜索、点击、编辑、导航命令和物体交互）分配信用。标准GRPO使用最终的验证器结果作为所有动作令牌的统一优势。这种结果信号是有用的，但在结构上不完整：它惩罚了失败轨迹中的有用探索，并在成功轨迹中强化了冗余或倒退的动作。我们提出TRIAGE，一个角色类型化的信用分配框架，为结果信用添加了一个语义角色轴。一个结构化的裁判将每个片段分类为决定性进展、有用探索、无进展基础设施或倒退，并且一个固定的角色条件规则将这些标签映射到有界的片段级过程奖励。这保持了验证器结果作为优化方向的来源，同时纠正了仅结果信用中的两个主要盲点。我们进一步表明，角色条件信用是从角色标签中可表达的最优片段级校正——每片段优势残差到角色变量的投影——因此只要裁判可靠，固定的角色常数就会减少优势估计误差，并且我们将此与较低方差策略梯度联系起来。在ALFWorld、Search-QA和WebShop上，TRIAGE相对于GRPO提高了两种策略模型的成功率，并且优于标量裁判导出的过程奖励和结果监督的共享骨干价值基线。消融实验表明，增益来自角色类型化而非仅仅增加密集奖励：可靠检测成功轨迹内部的倒退是主要贡献者，而探索信用提供了持续的次要增益；在完成的ALFWorld和WebShop轨迹上，TRIAGE相对于GRPO还额外减少了10.4%和14.8%的环境交互次数。

Original abstract: Agentic reinforcement learning requires assigning credit to environment-facing actions such as searches, clicks, edits, navigation commands, and object interactions. Standard GRPO uses the final verifier outcome as a uniform advantage over all action tokens. This outcome signal is useful but structurally incomplete: it punishes useful exploration in failed rollouts and reinforces redundant or regressive actions in successful rollouts. We propose TRIAGE, a role-typed credit assignment framework that adds a semantic role axis to outcome credit. A structured judge classifies each segment as decisive progress, useful exploration, no-progress infrastructure, or regression, and a fixed role-conditioned rule maps these labels to bounded segment-level process rewards. This keeps verifier outcomes as the source of optimization direction while correcting the two main blind spots of outcome-only credit. We further show that role-conditioned credit is the optimal segment-level correction expressible from role labels alone -- a projection of the per-segment advantage residual onto the role variable -- so that the fixed role constants reduce advantage estimation error whenever the judge is reliable, and we connect this to lower-variance policy gradients. Across ALFWorld, Search-QA, and WebShop, TRIAGE improves success rates over GRPO for two policy models and outperforms both a scalar judge-derived process reward and an outcome-supervised shared-backbone value baseline. Ablations show that the gain comes from role typing rather than merely adding dense rewards: reliable detection of regression inside successful trajectories is the dominant contributor, while exploration credit provides a consistent secondary gain; on completed ALFWorld and WebShop rollouts, TRIAGE also reduces environment-facing turns by an additional $10.4\%$ and $14.8\%$ relative to GRPO.

</details>


### [98] [AdaJEPA: An Adaptive Latent World Model](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.32026v1)
*Ying Wang,Oumayma Bounou,Yann LeCun,Mengye Ren*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 自适应隐世界模型用于规划，可迁移至agent世界模型自适应方法

TL;DR: AdaJEPA在测试时通过闭环自监督更新潜在世界模型，以应对分布偏移，仅需少量梯度步骤即可显著提升规划成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测试时分布偏移导致潜在世界模型预测不准确，使规划失败，而现有方法通常冻结模型无法适应。

Method: AdaJEPA在MPC闭环中，每次执行动作后利用观测到的状态转换作为自监督信号，更新世界模型，并用更新后的模型重新规划。

Result: 在多种目标达成任务中，每次MPC重新规划仅需一个梯度步骤，即可显著提高规划成功率。

Conclusion: AdaJEPA通过测试时自适应有效应对分布偏移，提升规划鲁棒性，且效率高。

中文摘要：潜在世界模型通过在紧凑的潜在空间中预测未来状态，实现了从高维观测中进行规划。然而，这些模型在测试时通常保持冻结状态：当它们的预测变得不准确时，规划可能会失败，尤其是在测试时的分布偏移下。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了AdaJEPA，一种自适应潜在世界模型，它在模型预测控制的闭环内执行测试时适应。训练后，AdaJEPA规划并执行第一个动作块，将观察到的下一状态转换作为自监督适应信号，并用更新后的模型重新规划。这种闭环更新持续重新校准世界模型，无需额外的专家演示。在一系列目标达成任务中，AdaJEPA仅需每次MPC重新规划步骤的一个梯度步骤就能显著提高规划成功率。

Original abstract: Latent world models enable planning from high-dimensional observations by predicting future states in a compact latent space. However, these models are typically kept frozen at test time: when their predictions become inaccurate, planning can fail, especially under test-time distribution shift. To address this, we propose AdaJEPA, an adaptive latent world model that performs test-time adaptation within the closed loop of model predictive control (MPC). After training, AdaJEPA plans and executes the first action chunk, uses the observed next-state transition as a self-supervised adaptation signal, and replans with the updated model. This closed-loop update continuously recalibrates the world model without additional expert demonstrations. Across a range of goal-reaching tasks, AdaJEPA substantially improves planning success with as few as one gradient step per MPC replanning step.

### [99] [QVal: Cheaply Evaluating Dense Supervision Signals for Long-Horizon LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.32034v1)
*Sergio Hernández-Gutiérrez,Matteo Merler,Ilze Amanda Auzina,Joschka Strüber,Ameya Prabhu,Matthias Bethge*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 直接相关：长程LLM agent密集监督信号的训练无关评估方法，对agent训练信号设计有指导价值

TL;DR: QVal是一个无需训练的直接评估密集监督信号质量的测试平台，通过Q值对齐度量方法评分，发现简单提示基线优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有密集监督方法评估依赖于下游训练性能，成本高昂且混杂因素多，不同方法论家族难以公平比较，缺乏共同基准。

Method: 提出QVal测试平台，通过计算方法评分与参考策略Q值的对齐程度（Q值对齐）来直接评估密集监督信号，无需训练。

Result: 在21种方法和6个模型上，简单提示基线始终优于文献中最近的密集监督方法，且性能按方法论家族强烈聚类。

Conclusion: QVal提供了可扩展的基准，能在训练前有效评估密集监督方法，揭示了简单方法的优势，有助于未来方法迭代。

中文摘要：LLM智能体越来越需要长时间跨度的行动，其中单个轨迹可能包含数百或数千个动作。在这些场景中，仅基于结果的奖励提供的指导过于稀疏，无法告知模型中间动作的好坏。密集监督方法旨在通过评分中间步骤来解决这一问题，评分方式包括内在置信度、自蒸馏以及嵌入相似度等。然而，通常的评估方式是通过测量整合了这些方法的训练流程的下游性能。这种做法成本高昂，将监督质量与训练工程混杂因素相混淆，并且使得需要不同训练设置的不同方法论家族无法进行比较。因此，密集监督方法很少在共同基准上进行评估。我们引入了QVal，一个无需训练的直接评估密集监督信号的测试平台。给定一个状态-动作对，QVal衡量方法的评分与Q值对齐的程度：即它是否根据强参考策略的Q值对动作进行排序。这使我们能够在任何训练运行之前比较信号，并将信号质量与其他工程选择分开。我们实例化了QVal-v1.0，在四个不同环境和七个方法论家族中对21种密集监督方法进行了基准测试，涉及超过1200次评估实验，涵盖六个开放权重模型主干。我们发现，简单的提示基线始终优于文献中最近的密集监督方法，并且性能按家族强烈聚类。这些发现跨模型大小、环境和观察模态均成立。QVal设计为易于扩展到新环境和方法，使研究人员能够在任何训练运行之前迭代密集监督方法。

Original abstract: LLM agents increasingly act over long horizons, where a single trajectory can contain hundreds or thousands of actions. In these settings, outcome-only rewards provide too sparse guidance, failing to inform the model about the goodness of intermediate actions. Dense supervision methods aim to solve this problem by scoring intermediate steps, from intrinsic confidence to self-distillation and embedding similarities. However, it is common practice to evaluate them by measuring the downstream performance of a training pipeline that integrates them. This is expensive, conflates supervision quality with training engineering confounders, and renders different methodological families requiring distinct training setups incomparable. As a result, dense supervision methods are rarely benchmarked on common ground. We introduce QVal, a training-free testbed for directly evaluating dense supervision signals. Given a state-action pair, QVal measures how well a method's score is Q-aligned: whether it orders actions according to the Q-values of a strong reference-policy. This lets us compare signals before any training run and separate signal quality from other engineering choices. We instantiate QVal as QVal-v1.0, benchmarking 21 dense supervision methods across four diverse environments and seven methodological families, with over 1.2K evaluation experiments across six open-weight model backbones. We find that simple prompting baselines consistently outperform recent dense supervision methods from the literature, and that performance clusters strongly by family. These findings hold across model sizes, environments, and observation modalities. QVal is designed to be easily extensible to new environments and methods, enabling researchers to iterate on dense supervision methods before any training run.

</details>
